    # **Beyond the Lab: Performance Engineering for Production AI Systems**


    The conversation around AI has shifted from whether to adopt the technology to
    how to make it economically viable at production scale. In previous articles,
    I’ve covered the strategic [**playbooks for AI adoption**](https://substack.com/redirect/987344f4-4446-4752-872c-b9bc0b1b91c2?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)
    and [**evaluation frameworks**](https://substack.com/redirect/78ca8254-ab01-4175-9a07-bc04caff5b3b?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)
    that define success. However, a critical gap persists between successful pilots
    and sustainable production systems—a gap that costs organizations millions in
    wasted infrastructure and missed opportunities. The companies that will lead the
    next wave of innovation understand that AI performance engineering isn''t about
    maximizing raw model capability, but about optimizing the entire system for business
    value. The following eight strategies represent hard-won lessons from teams that
    have moved beyond the lab to build AI systems that scale profitably.


    #### **1. Understand the Non-Linear Economics of AI Systems**


    Unlike traditional software where costs scale predictably with users, generative
    AI systems face exponential cost growth through hidden multipliers like context
    expansion, retry mechanisms, and cascading tool calls—similar to how distributed
    systems introduced new failure modes that monolithic architectures never encountered.
    A simple chatbot query that costs pennies in development can balloon to dollars
    in production when factoring in retrieval-augmented generation lookups, multi-turn
    conversation history, and safety filtering passes, creating budget surprises that
    derail AI initiatives.


    [![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!oLoC!,w_412,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F4de8e51c-3c98-4ae2-a16b-33ee6e7532fe_1156x910.jpeg)](https://substack.com/redirect/53589884-28c9-49f6-9b77-dec1a416c5bb?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)


    Organizations that internalize this reality early avoid the common pattern of
    successful pilots that stall at production scale, maintaining momentum while competitors
    hit cost walls that force feature rollbacks. By building cost awareness into architectural
    decisions from day one, teams significantly reduce time-to-market compared to
    those who attempt late-stage optimization sprints. _Task your lead engineer to
    trace a complex user query through your entire AI pipeline, documenting every
    API call, token multiplication point, and retry loop to reveal the true cost amplification
    factor—the results typically shock even experienced teams._


    #### **2. Implement Intelligent Model Routing for Cost Efficiency**


    Defaulting to your most powerful model for every request wastes resources on simple
    tasks that smaller models handle equally well, much like using a Formula One engine
    for neighborhood errands. A tiered routing system analyzes incoming requests and
    directs them to appropriately-sized models—lightweight 7B parameter models for
    FAQs and data extraction, mid-tier 13-30B models for moderate reasoning, and premium
    models only for complex creative or analytical tasks. This cascade architecture
    functions as a computational [CDN](https://substack.com/redirect/aaae4209-e119-4536-a8ec-58c0569b31c9?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8),
    where the majority of requests never need expensive inference, dramatically improving
    both cost and latency profiles.


    [![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!-5FQ!,w_532,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F28d06e18-7008-403b-8db8-b8809b1c3e95_1559x609.jpeg)](https://substack.com/redirect/2ba61f9e-dc4b-40f2-a2a6-57147be107b0?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)


    Teams implementing model cascades report substantial reductions in inference costs
    while actually improving average response times, as queue contention on expensive
    resources drops dramatically. This transforms previously uneconomical use cases
    into viable products, expanding the market for AI features while improving system
    reliability through better resource isolation. _Analyze your last 1,000 API calls
    to categorize them by complexity, then pilot routing your highest-volume simple
    queries to an open-source 7B parameter model, measuring both cost savings and
    quality retention._


    #### **3. Optimize Memory Bandwidth, Not Just Compute**


    Modern AI systems hit memory bandwidth limits long before exhausting computational
    capacity, similar to how Netflix discovered [content delivery performance](https://substack.com/redirect/fbd05e03-5f1c-4fa7-a959-6977d95b1987?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)
    mattered more than raw server processing power. The primary bottleneck for large
    language models isn''t computation, but data movement. This memory-bound reality
    creates a fundamental challenge that traditional, compute-focused scaling solutions
    are ineffective against. This memory wall becomes particularly acute during inference
    when models must sequentially generate tokens, with each step requiring access
    to cached attention states that grow linearly with context length.


    [![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!96IU!,w_510,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F3f3270ad-7168-4797-8347-73fe7bcfd7f2_1653x500.jpeg)](https://substack.com/redirect/4c73edcc-a78f-42da-84c4-86c78688ffb8?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)


    Teams that recognize this architectural reality avoid costly over-provisioning
    of GPUs while achieving significantly better hardware utilization through memory-aware
    optimizations. This shift in perspective transforms capacity planning from guesswork
    to engineering, enabling accurate predictions of real-world performance limits.
    _Instrument your highest-traffic AI endpoint to measure memory bandwidth utilization
    versus compute utilization during peak periods, then share these metrics with
    your infrastructure team to realign resource allocation strategies._


    #### **4. Deploy Modern Inference Stacks with Built-in Optimizations**


    Modern AI inference platforms deliver the same performance leap your organization
    experienced moving from basic web servers to enterprise application servers. These
    platforms come with built-in optimizations that dramatically boost your GPU efficiency—similar
    to how a load balancer prevents one slow request from choking your entire system.
    Instead of your team spending months building custom performance optimizations
    like continuous batching, paged attention, and efficient KV-caching, frameworks
    like the open-source [**vLLM**](https://substack.com/redirect/4a120fc2-eab9-4ef1-b0d4-a7f80208301b?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)
    project deliver substantially better throughput immediately.


    [![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!dVxG!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2Fb94a9e95-3739-4289-89d8-6f35c4e1c558_1820x575.jpeg)](https://substack.com/redirect/d2b737f8-3ff1-4505-bbc3-e5c39c84d946?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)


    The business impact is immediate and measurable. Organizations adopting these
    platforms see response times improve significantly, infrastructure costs drop
    substantially, and engineering teams shift from fighting performance issues to
    building features that matter. This infrastructure foundation accelerates your
    AI experimentation cycle—a critical competitive advantage when AI capabilities
    are evolving rapidly. _Direct your platform team to benchmark your current inference
    setup against a modern open-source serving framework, measuring tokens per second
    and latency—the results will provide clear justification for migration._


    #### **5. Compress Models Systematically Through Quantization**


    Quantization reduces model precision from 32-bit floating point to 8-bit integers
    or even 4-bit representations, achieving significant size reduction while maintaining
    most of the original accuracy—comparable to how video compression preserves visual
    quality while dramatically reducing bandwidth requirements. Smaller models mean
    larger batch sizes fit in the same GPU memory, directly translating to higher
    throughput and lower latency, while also reducing cold start times for serverless
    deployments. Combined with structured pruning that removes redundant parameters,
    these techniques turn memory constraints from barriers into optimization opportunities.


    [![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!0dbX!,w_498,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F8ed7e84a-ff4c-4440-baa3-de8a5c295b25_1180x424.jpeg)](https://substack.com/redirect/152f1930-e173-4537-b4e0-6220d7f090b4?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)


    Teams implementing systematic compression strategies report substantial improvements
    in inference speed and reductions in infrastructure costs, making previously impossible
    applications suddenly feasible. **The business impact extends beyond cost savings
    to enable new product categories like on-device AI and edge deployment, opening
    markets that cloud-only solutions cannot address**. _Apply INT8 quantization to
    your most resource-intensive model in a development environment, A/B testing the
    compressed version against the original to establish concrete metrics for accuracy
    versus efficiency trade-offs._


    #### **6. Establish Granular FinOps Discipline from Day One**


    When an AI feature''s monthly bill unexpectedly triples, who is accountable? This
    isn''t just a budget issue; it''s a symptom of a new kind of architectural complexity.
    Much like the move to microservices obscured system behavior until [distributed
    tracing](https://substack.com/redirect/8cd9ecdf-c6e6-4433-b197-5bcc593f6ee6?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)
    made it visible, AI''s cascading costs remain hidden from standard monitoring.
    A robust [**FinOps**](https://substack.com/redirect/4dfb6145-b5a4-4a63-9f50-6981bf6a188c?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)
    practice acts as that essential tracing layer for expenses, preventing the frustrating
    cycle of blame by making costs transparent and attributable from the start.


    [![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!RCKg!,w_312,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F1377f973-a77d-4a44-bf24-a2b3daadac73_1390x919.jpeg)](https://substack.com/redirect/aff08988-3d72-4220-a99f-a0b5139f24ee?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)


    Companies with [**AI FinOps**](https://substack.com/redirect/0c35e487-bbe3-4564-bd4e-cdc0e5b7740f?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)
    practices report significant reductions in operational expenses while actually
    increasing feature velocity, as teams make informed trade-offs between cost and
    capability. This discipline prevents the budget crises that derail roadmaps and
    maintains trust between engineering and finance organizations. _Mandate that every
    AI endpoint must deploy with cost allocation tags identifying the model used,
    feature served, and responsible team, then configure automated alerts at 50% and
    80% of current monthly spend thresholds._


    #### **7. Build **AI-Native** Observability Before Problems Surface**


    Traditional infrastructure monitoring misses critical [AI performance indicators](https://substack.com/redirect/8209caf5-bebd-44ae-9e03-b3dd7a5374af?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)
    like [time-to-first-token](https://substack.com/redirect/5e058520-59a7-4b54-abae-bf7ce861319f?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8),
    [inter-token latency](https://substack.com/redirect/8209caf5-bebd-44ae-9e03-b3dd7a5374af?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8),
    and [KV-cache efficiency](https://substack.com/redirect/5e058520-59a7-4b54-abae-bf7ce861319f?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8),
    leaving teams blind to degradations that directly impact user experience—similar
    to how early web applications measured uptime but not page load speed. These AI-specific
    metrics provide early warning systems for performance issues, enabling proactive
    optimization rather than reactive firefighting when users complain about slow
    responses. Modern AI observability also tracks prompt injection attempts, hallucination
    rates, and context overflow events that traditional [APM](https://substack.com/redirect/411f93c3-f46b-4e37-b718-f36b2f1bdd9c?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)
    tools cannot detect.


    [![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!bVwu!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F0ba3d9ef-11e4-4ea8-afb9-b712c44c60d1_1889x373.jpeg)](https://substack.com/redirect/4414d476-6f50-4879-8f7b-dd21a4005abd?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)


    ([**click to enlarge**](https://substack.com/redirect/4414d476-6f50-4879-8f7b-dd21a4005abd?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8))


    With specialized AI monitoring, organizations fix issues faster, ensuring the
    consistent performance that keeps users engaged. This data-driven observability
    also replaces guesswork with precision in capacity planning and cost optimization.
    _Implement time-to-first-token monitoring on your primary user-facing endpoint
    this week, establishing baseline p50/p90/p99 measurements and configuring alerts
    at 2x your normal baseline to catch degradations before users notice._


    #### **8. Prepare for the Inference-Time Compute Revolution**


    The next wave of AI breakthroughs will come from [inference-time scaling](https://substack.com/redirect/3bd5bc56-3c40-434c-b1dc-dc0537a0bea7?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)—using
    more computation during generation to improve output quality—rather than simply
    training larger models, paralleling how search engines evolved through better
    ranking algorithms rather than bigger indexes. Techniques like speculative decoding
    (using small models to draft tokens for large models to verify in batches) and
    [test-time fine-tuning](https://substack.com/redirect/bef528a8-816e-45b5-90d5-0d878416c1c9?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)
    represent early examples of this paradigm shift, offering substantial quality
    improvements for complex reasoning tasks. Organizations that architect for flexible
    inference-time computation today will leverage these advances without infrastructure
    rewrites tomorrow.


    [![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!JkKE!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F76f9ac05-e349-4f7b-bc2d-4504705fd838_1902x1033.webp)](https://substack.com/redirect/512caa66-d83c-4d32-97c0-ad5418551994?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)


    From: [**Understanding Inference Scaling**](https://substack.com/redirect/294f72cf-a2ab-4a39-bd0f-301f2faec17d?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)


    Early adopters of inference-scaling techniques report notable improvements in
    output quality for complex reasoning tasks while maintaining production latency
    requirements. _Enable speculative decoding in your serving framework—often just
    a configuration flag—and measure the impact on time-to-first-token for interactive
    workloads to understand the immediate benefits while building experience with
    next-generation techniques_


    ---


    ## Ray Summit 2025


    These performance engineering principles will be front and center at [**Ray Summit
    2025**](https://substack.com/redirect/79a3ba64-53e2-48d6-b65b-83dea170c191?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8),
    taking place November 3-5 in San Francisco. This year''s summit features a **dedicated
    vLLM track** focused on building the kind of high-throughput, low-latency inference
    services that separate successful AI products from expensive experiments. The
    sessions will offer a deep dive into the practical implementation of many concepts
    outlined here, from intelligent model routing to memory-aware optimization. For
    teams serious about scaling AI systems economically, [**Ray Summit**](https://substack.com/redirect/79a3ba64-53e2-48d6-b65b-83dea170c191?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)
    is a rare opportunity to learn directly from practitioners who are solving these
    challenges in production.

    Google''s Web Guide feature is designed to better organize Search results into
    categories with additional context and insights to make it easier to find information
    and web pages. It uses a custom version of Gemini that uses a query fan-out technique
    to perform multiple related searches to identify the most relevant results. The
    feature is ideal for both open-ended searches and detailed queries with multiple
    sentences. Web Guide is available in Search Labs.


    # **Science & Futuristic Technology**


    [**Could Down syndrome be eliminated? Japanese scientists use CRISPR to target
    extra chromosome (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fqazinform.com%2Fnews%2Fcould-down-syndrome-be-eliminated-japanese-scientists-use-crispr-to-target-extra-chromosome-7fa7eb%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/0100019841315ac9-cede30ad-1388-400c-8fa8-b79ff72d1d27-000000/twVOWmh7Ahl3otw9j3G1duYt9leA4JjKX5oArReTCZs=415)


    Japanese researchers used CRISPR-Cas9 to remove an extra copy of chromosome 21
    from affected cells in a laboratory setting. The scientific milestone could reshape
    future approaches to treating Down syndrome. The CRISPR system targets the extra
    chromosome without affecting the normal pair. If the technique proves safe and
    reliable, it could be used in regenerative medicine.


    [**Robotic neck incision replaces heart valve with no chest opening in world first
    (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Finterestingengineering.com%2Fhealth%2Frobotic-heart-surgery-neck-valve-replacement%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/0100019841315ac9-cede30ad-1388-400c-8fa8-b79ff72d1d27-000000/K2963x8F2AN128ERvuHs5UCfSzB2mciBgSmGPsKgIPs=415)


    Doctors at the Cleveland Clinic replaced heart valves through a small neck incision
    using robotic assistance, avoiding the need to open the chest. Four patients have
    so far undergone the procedure, called transcervical robotic access for aortic
    valve replacement, and were discharged within days, with one even resuming gym
    workouts just a week after surgery. The procedure is being performed exclusively
    at the Cleveland Clinic for now, but the team hopes to standardize it for use
    at other highly specialized centers. It could redefine what is possible for heart
    surgery.

    interrupts flow state - the key is finding a method that works automatically without
    adding friction to workflows.

    and whether everyone should be taking them. While the development of these drugs
    is exciting, the current side-effect profile isn''t worth the risk for otherwise
    healthy patients.

    of power in tech has shifted away from engineers and towards tech companies. The
    biggest change in Goedecke''s engineering values is that he no longer wants to
    work in a pure maintenance role on existing legacy systems. Overall, his 2021
    and 2025 statements of values are fairly similar, despite changing a lot as an
    engineer over the years.

    # TLDR 2025-07-23


    # **Big Tech & Startups**


    [**Foldable iPhone''s Display Sizes Leaked (1 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.macrumors.com%2F2025%2F07%2F22%2Ffoldable-iphone-display-sizes-rumor%2F%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/0100019836e42ccf-b1fb245b-1cba-4770-9a8e-d7ffc2a13da2-000000/RKKuDnKMYHmBFkiZakP2b7LigV6okVHWidGX0LRpdfk=415)


    Apple will likely launch its foldable iPhone in the second half of 2026. The device
    will come with a 7.8-inch inner display and a 5.5-inch outer display. The Samsung
    Galaxy Z Fold 7 has an 8-inch inner screen and a 6.5-inch outer screen. Apple''s
    foldable iPhone will feature a ''crease-free'' inner display and have two rear
    cameras, one front camera, and a Touch ID power button instead of Face ID.


    [**OpenAI agreed to pay Oracle \$30B a year for data center services (2 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ftechcrunch.com%2F2025%2F07%2F22%2Fopenai-agreed-to-pay-oracle-30b-a-year-for-data-center-services%2F%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/0100019836e42ccf-b1fb245b-1cba-4770-9a8e-d7ffc2a13da2-000000/ing72MftmRjCfh8WhJtvuEjKZ83Rca1mEIZYsSk3An4=415)


    Oracle disclosed in an SEC filing last month that it had signed a cloud deal that
    would generate \$30 billion a year in revenue. The company that signed that deal
    has been revealed to be OpenAI. Oracle collectively sold \$24.5 billion worth
    of cloud services in its fiscal 2025 to all customers combined. OpenAI and Oracle
    still have to build the data center, which will be a costly endeavor.


    # **Science & Futuristic Technology**


    [**DeepMind''s Quest for Self-Improving Table Tennis Agents (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fspectrum.ieee.org%2Fdeepmind-table-tennis-robots%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/0100019836e42ccf-b1fb245b-1cba-4770-9a8e-d7ffc2a13da2-000000/wQBOiwvEDNfF2J0pQOubgAMUoyXLWzuAIzVKYNMmyAY=415)


    Google DeepMind recently used table tennis as a testbed for its technology, as
    the sport requires robots to master a confluence of difficult skills - it requires
    perception and demands exceptionally precise control. This makes table tennis
    an ideal domain for developing and evaluating robust learning algorithms that
    can handle real-time interaction, complex physics, high-level reasoning, and the
    need for adaptive strategies. This article looks at the study and the insights
    gained from it. One important lesson learned from the project is that VLMs can
    be leveraged for explainable robot policy search.


    [**Genetics Reimagined (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.thestatesman.com%2Fopinion%2Fgenetics-reimagined-1503460842.html%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/0100019836e42ccf-b1fb245b-1cba-4770-9a8e-d7ffc2a13da2-000000/X649gMrRy8MN-hKHO7cNCcV9_ntnXc1IUPjbrpALXkM=415)


    Scientists recently confirmed the healthy births of children through mitochondrial
    donation. The innovation opens new doors for reproductive choice. It offers at-risk
    families a viable path to parenthood without the lingering fear of passing on
    devastating inherited conditions. However, it also opens up the possibility of
    designer genetics that will be passed down to future generations. Those currently
    living with conditions will still face daily challenges, but for the next generation,
    the landscape has changed.


    # **Programming, Design & Data Science**


    [**any-agent (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fmozilla-ai%2Fany-agent%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/0100019836e42ccf-b1fb245b-1cba-4770-9a8e-d7ffc2a13da2-000000/0958_nk1so4iCcMcp0ATAdgQC8fvx29SVcdtXpr_kVQ=415)


    any-agent is a Python library that provides a single interface for evaluating
    different agent frameworks. It can be used to create and evaluate agents, implement
    and use custom callbacks, integrate Model Context Protocol tools, deploy agents
    with Agent-to-Agent communication, and more. Tutorials on how to get started are
    available.


    [**Vibecoding a high performance system (24 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fandrewkchan.dev%2Fposts%2Fsystems.html%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/0100019836e42ccf-b1fb245b-1cba-4770-9a8e-d7ffc2a13da2-000000/c90kfYdW77DHZE1kw_qsgMtuZ7ZV2S_HmkVco5Lgz_s=415)


    This developer recently used agentic coding to build a system to crawl a billion
    web pages in around 24 hours. Less than 4% of the code was written by hand. The
    post discusses how AI helped code the tool and where it fell short. AI was a huge
    boost during the development process. Some of the learnings from this project
    could also apply to building other high-performance systems.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**How Apple''s Internal Veto Against Open-Source AI Sparked a Talent Exodus to
    Meta (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2Fg2Z3M8/1/0100019836e42ccf-b1fb245b-1cba-4770-9a8e-d7ffc2a13da2-000000/GXtU5rOagf9ehHEY3aNuPwv52jpCEQkzTBX988RCR5Q=415)


    Apple had a plan to open-source its core AI models, but its leadership decided
    against it due to fears of exposing performance compromises made for on-device
    processing, a pivotal decision that has ignited a crisis of confidence within
    the company''s AI division. The move has directly triggered an exodus of top talent
    to rivals like Meta. Many engineers are frustrated with the internal conflict
    between Apple''s famous secrecy and the open culture of AI research. There are
    now serious doubts over the future of Apple Intelligence and the company''s ability
    to compete in the AI arms race.


    [**Reading QR codes without a computer! (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fqr.blinry.org%2F%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/0100019836e42ccf-b1fb245b-1cba-4770-9a8e-d7ffc2a13da2-000000/7SNmaQ0PUxsRfQnXUxQdqmwjO8VDyTb0XIazN9h-A7g=415)


    This article provides an interactive explanation of how QR codes work. It covers
    the anatomy of a QR code, mask patterns, encoding, reading, and decoding. Readers
    can enter their own custom data to generate a QR code to follow along with the
    article. The article gives readers all the information they need to decode simple
    QR codes by hand.

    # AI


    ## [And, action!](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/Cis?mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    [![Trump speaks at AI Summit in Washington DC ](https://cdn.sanity.io/images/bl383u0v/production/66173a7804d321696ec8fad8942f0806134c8a1d-5073x3383.jpg?w=668&q=70&auto=format)](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/Cis?mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    *Chip Somodevilla/Getty Images*


    The Trump administration’s long-awaited AI action plan is here, and it’s hitting
    notes [likely familiar](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/rVN?mblid=ec76fd334772&mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    to watchers of the administration’s AI policy so far: slashes to “onerous regulation,”
    opposition to “woke AI,” antagonism toward states that regulate AI, and fostering
    “global AI dominance.”


    The administration released the plan this week to follow through on a deadline
    it set in January, when [Trump repealed](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/uw4?mblid=ba72deeab9e1&mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    former President Biden’s AI executive order shortly after his inauguration. The
    plan encompasses a set of policy guidelines along with three executive orders
    covering expansion of tech exports to allies, speeding data center construction,
    and attempting to curb ideological bias in models.


    Here are some takeaways:


    **The tech industry cheered the plan, while safety groups criticized it:** Tech
    executives like Nvidia CEO Jensen Huang and AMD’s Lisa Su reportedly spoke in
    support of the plan at an unveiling event in Washington, DC, the [Wall Street
    Journal reported](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/Cit?mblid=dcf351d2e124&mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).


    Tech industry trade group NetChoice, which counts Amazon, Google, and Meta as
    members, also welcomed the plan.


    “NetChoice applauds the White House’s AI Action Plan overall and is encouraged
    to see the focus on red tape reduction and investment in America’s future,” Patrick
    Hedger, NetChoice’s director of policy, said in a statement.


    [**Keep reading here**](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/Cis?mblid=9bb6baf11555&mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).—PK


    # GREEN TECH


    ## [Power problems](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/Ci0?mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    [![Capitol Hill with he lights on](https://cdn.sanity.io/images/bl383u0v/production/1e88fa56596cf19effa14d09bb1d37f355696767-1500x1000.jpg?w=668&q=70&auto=format)](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/Ci0?mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    *Francis Scialabba*


    The debate over how the US will satisfy energy demand from data centers, EVs,
    and rising electrification continued this week in a divided Senate Committee on
    Energy and Natural Resources hearing.


    Republicans and Democrats offered different solutions to the problem, and were
    split on recent energy permitting executive orders from the Trump administration.


    Committee Chairman Sen. Mike Lee (R-UT) opened the hearing by claiming that wind
    and solar power aren’t reliable sources of energy—even when paired with battery
    storage—and that the US has “spent much of the last 20 years shutting down the
    generation that can actually meet that demand,” like coal- and natural gas-fired
    power plants.


    “The federal government has been investing heavily in certain green energy technologies
    for decades, handing out tax credits like candy,” Lee said. “Renewables and storage
    have a place. They’re capable of helping do their part to make the grid more resilient
    and reliable, but [scalability is an issue](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/wqq?mblid=87828e38892c&mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).”


    [**Keep reading here**](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/Ci0?mblid=69a78ada60f3&mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).—TC


    # AI


    ## [Still searching](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/Ci1?mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    [![An image of Google''s AI mode on a phone screen](https://cdn.sanity.io/images/bl383u0v/production/634e569e88a4170de1d527b599cf489d4473e1ac-5197x3463.jpg?w=668&q=70&auto=format)](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/Ci1?mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    *Smith Collection/Gado/Getty Images*


    You may have noticed a new tab appearing alongside the familiar news, images,
    and shopping options on the Google homepage: AI Mode.


    It’s the tech giant’s latest answer to [surging search competition](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/sjl?mblid=6649910da55a&mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    from AI apps like ChatGPT and Perplexity, and the next step after the AI Overviews
    it now inserts atop many results pages. AI Mode taps Google’s Gemini models to
    offer a more conversational search experience while drawing from content around
    the web.


    Google started testing the feature in March, rolling it out to users nationwide
    in recent weeks.


    Generative AI tools are already [reshaping the way](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/Ci6?mblid=43b572da1e9a&mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    people access information on the web. With AI Mode tucked beside the familiar
    lists of links, it could accelerate these changes. We spoke with Soufi Esmaeilzadeh,
    director of product management for Google Search, about what this might mean for
    the future of search.


    **“Fan out”:** Esmaeilzadeh said Google has been encouraged by how AI Overviews
    have led to more complex and nuanced queries. AI Mode is designed to build on
    that with an under-the-hood feature called “fan outs” that breaks questions into
    subtopics for the model to explore.


    “It brings forward a comprehensive response that gives users an overview and then
    enables them to go deeper themselves when they want to go into various websites
    and dig in further,” Esmaeilzadeh said.


    [**Keep reading here**](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/Ci1?mblid=c3f53937f600&mbcid=40841078.388531&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).—PK

    # TLDR Design 2025-07-21


    # **News & Trends**


    [**AI Vibe Coding Startup Lovable Raises $200M at $1.8B Valuation (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fsiliconangle.com%2F2025%2F07%2F17%2Fai-vibe-coding-startup-lovable-raises-200m-1-8b-valuation%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001982ceb2357-3107db08-a69a-4a13-87da-967b488b9649-000000/dnKaOhVG--ssEZ7Zg44LiJJ8C5ZXFhG39kPBDNWv4QY=414)


    Swedish AI startup Lovable Labs raised $200 million in Series A funding at an
    $1.8 billion valuation just six months after securing $15 million in pre-Series
    A funding. The company''s platform enables rapid website and app development through
    "vibe coding," where users describe their ideas in natural language and AI generates
    the corresponding code. Lovable now serves over 180,000 paying subscribers. It
    achieved $75 million in annual recurring revenue within seven months.


    [**Adobe Firefly Can Now Create Sound Effects With Your Voice and Adds More Advanced
    Video Capabilities (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.maginative.com%2Farticle%2Fadobe-firefly-can-now-create-sound-effects-with-your-voice-and-adds-more-advanced-video-capabilities%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001982ceb2357-3107db08-a69a-4a13-87da-967b488b9649-000000/B8iYgt3QIhkY9lgEO7pFU35T-5bjG8EsUN1eaGNN_iA=414)


    Adobe has introduced voice-guided sound effects to Firefly, allowing users to
    create custom audio by speaking into their microphone with precise timing and
    intensity control. The platform now integrates competitor AI models, including
    Runway''s Gen-4 and Google''s Veo3, directly within the Firefly app, eliminating
    the need to switch between different tools. Adobe maintains its focus on commercially
    safe content while adding professional video controls, such as composition reference,
    style presets, and keyframe cropping, for creators.


    [**These new emojis are coming to your iPhone in iOS 26 (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2F9to5mac.com%2F2025%2F07%2F17%2Fthese-new-emoji-are-coming-to-your-iphone-in-ios-26%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001982ceb2357-3107db08-a69a-4a13-87da-967b488b9649-000000/EU8-KoY33OEIhaqQUvehCFFjhCrgwxpBPYdCuC0xCuU=414)


    The Unicode Consortium has announced eight new emojis that will be included in
    iOS 26, including Bigfoot (Hairy Creature), Orca, Apple Core, and Ballet Dancers.
    Although Apple will design its own versions, these emojis are expected to roll
    out in a later iOS 26 update, likely not in the initial release. Until then, users
    can experiment with similar creations using Apple''s Genmoji feature.


    # **Opinions & Tutorials**


    [**How would Nietzsche redesign Instagram if he were Zuckerberg? (13 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fuxdesign.cc%2Fhow-would-nietzsche-redesign-instagram-if-he-were-zuckerberg-375a62e398db%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001982ceb2357-3107db08-a69a-4a13-87da-967b488b9649-000000/W19gtrgkPCdfgfsU5Fz7l7a4lF8iqsbMOXbwVnVs4t0=414)


    Nietzsche would likely oppose fact-checking and hate speech bans and beauty filters,
    favoring free expression, authenticity, and the rejection of imposed moral norms.
    His philosophy encourages individuals to embrace their fate, experiment with values,
    and confront convention through art, contradiction, and unfiltered self-expression.


    [**Design Patterns For AI Interfaces (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fsmart-interface-design-patterns.com%2Farticles%2Fai-design-patterns%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001982ceb2357-3107db08-a69a-4a13-87da-967b488b9649-000000/2GxQk12BeRLFfSbexTx245jvXxAB7rBivp4pXRWq074=414)


    Traditional AI chat interfaces are giving way to task-oriented UIs with controls
    like sliders and buttons, as chatbots burden users with inefficient intent articulation.
    Better AI experiences involve using visual nodes and canvases instead of manual
    prompts, visualizing results, employing UI controls and presets for tweaking,
    enabling task completion and result manipulation, and embedding features where
    actual work happens rather than isolated products. Successful AI design prioritizes
    user needs, incorporating AI functionality strategically across customer journeys
    where it delivers genuine value, rather than imposing AI-first approaches.


    [**Beyond Copilots: The Rise of the AI Agent Orchestration Platform (5 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fuxmag.com%2Farticles%2Fbeyond-copilots-the-rise-of-the-ai-agent-orchestration-platform%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001982ceb2357-3107db08-a69a-4a13-87da-967b488b9649-000000/7R9ALt6jcoAQv-CBfKrEBWt-SoGV9t8Ci9m-qKqxSc0=414)


    AI agent orchestration platforms are emerging as the next evolution beyond copilots,
    coordinating fleets of specialized autonomous agents across workflows and tools
    rather than offering siloed assistance. These platforms break down complex goals
    into subtasks, assign them to appropriate agents, and manage coordination across
    systems, transforming isolated AI actions into comprehensive operations. The shift
    represents a strategic inflection point driven by agent maturity, enterprise demand
    for autonomy, and vendor momentum toward AI-first architectures that reimagine
    software around agents and natural language.

    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Crafting Visual Identity: Acrea''s Digital Transformation Journey (3 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fabduzeedo.com%2Fcrafting-visual-identity-acreas-digital-transformation-journey%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001982ceb2357-3107db08-a69a-4a13-87da-967b488b9649-000000/OSP6f54aE0TjEuuJmHaBvOKkk8lHJMepPyPqbPhlDkY=414)


    Alphamark''s rebranding of Swiss consultancy Acrea brings a human, approachable
    touch to the often impersonal world of digital transformation, aligning the brand''s
    identity with its values of professionalism, clarity, and personalized service.
    Through thoughtful design choices—like a transformation-themed logo, people-focused
    photography, and a warm, clean visual system—Acrea now communicates trust, expertise,
    and digital progress across all platforms.


    [**Six Design Lessons from this Year''s Cannes Lions (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.designweek.co.uk%2Fsix-design-lessons-from-this-years-cannes-lions%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001982ceb2357-3107db08-a69a-4a13-87da-967b488b9649-000000/XTGwkYw_BI7R2cJ7g4-IpM02bj4J7p25OkQALd3yFT8=414)


    This year''s Cannes Lions examined how technology, purpose, and design are reshaping
    brand building. AI is transforming workflows by handling production while humans
    focus on taste and judgment, with designers moving upstream to lead rather than
    compete with machines. Brand purpose has evolved from lofty statements to measurable
    action, with companies like Reckitt demonstrating a long-term commitment through
    programs like Catalyst, featuring Serena Williams.


    [**Brand Architecture: A Strategic Tool (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fbrandingstrategyinsider.com%2Fbrand-architecture-a-strategic-tool%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001982ceb2357-3107db08-a69a-4a13-87da-967b488b9649-000000/02AuzIcAKwDsdefT3o-SotBSlRfSji-ODt9lvt9RdoQ=414)


    Brand architecture serves as a strategic tool for marketing leaders to organize
    complex brand portfolios, necessitating in-depth conversations about business
    strategy and customer needs, rather than simple structural decisions. Marketing
    directors must guide organizations through two critical perspectives: understanding
    the business''s strategic growth plans and examining how brands serve customers
    in the marketplace. When executed appropriately with stakeholder involvement,
    portfolio auditing, and research-driven decisions, brand architecture becomes
    a powerful driver of long-term value, aligning brand clarity with business growth.

    # TLDR Founders 2025-07-25


    # **Headlines & Trends**


    [**OpenAI prepares to launch GPT-5 in August (13 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2Fnotepad-microsoft-newsletter%2F712950%2Fopenai-gpt-5-model-release-date-notepad%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001984188aa09-a9f490ab-ab56-492b-bb73-abffcb52e414-000000/Xk8yhdEXBQpFHRrO5Te4l-qL3j8vTMJYO-5WJWq4DWY=415)


    OpenAI plans to launch GPT-5 in early August, offering integrated o3 reasoning
    capabilities and mini/nano versions available through its API. GPT-5 aims to unify
    OpenAI''s language models and simplify usage across applications, although it
    won''t reach AGI status immediately. The anticipated declaration of AGI could
    impact OpenAI''s revenue agreement with Microsoft.


    [**CrowdStrike-backed compliance startup Vanta valued at \$4 billion in new funding
    round (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.cnbc.com%2F2025%2F07%2F23%2Fcrowdstrike-backed-vanta-is-valued-at-4-billion-in-new-funding-round.html%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001984188aa09-a9f490ab-ab56-492b-bb73-abffcb52e414-000000/pg_Ix-WdjdlPXjDCcW8cxPJUphiYgrjDc2Ob2WGX1_I=415)


    Vanta''s valuation surged to \$4 billion after closing a \$150 million funding
    round backed by CrowdStrike Ventures. The startup, which helps companies manage
    compliance with cybersecurity frameworks like SOC 2 and ISO 27001, serves over
    12,000 customers, including tech giants Atlassian and Snowflake. More investors
    included Wellington Management, Atlassian Ventures, JPMorgan Chase, and Sequoia
    Capital.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**How to get recommended by ChatGPT (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.growthunhinged.com%2Fp%2Fget-recommended-by-chatgpt%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001984188aa09-a9f490ab-ab56-492b-bb73-abffcb52e414-000000/kekKHOGXa6Avqep_UOFYf8rFISvaigc768STQmcrlp0=415)


    AI answer engines are becoming the most influential gatekeepers in B2B buying,
    with ChatGPT hitting a billion users and 2.5 billion daily prompts. Buyers now
    ask AI what to buy instead of researching themselves - if your product isn''t
    mentioned, it might as well not exist. Josh Blyskal from Profound found only 11%
    of citations overlap between ChatGPT and Perplexity, meaning you need platform-specific
    strategies. Reddit is now the most-cited domain at 6% of citations, and one-in-three
    citations come from comparative listicles. Almost half of cited domains shift
    within a single month.


    [**Your Complete Guide to Revenue Leakage (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.mostlymetrics.com%2Fp%2Fyour-complete-guide-to-revenue-leakage%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001984188aa09-a9f490ab-ab56-492b-bb73-abffcb52e414-000000/WaljiRsnoXjsCcgYqJmKqqBBIgT4OGftd2erf2U4FMk=415)


    Revenue leakage is the gap between what you should earn and what you actually
    collect - the ghost quietly draining dollars through missed invoices, zombie accounts
    still getting service, and pilot pricing that never graduates. It''s a systems
    problem disguised as a people problem, living in the cracks between sales handoffs
    and billing processes. Common culprits include auto-renewals that silently fail,
    discounts hardcoded forever, and churned customers still accessing your product
    months later.


    [**Reframing AI chatbots as self-service tools (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.helpscout.com%2Fblog%2Freframing-as-chatbots%2F%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001984188aa09-a9f490ab-ab56-492b-bb73-abffcb52e414-000000/TjJxDBs2ZfwcLnIlK5s8mz1sa-1Kw73Orb7ZkM8SLgo=415)


    AI chatbots should be reframed as self-service tools rather than human support
    replacements due to their limitations. Achieving this involves clearly defining
    their purpose and implementing technical guardrails to ensure alignment. Understanding
    AI''s capabilities and limits helps in effectively integrating them into customer
    support.

    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Zero-sum Thinking and the Labor Market (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fkyla.substack.com%2Fp%2Fzero-sum-thinking-and-the-labor-market%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001984188aa09-a9f490ab-ab56-492b-bb73-abffcb52e414-000000/hEDjulXTP8Qu1ZFj2XC00IU1guPL3yd7Ia33ZvrE2RE=415)


    College graduates now have higher unemployment rates than the overall workforce
    for the first time since 2018 - the opposite of how this is supposed to work.
    Young men are struggling most, with 50,000 healthcare jobs going to women graduates
    while men gained far fewer positions across all sectors. People are applying to
    1,000 jobs and getting rejected by algorithms in what''s become a casino economy
    where getting hired feels like winning the lottery. This broken system feeds zero-sum
    thinking - the belief that my success requires your failure - which has replaced
    the Sputnik generation''s positive-sum worldview where everyone could grow together.


    [**The General Theory of Enshittification (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fpaulkrugman.substack.com%2Fp%2Fthe-general-theory-of-enshittification%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001984188aa09-a9f490ab-ab56-492b-bb73-abffcb52e414-000000/ZthZUNxeQMQ7ffHGxJKhI-vVcocdmq-DPw5aO9DbzH8=415)


    Enshittification isn''t just about social media - it''s the natural lifecycle
    of any business with network effects. Companies offer great value to build their
    user base, then exploit that base once locked in. Uber''s "earnings inflection
    strategy" jumping from losses to profits by squeezing customers proves this was
    always the plan.


    [**What Founders Teach Us (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdebliu.substack.com%2Fp%2Fwhat-founders-teach-us%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001984188aa09-a9f490ab-ab56-492b-bb73-abffcb52e414-000000/TWrtlcIELAWMyU78FRSR5w3aw3eBywRukKXumIeRrLY=415)


    Founders are river people, not villagers - they thrive in uncertainty while others
    choose stability. They see differently: they''re fearless enough to hear "no"
    constantly but keep asking, they actively seek contrarians to challenge their
    thinking, and they know execution beats strategy. They ignore the right feedback,
    focus obsessively on recruiting A-players, and carry unshakable optimism despite
    knowing 90% of startups fail.

    # TLDR 2025-07-24


    # **Big Tech & Startups**


    [**Tesla claims it produced the first builds of its ‘new affordable'' electric
    car models (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Felectrek.co%2F2025%2F07%2F23%2Ftesla-claims-produced-first-builds-new-affordable-electric-car-models%2F%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/010001983c0a2076-ed274b92-9519-4261-b42f-db2a7ac06d6b-000000/iLPpMM1z5J9O5SfAfVxiNoW_Z7zLM96QgWIyVms1VC0=415)


    Tesla claims to have produced the first builds of its new, more affordable electric
    car models in June. Volume production has been planned for the second half of
    the year. Plans for a 2025 launch remain on track. The vehicle is expected to
    be a ''stripped-down'' Model Y with fewer materials, fewer features, and possibly
    a slightly smaller size.


    [**SpaceX''s Cellular Starlink Launches Today Via T-Mobile: What You Need to Know
    (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2F6w0TWc/1/010001983c0a2076-ed274b92-9519-4261-b42f-db2a7ac06d6b-000000/hexJXxJYzhmEXRPsR_pertl2cXeTfIRbMM5QjrmrGRQ=415)


    T-Mobile and SpaceX''s T-Satellite service is now available to subscribers, allowing
    smartphone users to remain connected even in deadzones. Existing T-Mobile customers
    can purchase the cellular Starlink service as an add-on - those on pricier plans
    like Experience Beyond and Go5G Next get it as a free perk. People on other networks
    can also subscribe through a secondary eSIM. Those who participated in the free
    trial should now expect to be charged for the service.


    # **Science & Futuristic Technology**


    [**Meta Unveils Wristband for Controlling Computers With Hand Gestures (7 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FldIBaI/1/010001983c0a2076-ed274b92-9519-4261-b42f-db2a7ac06d6b-000000/4N4LPMmG-XOks10M1tveIgrKxXjl5dSBboxZJAXPRx0=415)


    Meta''s wristband reads the electrical signals that pulse through the muscles
    when people move their fingers. It uses a technique called electromyography to
    gather electrical signals from muscles in the forearm. These signals can reveal
    what people are about to do even before they do it. With enough practice, people
    using the wristband can control devices simply by producing the right thought.


    [**Neuralink Sees \$1 Billion of Revenue by 2031 in Vast Expansion (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2F3N9ick/1/010001983c0a2076-ed274b92-9519-4261-b42f-db2a7ac06d6b-000000/bq9bT0rA_qLxU4zO2owE1Wba0l5b7SzYJQeSFbZMqs4=415)


    Neuralink expects to put its chips in 20,000 people a year and generate at least
    \$1 billion in annual revenue by 2031. It plans to have about five large clinics
    in operation and at least three versions of its device available. The company''s
    figures assume a conservative reimbursement of \$50,000 per surgery. Several other
    brain companies are building and testing similar devices. No brain-computer interfaces
    have yet been commercially approved for permanent implantation by the US FDA -
    Neuralink expects to gain regulatory approval in the US for its first device by
    2029.


    # **Programming, Design & Data Science**


    [**Docs for AI agents (11 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ftechnicalwriting.dev%2Fai%2Fagents%2F%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/010001983c0a2076-ed274b92-9519-4261-b42f-db2a7ac06d6b-000000/YWXPX7ihLnEeo-2GPLRcMOYKG2Zwhy5onNhfPoTRO6M=415)


    Agent docs are a way to get better results from agents. They make agent output
    more consistent, more aligned with codebase conventions, and more accurate. This
    post discusses how to implement agent docs into a project. It covers how agent
    docs are different from internal eng docs, best practices for AI docs, and reasons
    why agent and eng docs should be kept separate.


    [**A valid HTML zip bomb (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fache.one%2Fnotes%2Fhtml_zip_bomb%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/010001983c0a2076-ed274b92-9519-4261-b42f-db2a7ac06d6b-000000/qy6DY1vN3VodgKi_lMaWKh_juveZOTScpjGhqtXD55E=415)


    One way to deal with aggressive web crawlers that don''t respect robots.txt is
    to exhaust their resources. This post goes through how to build a valid HTML zip
    bomb that exhausts bots'' RAM. The implementation technique exploits the asymmetry
    of the resources needed to serve the zip bomb versus those needed to detect it.
    Bots that respect robots.txt won''t be affected by the zip bomb as the path to
    the zip bomb is forbidden in the specification.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Why Amazon Wants an AI Bracelet That Records Everything You Say (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2F5oGTD2/1/010001983c0a2076-ed274b92-9519-4261-b42f-db2a7ac06d6b-000000/YJ-Kt6q9-g9Z6cO2zOcR8pUXYtXhqptHywpSpH-c8ak=415)


    Bee''s wearable bracelet transcribes users'' conversations and then uses artificial
    intelligence to turn that data into searchable history. The company''s chief executive
    recently announced that Bee is joining Amazon in a yet-to-be-signed deal. The
    data that such a device could gather could help Amazon build more advanced AI
    models. Amazon hasn''t provided any official details on its motivations for acquiring
    the company.


    [**Jeff Bezos weighing possible acquisition of CNBC cable network (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fnypost.com%2F2025%2F07%2F23%2Fmedia%2Fjeff-bezos-has-been-weighing-a-possible-acquisition-of-cnbc-sources%2F%3Futm_source=tldrnewsletter/1/010001983c0a2076-ed274b92-9519-4261-b42f-db2a7ac06d6b-000000/nFiMbDQs3P_LwlG8fRfVikzLOoAb5nrQ4tWhn2xdVV4=415)


    Jeff Bezos has signaled his interest in buying CNBC. The network would serve as
    a credible ''neural voice'' in his media portfolio. Bezos also owns the left-leaning
    Washington Post. Comcast plans to spin off its struggling cable assets by the
    end of the year. CNBC will become part of a publicly-traded company called Versant
    - there will be a two-year period where Versant will not be able to sell major
    assets without major tax implications.

    # AI


    ## [Trusted agents](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BYI?mbcid=40748606.390640&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    [![A pair of glasses hovering over an accounting spreadsheet, binary code floating
    over the document.](https://cdn.sanity.io/images/bl383u0v/production/a0fbf67cf388de99d1ac03a68ea6101d1a0c173c-1500x1000.jpg?w=668&q=70&auto=format)](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BYI?mbcid=40748606.390640&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    *Credit: Illustration: Morning Brew, Photos: Getty Images*


    It’s humbling to admit you don’t know something—maybe doubly so for an AI trained
    to be an all-knowing answer machine. Put on the spot, these systems just seem
    to prefer fudging facts.


    Needless to say, that’s not a trait that small businesses want in a bookkeeper.
    But Intuit CTO Alex Balazs tells us it’s hammered that habit out of QuickBooks’s
    AI products.


    “We spend a lot of time and energy making sure that the [agents](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BYL?mblid=3c47fccf0e9b&mbcid=40748606.390640&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    err on the side of saying, ‘I don’t know,’” Balazs said at a recent Manhattan
    event.


    The financial software giant behind services like TurboTax, Credit Karma, and
    Mailchimp has a new cast of AI helpers on offer to its small and medium-sized
    business clients.


    One is a payments agent that will manage and predict the lateness of invoice collection
    and draw up reminder emails in a chosen tone. An accounting agent categorizes
    expenses, and a customer agent prioritizes leads, drafts introductory chats, and
    schedules meetings. Other tools cover payroll, finance, and project management.


    Balazs said the goal is to make the businesses feel as if they can delegate these
    tasks in the same way they would to a human worker.


    “We instructed \[the agents] to say, ‘Here’s where you’re starting; this is what
    the outcome is; here are the things you have access to; go complete the task for
    the customer. And oh, by the way, keep track of everything you’re doing and show
    them all your work at the end so they have complete control,’” Balazs said.


    [**Keep reading here**](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BYI?mblid=5cd9a9710742&mbcid=40748606.390640&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).—PK

    # FUTURE OF TRAVEL


    ## [Tick tock](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BYJ?mbcid=40748606.390640&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    [![A Ford EV plugged into a charger.](https://cdn.sanity.io/images/bl383u0v/production/91e226fbdb5af9e6d7b73d0b45f90474b7736d88-5812x3875.jpg?w=668&q=70&auto=format)](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BYJ?mbcid=40748606.390640&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    *Nathan Howard/Getty Images*


    Now’s the time to buy.


    That’s the message Ford is pitching amid a bevy of EV deals industrywide ahead
    of the Sept. 30 expiration of tax credits on EV purchases and leases.


    The automaker recently extended through the end of September its Ford Power Promise,
    which aims to promote at-home charging by providing EV buyers with complimentary
    home chargers and installation.


    “With everything that’s happening in the marketplace, not only the incentives
    that we have…and the fact that tax credits are still out there for some of these
    makes and models, now is the time to really double down and get as much as you
    can as a consumer,” Stacey Ferreira, Ford’s director of US sales strategy, told
    Tech Brew.


    **What’s changing:** President Donald Trump signed the “One Big Beautiful Bill
    Act” into law on July 4, nixing EV tax credits from the 2022 Inflation Reduction
    Act.


    Those include a $7,500 tax credit for qualified new EV purchases, a $4,000 credit
    for qualified used EVs, and a “leasing loophole” that allows automakers to pass
    on incentives for some models that don’t qualify for the other credits.


    [**Keep reading here**](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BYJ?mblid=a4a51065ba1b&mbcid=40748606.390640&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).—JG


    # AI


    ## [In summary](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BYK?mbcid=40748606.390640&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    [![A doctor''s hand selecting from a clear AI screen with a digitized body in
    front of a laptop.](https://cdn.sanity.io/images/bl383u0v/production/acd075d0e9e0a3fdfd40f497732670a93d14760a-5422x3614.jpg?w=668&q=70&auto=format)](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BYK?mbcid=40748606.390640&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    *Pcess609/Getty Images*


    With AI wearing ever-more hats in all kinds of workplaces, researchers are scrambling
    to [devise tests](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/xkB?mblid=d7a576153c48&mbcid=40748606.390640&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    that grade how well the technology actually performs in its myriad roles. In healthcare
    alone, several new benchmarks aim to gauge AI’s prowess in medical settings.


    But none of the current tests look at how well AI can summarize real-world medical
    studies, a new report from startup Atropos Health claimed. The authors proposed
    a new framework to evaluate this skill on nine major models from Google, OpenAI,
    and Anthropic.


    This kind of summarization is important because large linked databases of electronic
    health records and automation tools have made real-world evidence more abundant
    and accessible, the authors wrote. As a company that uses AI to generate real-world
    evidence reports, Atropos has a vested interest here as well.


    **Report card:** Google’s Gemini models were the clear winners among the nine
    models that researchers tested. But different models had various pros and cons.


    [**Keep reading here**](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BYK?mblid=eac332cb2a88&mbcid=40748606.390640&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).—PK

    # TLDR Product Management 2025-07-22


    # **News & Trends**


    [**Content and Community (24 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fstratechery.com%2F2025%2Fcontent-and-community%3Futm_source=tldrproduct/1/01000198319f10c7-a11303ef-5afb-43a9-966f-4f91e276195a-000000/5C19MhUX0eEBGo-VqDOqCbBfLsWvXT4RFYtLXU3qn3A=414)


    Content creation has evolved from manual duplication to AI-driven automation,
    unbundling every step in the communication value chain. As AI commoditizes content,
    traditional publishers will lose their edge. Future success will hinge on building
    communities and direct relationships rather than relying on scale or advertising.


    [**Death by Tooling: How Multiple Tools Kill Product Management (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdpereira.substack.com%2Fp%2Fdeath-by-tooling-how-multiple-tools%3Futm_source=tldrproduct/1/01000198319f10c7-a11303ef-5afb-43a9-966f-4f91e276195a-000000/-FuOiN6qxBKeFh5vGfvxHot1VvszvZ2ITqiktLhZocg=414)


    Teams often become overwhelmed by excessive tool usage, causing fragmented communication
    and decreased productivity. The solution lies in using fewer, comprehensive tools
    and regularly reviewing their actual value to streamline workflows effectively.


    # **Opinions & Tutorials**


    [**A startup is a bundle, and Windsurf broke the bundle (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdanco.substack.com%2Fp%2Fa-startup-is-a-bundle-and-windsurf%3Futm_source=tldrproduct/1/01000198319f10c7-a11303ef-5afb-43a9-966f-4f91e276195a-000000/Dpqx7Bq98-Zdwanz5kQV6pBia0eL8SHwI1EDlYbzM5s=414)


    Windsurf''s outcome may look like a win for everyone, but it reveals a deeper
    shift: the breakdown of the startup bundle that once aligned founders, investors,
    and employees around shared equity. As AI talent grows more valuable, deals are
    becoming unbundled, making it harder to build unified startups and weakening the
    collaborative spirit that drives innovation.


    [**How to Build a Successful Product: Lessons from Launching and Growing a Freight
    Transportation Platform (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fuxplanet.org%2Fhow-to-build-a-successful-product-lessons-from-launching-and-growing-a-freight-transportation-1b340b38399c%3Futm_source=tldrproduct/1/01000198319f10c7-a11303ef-5afb-43a9-966f-4f91e276195a-000000/7iQTCrWIjtQrMTiqPKHDP0IVFiM2Rlv88er28Pbf9kY=414)


    Successful product building requires flexibility, constant adaptation to user
    feedback, and rapid validation of hypotheses instead of strictly following initial
    plans. Focusing on user needs, ensuring the product solves valuable problems (not
    just usability), and maintaining direct communication within teams accelerates
    meaningful growth.

    # TLDR Design 2025-07-24


    # **News & Trends**


    [**Netflix Starts Using GenAI in its Shows and Films (1 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ftechcrunch.com%2F2025%2F07%2F18%2Fnetflix-starts-using-genai-in-its-shows-and-films%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001983c5a2f28-5699bdea-6fb4-4592-bc60-6853416ca026-000000/U16dE2ESpZZu8BaBFJXHle98Bs06ENPTJbgFfoD94a0=415)


    Netflix has begun incorporating generative AI into its original productions. Co-CEO
    Ted Sarandos recently revealed that the first AI-generated final footage appeared
    in the Argentine show, "El Eternauta," in a scene involving a building collapse.
    The AI-created scene was completed 10 times faster and at lower cost than traditional
    visual effects methods would have required. Beyond production, Netflix is expanding
    its use of AI across personalization, search, and advertising. It plans to launch
    interactive ads later this year.


    [**Polaroid Just Dropped the Most Iconic Anti-AI Ad of the Year (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.creativebloq.com%2Fdesign%2Fbranding%2Fpolaroid-just-dropped-the-most-iconic-anti-ai-ad-of-the-year%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001983c5a2f28-5699bdea-6fb4-4592-bc60-6853416ca026-000000/t1O2-RWbwKIhfDGcW3XZEEILGfsgufcmQqaB6Nx3rNo=415)


    Polaroid has launched a powerful anti-AI campaign to promote its new Flip camera,
    emphasizing the value of tangible, real-life experiences over digital saturation.
    The campaign uses nostalgic Polaroid imagery paired with provocative slogans like
    “AI can''t generate sand between your toes” to highlight the emotional depth and
    authenticity of analog living. Strategically placed near tech hubs like Apple
    and Google offices, the campaign has resonated widely online, drawing praise for
    its aesthetic and timely critique of tech culture.


    [**Figma Announces Launch of Initial Public Offering Roadshow (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.figma.com%2Fblog%2Fipo-roadshow-launch%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001983c5a2f28-5699bdea-6fb4-4592-bc60-6853416ca026-000000/mKPFHhQSLnLVuY8mMNGHOmCA-3fMBB5lJR5eACSoH8E=415)


    Figma launched its IPO roadshow, offering 12.5 million new shares, plus 24.6 million
    from existing stockholders, at a price range of \$25 to \$ 28 per share. The design
    platform company applied to list on the NYSE under the ticker "FIG" with significant
    investment banks leading the offering. Figma won''t receive proceeds from existing
    stockholder sales, while underwriters have a 30-day overallotment option for additional
    shares.


    # **Opinions & Tutorials**


    [**Afraid of losing your design job to AI? This McDonald''s story might help you
    sleep better (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.creativebloq.com%2Fai%2Fafraid-of-losing-your-design-job-this-mcdonalds-story-might-help-you-sleep-better%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001983c5a2f28-5699bdea-6fb4-4592-bc60-6853416ca026-000000/HCvrhgmfhpvIVPjwi2fg6VuhsbOc9Qkb7A71EYZxNLw=415)


    Fears that AI will replace creative jobs echo earlier anxieties about McDonald''s
    touchscreen kiosks, which were expected to eliminate human roles but instead led
    to more jobs and higher sales by enhancing the customer experience. The key takeaway
    is that technology doesn''t determine outcomes—organizations do. Design studios
    that use AI to amplify human creativity, not just cut costs, will thrive.


    [**Designing Software for AI Agents (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.lukew.com%2Fff%2Fentry.asp%3F2111%26utm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001983c5a2f28-5699bdea-6fb4-4592-bc60-6853416ca026-000000/5u2-_A5FyG6S_kyWarOut4m3SDbWl6EJQARMh-ommbE=415)


    AI agents increasingly handle computing tasks but struggle with software designed
    for humans, creating opportunities to redesign systems for machine use. Web search
    APIs limit results and provide condensed snippets suited for human scanning, while
    agents could benefit from more comprehensive results and larger document summaries.
    AgentDB exemplifies agent-first design by utilizing UUIDs for instant database
    creation, storing databases as files rather than hosting them as services, and
    integrating with MCP servers to make data easily accessible as AI model context.


    [**AI Tools + AI Fluency + Human Advantage = AI-native Designer (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fuxdesign.cc%2Fai-tools-ai-fluency-human-advantage-ai-native-designer-bade3494e7aa%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001983c5a2f28-5699bdea-6fb4-4592-bc60-6853416ca026-000000/NeKgwEHvNCjwZeyds2RSEkwA6R_MVEUiRm8CYcb8big=415)


    Product designers can thrive in the AI era by mastering three key areas: leveraging
    AI tools for faster shipping, developing AI fluency for designing probabilistic
    systems, and harnessing human advantages such as craft and creative direction.
    While AI handles routine tasks and generation, designers must evolve into orchestrators
    who provide vision, set constraints, and make high-level decisions that guide
    AI outputs. The future belongs to AI-native designers who combine technical literacy
    with uniquely human skills like strategic thinking, storytelling, and the ability
    to create memorable experiences that transcend generic AI outputs.

    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Impact Stories: How Bloom repositioned Ginsters (2023) (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.designweek.co.uk%2Fimpact-stories-how-bloom-repositioned-ginsters-2023%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001983c5a2f28-5699bdea-6fb4-4592-bc60-6853416ca026-000000/hGXXG-wSDe9erU_WK3obYkZuZPyvJC0AQkpEMvn_pj4=415)


    By 2022, Ginsters faced a perception problem: widely recognized but associated
    with low quality and outdated imagery, it struggled to attract new customers despite
    a strong sales history. A strategic rebrand by Bloom in 2023 revitalized the brand
    through updated design, storytelling, and a more confident tone, resulting in
    major sales growth, improved brand perception, and successful product innovation
    aimed at younger audiences.


    [**How Semantics and ARIA Attributes Support Accessible Design (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.tpgi.com%2Fhow-semantics-aria-attributes-support-accessible-design%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001983c5a2f28-5699bdea-6fb4-4592-bc60-6853416ca026-000000/yZnHmjO6qmXCDL269SOMK6FH5yx02lZY8S2aB2VBhoI=415)


    Accessibility issues stem from missing semantic meaning rather than visual problems,
    as elements may look correct but fail to communicate their purpose to assistive
    technologies. Proper semantics using HTML elements, consistent ARIA design patterns,
    and appropriate attributes work together to create interfaces that screen readers
    and keyboard users can navigate effectively. Comprehensive accessibility audits
    must test beyond visual appearance to ensure semantic roles match user expectations
    and that interactive elements behave predictably for all users.


    [**Design Tokens for Links (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdesigntokens.substack.com%2Fp%2Fdesign-tokes-for-links%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001983c5a2f28-5699bdea-6fb4-4592-bc60-6853416ca026-000000/DV9GFV1veFvAP3RqfVcCEuF6ocq-Ul9TJeSlNTuIhoo=415)


    Design systems face an architectural challenge when organizing hyperlinks within
    token structures, as links occupy a unique position between atomic elements that
    can exist independently or integrate into complex components. Two approaches emerge:
    treating links as semantic tokens (reusing text category tokens for flexibility
    and reusability) versus specific tokens (creating dedicated link namespaces for
    clarity and explicit purpose). The choice depends on system complexity, with semantic
    tokens being better suited for scalable systems that support multiple themes,
    while specific tokens work well for simpler systems with clearly differentiated
    link behaviors.
