    # TLDR Web Dev 2025-07-21


    # **Articles & Tutorials**


    [**Make Your Own Backup System – Part 1: Strategy Before Scripts (13 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fit-notes.dragas.net%2F2025%2F07%2F18%2Fmake-your-own-backup-system-part-1-strategy-before-scripts%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001982cb8aadd-adcf0c2b-eb6a-4bd4-9633-8e1d209bad10-000000/DHIPQmgQmHaDvYG72NkTKwaiyyQUmonzNFnjlDPPKsA=414)


    Common pitfalls of inadequate backups include relying solely on cloud providers
    or failing to test restoration procedures. There are many important decisions
    to think through in a backup strategy, such as the critical decision between full
    disk and individual file backups. All systems should have a secure, fast, and
    efficient backup system with external storage and minimal invasiveness, with a
    "pull" architecture where the backup server initiates the process when possible.


    [**How we tracked down a Go 1.24 memory regression across hundreds of pods (12
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.datadoghq.com%2Fblog%2Fengineering%2Fgo-memory-regression%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001982cb8aadd-adcf0c2b-eb6a-4bd4-9633-8e1d209bad10-000000/L5sIz0Pg-x1uMD0A6mYRDsEpxGkEaqcMmWzgzA0WFJA=414)


    Datadog investigated an unexpected memory usage increase after upgrading to Go
    1.24 in its data-processing services. The issue came from a regression in the
    memory allocator that caused unnecessary zeroing of large objects with pointers,
    leading to higher Resident Set Size (RSS). Collaborating with the Go community,
    it identified the root cause and validated a fix that will be included in Go 1.25,
    restoring the previous memory optimization.


    [**Asynchrony is not Concurrency (12 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fkristoff.it%2Fblog%2Fasynchrony-is-not-concurrency%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001982cb8aadd-adcf0c2b-eb6a-4bd4-9633-8e1d209bad10-000000/epIlTk08m3ISQcB8RZTGWNCtDeMOuD10j0yAZh0hwdM=414)


    Asynchrony and concurrency are distinct concepts, a nuance often missed. Asynchrony
    allows tasks to run out of order while remaining correct, while concurrency enables
    a system to progress multiple tasks, either simultaneously or through task switching.
    The lack of distinction between these concepts has led to duplicated efforts in
    libraries, viral async code, and suboptimal solutions.


    # **Opinions & Advice**


    [**Coding with LLMs in the summer of 2025 (an update) (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fantirez.com%2Fnews%2F154%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001982cb8aadd-adcf0c2b-eb6a-4bd4-9633-8e1d209bad10-000000/DMjOws5CpumFooiBuQuc8p4iTC948qPcIvG9qPIW5Pc=414)


    Frontier LLMs like Gemini 2.5 Pro are great for coding by finding bugs, exploring
    ideas, helping with pair-design, speeding up code writing, and allowing work in
    unfamiliar technologies. Developers should avoid letting LLMs autonomously code
    complex projects and provide extensive context, including potential solutions
    and code style, to use LLMs effectively.


    [**Why I''m Betting Against AI Agents in 2025 (Despite Building Them) (10 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Futkarshkanwat.com%2Fwriting%2Fbetting-against-agents%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001982cb8aadd-adcf0c2b-eb6a-4bd4-9633-8e1d209bad10-000000/UrWiHaOSzHX6W6BW5a8PQbf4noBFzsuJRlxnnocmntw=414)


    The current hype around fully autonomous AI agents in 2025 is unrealistic due
    to mathematical limitations and engineering challenges. Error compounding in multi-step
    workflows and the quadratic token costs of conversational agents make truly autonomous
    systems impractical currently. Instead, it''s better to build constrained, domain-specific
    AI tools that handle complexity while maintaining human control.


    [**Nobody Knows How to Build With AI Yet (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fworksonmymachine.substack.com%2Fp%2Fnobody-knows-how-to-build-with-ai%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001982cb8aadd-adcf0c2b-eb6a-4bd4-9633-8e1d209bad10-000000/rkNprvdfVMddcB33ycrGJRFYjX29o3yNG8SFWDl-lew=414)


    Building software fast and efficiently with AI is still a personal experience.
    This developer uses a four-document system to manage AI''s work along with his
    own workflow. The four documents are (1) an architecture overview, (2) technical
    considerations, (3) a workflow process for both AI and humans to follow, and (4)
    the story breakdown to make sure AI always has recent context.


    # **Launches & Tools**


    [**Conductor (Website)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fconductor.build%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001982cb8aadd-adcf0c2b-eb6a-4bd4-9633-8e1d209bad10-000000/b20ESzVsF2Q9cX0rqxuD34WU613yzPzufo1vHkEn3n4=414)


    Conductor is a UI-driven tool that allows devs to run multiple Claude Code agents
    in parallel, each with its own isolated workspace. The tool handles git worktrees
    automatically, letting devs monitor agent progress, identify issues, and review
    code changes.


    [**Am I Vibing (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fascorbic%2Fam-i-vibing%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001982cb8aadd-adcf0c2b-eb6a-4bd4-9633-8e1d209bad10-000000/XuQawDL9D4VY310PN-Iq3BlOpwoQXCfLMWgv5pkb9Vw=414)


    am-i-vibing is a library and CLI tool that detects if code is being executed within
    an AI agentic environment. It identifies agent, interactive, and hybrid environments
    to allow CLI tools and Node apps to adapt their behavior and outputs to help agents
    out.


    [**Kilo Code (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2FKilo-Org%2Fkilocode%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001982cb8aadd-adcf0c2b-eb6a-4bd4-9633-8e1d209bad10-000000/A6qFDLwcDZUctJp2low3J5Nj2CMR-hTknJId0dehHec=414)


    Kilo Code is an open-source VS Code AI agent that merges features from Roo Code
    and Cline, with code generation from natural language and task automation. It
    offers $20 in free credits for advanced AI models like Gemini 2.5 Pro and Claude
    4 Sonnet and Opus and does not require API keys to get started.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Death by AI (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdavebarry.substack.com%2Fp%2Fdeath-by-ai%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001982cb8aadd-adcf0c2b-eb6a-4bd4-9633-8e1d209bad10-000000/iu1fWpXugf6eDmkHWAomW7GyrkalRgvatXCKtKSZX3k=414)


    Google AI incorrectly declared Dave Barry dead in its search summary. Despite
    Barry''s attempts to correct the AI''s error through feedback and chat, the AI
    continued to alternate between declaring him dead or providing inaccurate information
    about his life.


    [**Rethinking CLI interfaces for AI (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.notcheckmark.com%2F2025%2F07%2Frethinking-cli-interfaces-for-ai%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001982cb8aadd-adcf0c2b-eb6a-4bd4-9633-8e1d209bad10-000000/g8LrN88P_C4kBoLTDagli0ggU8S980oTTsUZCJ41cjo=414)


    CLI interfaces and APIs will need to be rethought to better suit LLM agents, especially
    those with limited context windows. Current designs often lead to excessive tool
    calls and inefficient use of resources. Instead, it''s probably better to augment
    CLI tools with additional context and structure to improve the LLM''s understanding
    and reduce wasted efforts.

    Rust''s borrowchecker, while intended to help with memory safety, causes ergonomic
    problems, overstates its role in Rust''s overall safety, and often enforces overly

    # TLDR Information Security 2025-07-21


    # **Attacks & Vulnerabilities**


    [**Ivanti Zero-Days Exploited to Drop MDifyLoader and Launch In-Memory Cobalt
    Strike Attacks (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FBHDHnhy/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/6IdQg-hr3G03D34wy_tKnVaxL3QrB8oO5hlrZRhIGUU=414)


    Threat actors exploited two Ivanti Connect Secure zero-day vulnerabilities (CVE-2025-0282
    and CVE-2025-22457) from December 2024 to July 2025 to deploy MDifyLoader malware
    and launch in-memory Cobalt Strike attacks. They used DLL side-loading, open-source
    tools like VShell and Fscan, then moved laterally via brute-force and EternalBlue.
    Inside networks, they created persistent accounts and registered malware as services
    for long-term access.


    [**Anne Arundel Dermatology data breach impacts 1.9 million people (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fsecurityaffairs.com%2F180100%2Fdata-breach%2Fanne-arundel-dermatology-data-breach-impacts-1-9-million-people.html%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/aitUI3G5pfSwfTBBvjytarodq9We6IMAIngHBwsBzkA=414)


    Anne Arundel Dermatology suffered a data breach affecting 1.9 million people after
    attackers maintained unauthorized access to its systems for three months (February
    14 to May 13). The breach potentially exposed personal and health information
    of patients across the dermatology provider''s 100+ clinics in seven states. No
    ransomware group has claimed responsibility for the attack. The company is providing
    24 months of identity protection services to affected individuals.


    [**1.4 Million Affected by Data Breach at Virginia Radiology Practice (2 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.securityweek.com%2F1-4-million-affected-by-data-breach-at-virginia-radiology-practice%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/FV_PVB14B8zdb7gq9ewa2oGdVOdyl6VCBKz--Fl2eGk=414)


    Radiology Associates of Richmond disclosed a data breach affecting 1.4 million
    individuals after hackers accessed its systems for several days in April 2024.
    The breach, which was discovered over a year after the incident, exposed protected
    health information and personal data.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**Building secure messaging is hard: A nuanced take on the Bitchat security debate
    (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fblog.trailofbits.com%2F2025%2F07%2F18%2Fbuilding-secure-messaging-is-hard-a-nuanced-take-on-the-bitchat-security-debate%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/xVDhCX31ho6ErX--T0ZA34RXoHNhaRn7TOefHatjxR8=414)


    Security researcher Alex Radocea has discovered a man-in-the-middle attack on
    Jack Dorsey''s Bitchat app, exploiting a broken identity verification that allows
    attackers to impersonate contacts. The app also lacks per-message forward secrecy.
    Dorsey responded by open-sourcing code, patching a buffer overflow in four hours,
    and adopting the Noise protocol, demonstrating that security is an ongoing process.
    The security community''s dismissive response discourages open-source and transparent
    security.


    [**NVIDIAScape - Critical NVIDIA AI Vulnerability: A Three-Line Container Escape
    in NVIDIA Container Toolkit (CVE-2025-23266) (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.wiz.io%2Fblog%2Fnvidia-ai-vulnerability-cve-2025-23266-nvidiascape%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/QTOaWrU1hRwO4iLVcjPA2I-TRNbnWoBjbcfoWfOzYq8=414)


    Wiz Research discovered a critical vulnerability (CVE-2025-23266, CVSS 9.0) in
    the NVIDIA Container Toolkit, named NVIDIAScape. Exploitable with a simple three-line
    Dockerfile, it enables container escape, allowing for root access on host machines.
    This poses a threat to managed AI cloud services, allowing attackers to access
    sensitive data and models of other customers on shared infrastructure.


    [**Differentiating Between IoC, IoA, and Indicators of Fraud (11 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdetect.fyi%2Fdifferentiating-between-ioc-iac-and-indicators-of-fraud-bac4b79a974a%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/kg_6I9gRuFznrj86xpcWSTZ4Wtxfu5lxamNg6x9nlVI=414)


    Indicators of Attack (IoA) are signs that a system may be under attack, such as
    the creation of unusual processes or Command and Control (C2) communication. Indicators
    of Compromise (IoCs) are artifacts or forensic signs that a system has been compromised,
    such as disabled security controls, malicious file hashes, or malicious host communication.
    Indicators of Fraud (IoF) are like IoAs but focus on system misuse for financial
    gain, e.g., a credit card used in London then immediately in Tokyo.


    # **Launches & Tools**


    [**New Phobos ransomware decryptor lets victims recover files for free (3 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.bleepingcomputer.com%2Fnews%2Fsecurity%2Fnew-phobos-ransomware-decryptor-lets-victims-recover-files-for-free%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/Lyjx5uUqA5wV5p2n2IPhoWwjdDWDxtzF7nFpqZhl_gk=414)


    Japanese police have released a free decryptor for Phobos and 8-Base ransomware,
    allowing users to recover encrypted files after law enforcement operations seized
    27 servers and disrupted the gangs. The tool supports extensions like ".phobos",
    ".8base", ".elbie", ".faust", and ".LIZARD" and is available via Japanese police,
    Europol''s NoMoreRansom, and the FBI. BleepingComputer confirmed it decrypted
    150 test files, though some browsers may flag it as malware.


    [**Confident Security (Product Launch)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fconfident.security%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/IjygV0StoxBtSS_wYrNNyyb6IdtnjEILHmUtuojxwzE=414)


    Confident Security has its own AI inference technology, called CONFSEC, which
    ensures that user prompts and data remain completely private and secure during
    AI interactions. It utilizes advanced cryptographic techniques such as remote
    attestation and trusted execution environments.


    [**ReARM (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Frelizaio%2Frearm%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/qAAr68K_fc163fLJOKtKUvIx37l_29dlu4SEscVpnoo=414)


    ReARM is an abbreviation for "Reliza''s Artifact and Release Management". It is
    a DevSecOps and Supply Chain Security tool to organize product releases with their
    metadata, including various Bills of Materials (SBOMs/xBOMs).


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Google Sues 25 Chinese Entities Over BADBOX 2.0 Botnet Affecting 10M Android
    Devices (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2Fd3z3wL/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/CZOVl42GlK93qHvYRyI4Z8bx-tGbbNiUy8z8w6ylKNM=414)


    Google sued 25 Chinese entities in New York over the BADBOX 2.0 botnet, which
    infected over 10 million uncertified Android devices via pre-installed malware
    on IoT products like TVs and projectors. The botnet teams, including Infrastructure,
    Backdoor Malware, Evil Twin, and Ad Games, carried out large-scale ad fraud through
    fake apps, hidden browsers, and click scams, earning revenue from Google''s ad
    network. A federal court ordered an immediate shutdown of the botnet and instructed
    ISPs and domain registries to block relevant traffic.


    [**For privacy and security, think twice before granting AI access to your personal
    data (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ftechcrunch.com%2F2025%2F07%2F19%2Ffor-privacy-and-security-think-twice-before-granting-ai-access-to-your-personal-data%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/q9s7K_Kg2Xp6dvUlXXVkfzcILiDcGqslgkzQrhd6ubY=414)


    AI tools increasingly demand excessive access to personal data—contacts, emails,
    calendars, and photos—similar to suspicious apps of the past. Companies like Perplexity
    request broad permissions under the guise of functionality, storing data to improve
    AI models. These privacy risks outweigh the benefits, requiring users to evaluate
    critically whether the convenience justifies surrendering their personal information.


    [**Poor Passwords Tattle on AI Hiring Bot Maker Paradox.ai (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fkrebsonsecurity.com%2F2025%2F07%2Fpoor-passwords-tattle-on-ai-hiring-bot-maker-paradox-ai%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001982d24782c-16638271-e2fa-4c1c-99a9-9a2e1b76bb65-000000/LD3vLPxGxhjnZTZCd1et-sUSrJSY3S6k-3p_wiLazQw=414)


    Security researchers accessed McDonald''s hiring data by guessing Paradox.ai''s
    weak password ("123456"), exposing 64 million applicant records. Additionally,
    a Paradox.ai developer in Vietnam was infected with malware that stole hundreds
    of passwords for Fortune 500 client accounts.

    # TLDR Data 2025-07-24


    # **Deep Dives**


    [**Ray Data, Train & Tune at Klaviyo (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fklaviyo.tech%2Fray-data-train-tune-at-klaviyo-bca9f14abf21%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/pCuY67SC6v80eLRKXC5FGJl1SfN-0Gqv5Hq5bgjokaI=415)


    Klaviyo uses the open-source Ray framework for efficient, scalable machine learning
    workflows, addressing bottlenecks in data preprocessing, training, and hyperparameter
    tuning. Ray Data accelerates preprocessing via parallelism and distributed computation.
    Ray Train simplifies distributed training across GPUs and CPUs. Ray Tune optimizes
    hyperparameters through parallel trials, significantly reducing model development
    time. Together, these components provide Klaviyo with a cost-efficient and scalable
    platform for its machine learning workflows.


    [**3 pandas Workflows That Slowed to a Crawl on Large Datasets—Until We Turned
    on GPUs (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdeveloper.nvidia.com%2Fblog%2F3-pandas-workflows-that-slowed-to-a-crawl-on-large-datasets-until-we-turned-on-gpus%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/4SxnCnt-_lt2lz7424T1L3IuNcAPdHRgkuO2O8aXqh0=415)


    GPU acceleration significantly enhances the performance of common pandas workflows
    on large datasets, enabling operations that traditionally slow down to execute
    up to 30x faster. Key use cases include analyzing time-series stock data, processing
    text-heavy job postings, and building responsive interactive dashboards, all of
    which benefit from NVIDIA cuDF without requiring code rewrites. Additionally,
    Unified Virtual Memory allows processing of datasets exceeding GPU memory limits,
    facilitating the management of large DataFrames. This deep dive contains additional
    videos and code examples.


    [**Context Engineering: 2025''s #1 Skill in AI (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdecodingml.substack.com%2Fp%2Fcontext-engineering-2025s-1-skill%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/RIDnna-Qb-MZRq8MY1SIoAfITAdZLHdcBFi_Y7l4l10=415)


    Context engineering has emerged as the critical discipline for maximizing LLM
    performance, moving beyond static prompt engineering to architecting dynamic,
    task-specific context pipelines. Key strategies such as selective RAG retrieval,
    context compression, structured outputs, and multi-agent separation address context
    window limits, reduce hallucinations, and optimize cost and latency.


    # **Opinions & Advice**


    [**Why Startups Are Betting Everything on Apache DataFusion (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fthenewstack.io%2Fwhy-startups-are-betting-everything-on-apache-datafusion%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/7nyp0Ens0O4-mFaCuYlUT59Zcolkzn4VTiVNxSbzKTM=415)


    Apache DataFusion is emerging as a crucial open-source library for building high-performance
    analytic systems. It''s being adopted by startups, established companies, and
    open-source projects to create innovative data solutions, offering the performance
    of expensive proprietary systems with a lower barrier to entry and the benefits
    of community-driven development.


    [**Atlassian Research: AI Adoption is Rising, But Friction Persists (5 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.atlassian.com%2Fblog%2Fdeveloper%2Fdeveloper-experience-report-2025%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/mi3WHEQloONjXtwHzWORoJ37CpZI4xeWYhRefT5qBro=415)


    According to Atlassian''s recent survey, 68 percent of developers report saving
    over 10 hours weekly from AI tools, primarily in non-coding tasks. On the flip
    side, the top time-wasters for developers are finding information (services, docs,
    and APIs), adapting new technology, and context switching between tools. These
    are areas where AI can potentially improve developer experience.


    [**Why Good Data Doesn''t Guarantee Good Decisions (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.datasciencecentral.com%2Fwhy-good-data-doesnt-guarantee-good-decisions%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/zDOJC7bs8wf4yKotQLOIj0Y79yrPY9k71p15_wn_72A=415)


    Data professionals need to focus on making insights actionable, not just generating
    them. This involves framing forecasts around decisions, providing context in dashboards,
    considering multiple interpretations of data, and ultimately acting as strategic
    enablers who design their work to facilitate better decision-making rather than
    simply providing raw data.


    [**SQL Injection as a Feature (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fidiallo.com%2Fblog%2Fsql-injection-as-a-feature%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/aV8ICHyw-dRUSzdAsMn0AGJdzZlbQE6AyJ9c3hTjWIo=415)


    An application initially designed with a structured report generation feature
    devolved into a SQL Injection As A Service model, allowing users to directly input
    SQL queries due to incremental feature requests over a decade. This evolution
    highlights the risks of insufficient input validation and the need for robust
    database security practices, as user demands led to exposing the entire database.


    # **Launches & Tools**


    [**Vibe Coding a Data Transformation using MCPs (16 minute video)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv=AK2qm-4SazE%26utm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/lLopJ4PinOflvoIC6ZF9JuWGeatFYEWYGYF9oXFvyQk=415)


    A data engineer shows how they used LLMs to go from data model design to a working
    pipeline using real business data, Keboola, and chat interfaces. The workflow
    sped up development and task creation, but the engineer highlights the need for
    manual validation to build trust in the outputs.


    [**Accelerating Development with the AWS Data Processing MCP Server and Agent
    (12 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Faws.amazon.com%2Fblogs%2Fbig-data%2Faccelerating-development-with-the-aws-data-processing-mcp-server-and-agent%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/6gfVkntBfnAeiqSr7DoXaXuIc7wPD7F5KBvSII-B_pM=415)


    The AWS Data Processing MCP Server is a new open-source tool that simplifies the
    setup and management of analytics environments on AWS. It uses the MCP to enable
    AI assistants to understand and interact with various AWS data processing services,
    including AWS Glue, Amazon EMR, and Amazon Athena, through natural language interactions.


    [**Code Sandbox MCP: A Simple Code Interpreter for Your AI Agents (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.philschmid.de%2Fcode-sandbox-mcp%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/m_mdy2Ub_fr9cg7mlasLQ9JaI8dmUUHfEZ5CJ3CZX1o=415)


    Code Sandbox MCP is a newly launched lightweight server that enables AI assistants
    and LLM applications to safely execute Python and JavaScript code snippets in
    containerized environments. It uses the llm-sandbox package for containerization
    and provides a secure way for AI agents to run code on your infrastructure.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**The Rise of the AI Database: Powering Real-Time AI Applications (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.singlestore.com%2Fblog%2Fthe-rise-of-the-ai-database-powering-real-time-ai-applications%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/8MDXynuj8nmBiv_4BQwlS4TYVXXkb7mHRm9_yRcEtOs=415)


    Generative AI databases combine relational data management, vector search, and
    full-text indexing in a single platform, supporting real-time AI and analytic
    workloads. This unified architecture streamlines the development of AI services
    like chatbots, recommendation engines, and fraud detection systems.


    [**Agent Infrastructure and Control Planes (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.datagravity.dev%2Fp%2Fagent-infrastructure-and-control%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001983bebb50d-beaa4710-7a27-491b-a326-97e19854c6b2-000000/plWu8Lx_hdf48RaFpidjY68NosIcwMel2Y_LVPxaXxM=415)


    As LLM inference matures and costs drop, enterprise focus is shifting to agent
    orchestration, memory, durability, and governance, requiring a whole new infrastructure
    stack. Critical areas include composable agent frameworks (e.g., LangChain), stochastic
    workflow orchestrators, robust agent memory layers, UI automation via headless
    browser protocols, and agent-native security/auth. No single vendor owns this
    space yet, and the battle for dominance has begun.

    # TLDR Founders 2025-07-21


    # **Headlines & Trends**


    [**The HALO Effect (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fkwokchain.com%2F2025%2F07%2F15%2Fthe-halo-effect%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001982cee44d9-34bac4b3-82a7-478e-a051-b19c54d33bfe-000000/qGQBPXa8kcqUphSN4cKgcjDWGojZGyGrb6fh3VOPzEA=414)


    Google paid \$2.4B to "hire" Windsurf''s team while the startup somehow keeps
    operating. These aren''t acquisitions - companies hire the founders and license
    the IP while the startup continues under new leadership. Kevin Kwok calls them
    HALOs (Hire And License Out). Antitrust killed normal acquisitions, but that''s
    not the real story. In AI, value isn''t in products that go obsolete yearly -
    it''s in teams who know how to ship at the frontier. Google doesn''t want Windsurf''s
    \$80M revenue. It wants people who can transform models into products. HALOs close
    in days because they''re honest about what matters - the people.


    [**AI Agents Are Creating a New Security Nightmare for Enterprises and Startups
    (10 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fthenewstack.io%2Fai-agents-are-creating-a-new-security-nightmare-for-enterprises-and-startups%2F%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001982cee44d9-34bac4b3-82a7-478e-a051-b19c54d33bfe-000000/PFgtFxlhb5EcxHJyZD8YTZRb_x9q4aF2ufr4wF9G0y8=414)


    AI agents are creating security challenges with unchecked outbound API traffic,
    introducing complex risks in visibility, security, and cost management. The emergence
    of protocols like Anthropic''s MCP and Google''s A2A increases the risk of data
    breaches due to excessive permissions given to AI agents. AI gateways can regulate
    these risks by enforcing security measures, providing oversight, and enhancing
    observability in agentic traffic.


    [**The Sales Strategy Conquering the AI Market (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ftomtunguz.com%2Ffde-cs%2F%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001982cee44d9-34bac4b3-82a7-478e-a051-b19c54d33bfe-000000/W9d5XUYycsUmFuNB5KcNhMydGstT82omixasJJ3w0M4=414)


    AI''s rapid evolution has disrupted traditional software sales strategies, making
    forward-deployed engineers (FDEs) crucial for success. FDEs work with clients
    to customize AI solutions, prioritizing outcomes over simply selling products.
    This approach, first modeled by Palantir, is essential for enterprise contracts
    over \$100k due to high staffing costs.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**Writing Content That Ranks with LLMs (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.dearstage2.com%2Fp%2Fwriting-content-that-ranks-with-llms%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001982cee44d9-34bac4b3-82a7-478e-a051-b19c54d33bfe-000000/TU1QK_vBu4GqF_2xyouIzl7pI5WruGQuZayrIBHcFVk=414)


    Buyers stopped Googling and started asking ChatGPT - now those AI-sourced leads
    convert way better than traditional search traffic. One Head of GTM noticed this
    shift and rebuilt his entire content process. Instead of chasing keywords, he
    mines sales calls for actual buyer questions, then feeds competitor content into
    Claude to spot patterns everyone else misses. The secret to ranking with LLMs?
    Format everything like an AI would think. Clear question as your H1, logical follow-ups
    as H2s, supporting proof as H3s. LLMs don''t scan for keywords - they parse structure
    and intent.


    [**Never Make the Same Mistake Twice (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fbenmeer.com%2Fnewsletter%2Fafter-action-review%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001982cee44d9-34bac4b3-82a7-478e-a051-b19c54d33bfe-000000/LPmW1uvqV23V3T07ekw4aQHuz-sKX6V0ZUjWm5slxmY=414)


    The U.S. Armed Forces and Fortune 500 companies use After-Action Reviews to learn
    from every win and loss. Four simple questions turn mistakes into growth: What
    did I intend? What happened? Why did it happen? What will I do differently?


    [**Why Startup Founders Struggle With Adaptability (And How To Overcome The Challenge)
    (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fnews.crunchbase.com%2Fstartups%2Fovercoming-founder-struggles-hagberg-tzuo-zuora%2F%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001982cee44d9-34bac4b3-82a7-478e-a051-b19c54d33bfe-000000/IF2oHlbyntUpOC2lDx3jImxf_fm6t3sWxr79sHuOnl0=414)


    Startup founders struggle with adaptability due to their inherent rigidity, preference
    for past successes, and discomfort with uncertainty. Their leadership style often
    involves dictatorial decision-making and resistance to feedback, stifling innovation.
    To improve, founders should focus on listening, delegating tasks, and embracing
    ambiguity to enhance personal and business growth.

    [**Zapier MCP 2.0 (Tool)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fzapier.com%2Fmcp%2F%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001982cee44d9-34bac4b3-82a7-478e-a051-b19c54d33bfe-000000/FJPHK_K4sD6SqcJjP0GQY6g0r7Cdlm4NrddRldFOSIY=414)

    remio is a local-first AI note-taking tool that helps users collect, organize,

    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**The Return of the Point Solution (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fcloudedjudgement.substack.com%2Fp%2Fclouded-judgement-71825-the-return%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001982cee44d9-34bac4b3-82a7-478e-a051-b19c54d33bfe-000000/xcGgC9ThKHopexJeBmCora9JtqPyp5buKBjTLGRJGTo=414)


    The next trillion-dollar platforms are hiding as point solutions growing faster
    than anything from the SaaS era. Datadog started tiny when New Relic owned the
    market. Now Datadog''s bigger than everyone who tried to kill it. AI accelerates
    this - Claude Code threatens entire categories overnight, yet survivors will dwarf
    cloud giants. We''re 3 years post-ChatGPT, right where cloud was in 2010 before
    the boom.


    [**SaaS vs AI-Native Software (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fthesaasbarometer.substack.com%2Fp%2Fsaas-vs-ai-native-software%3Futm_source=tldrfounders/1/010001982cee44d9-34bac4b3-82a7-478e-a051-b19c54d33bfe-000000/kDO-PRCRD3J0LqwUpWrUrt9TvR4wzudFXumedpPcQpE=414)


    Everyone claims to be AI-powered, but there''s a huge difference between SaaS
    with AI sprinkled on top and true AI-native software. The test is simple - does
    the product still work if you remove the AI? Salesforce works fine without AI
    features. Jasper dies instantly. The modern software stack now has five layers:
    cloud platforms (AWS), infrastructure (MongoDB), LLM providers (OpenAI), traditional
    SaaS (Zoom), and AI-native apps (Perplexity). AI compute demand will grow 1,000x
    this decade. The infrastructure giants - cloud and LLM providers - are the new
    kings because they power everything else.


    [**How YouTube Won the Battle for TV Viewers (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2F1ERyl9/1/010001982cee44d9-34bac4b3-82a7-478e-a051-b19c54d33bfe-000000/ezoO0iMzEHaFU8adQlEHCQuEhI0bSz53U0xhUx96nQg=414)


    YouTube now gets more TV viewing than Disney''s entire empire - broadcast network,
    a dozen cable channels, and three streaming services combined. People watch over
    a billion hours daily on TVs, not phones. Creators noticed and adapted - "Good
    Mythical Morning" hosts employ 100 people and make hour-long episodes now. Netflix
    analysts suggest spending \$500M to poach top YouTubers, but creators say no check
    is big enough to abandon channels they spent years building.

    # TLDR Design 2025-07-22


    # **News & Trends**


    [**Figma introduces the new glass effect and Apple''s liquid glass UI Kit (2 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fux-news.com%2Ffigma-introduces-the-new-glass-effect-and-apples-liquid-glass-ui-kit%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/01000198320e9372-6447a883-5b53-4547-81ae-091f66939b8a-000000/kc-_dmn_TjkDdoq5fab2rBrD6ovnVs9PJDwJ6KwMsMg=415)


    Figma has launched a new visual effect called Glass. Currently in beta, it enables
    designers to create translucent, glass-like UI elements with realistic depth,
    refraction, and customizable parameters like light, blur, and dispersion. The
    effect is limited to one instance per frame and not compatible with certain layer
    settings or exports. It integrates with Apple''s new Liquid Glass UI in iOS 26
    and is supported by an official Figma UI kit and a playground file for experimentation.


    [**DuckDuckGo Now Lets You Hide AI-generated Images in Search Results (1 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ftechcrunch.com%2F2025%2F07%2F18%2Fduckduckgo-now-lets-you-hide-ai-generated-images-in-search-results%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/01000198320e9372-6447a883-5b53-4547-81ae-091f66939b8a-000000/u0eMhNRVCfNYRNx99tVIeWssWxZNVuWHCXeiZtWt0us=415)


    Responding to user feedback about AI content hindering their search results, DuckDuckGo
    introduced a new setting that allows users to filter out AI-generated images from
    search results. The feature utilizes manually curated open-source blocklists and
    can be accessed through the Images tab or search settings, although it may not
    catch all AI-generated content. This comes amid growing concerns about "AI slop"
    flooding the internet with low-quality generative AI content.


    [**Take note, this is how you modernise a 500-year-old brand (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.creativebloq.com%2Fdesign%2Fbranding%2Ftake-note-this-is-how-you-modernise-a-500-year-old-brand%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/01000198320e9372-6447a883-5b53-4547-81ae-091f66939b8a-000000/BW-B_5IGWmm39B717Hh0tDvqSXRdgyPrvT3x6JAzvAM=415)


    The rebrand of St John''s College, Cambridge, masterfully balances historical
    heritage with contemporary design through refined updates like a polished crest,
    bespoke monogram, and modern typography, creating a timeless yet flexible identity.
    Developed by agency SomeOne, the rebrand draws from the college''s archives and
    architecture, using minimal colors, cinematic visuals, and dynamic layouts to
    project authority, warmth, and relevance for a modern audience.


    # **Opinions & Tutorials**


    [**Should Designers Train Models? (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fcarly.substack.com%2Fp%2Fshould-designers-train-models%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/01000198320e9372-6447a883-5b53-4547-81ae-091f66939b8a-000000/PYkP_m38SPTR_7IFSclO99FankIZOz8IqEUKyLeQp7U=415)


    Designers need to understand AI model training not to become engineers, but to
    design better consumer products that embed AI responsibly. AI functions as a design
    material with real constraints, requiring interfaces that reveal uncertainty and
    limitations rather than hiding them behind misleading chatbot metaphors. That
    approach emphasizes building tools deliberately for longevity over chasing trends,
    focusing on AI''s genuine strengths in pattern recognition while avoiding misapplication
    to problems requiring precision and context.


    [**The best start-ups are built on brand, so designers should have a stake (4
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.designweek.co.uk%2Fthe-best-start-ups-are-built-on-brand-designers-should-have-a-stake%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/01000198320e9372-6447a883-5b53-4547-81ae-091f66939b8a-000000/BJ22P2DwGz7R8aPEdmmIaKzhrXJ3yY0D9qFHDb3Kb18=415)


    In early-stage ventures, creative clarity and distinct brand perspective are often
    the true differentiators that shape a company''s trajectory long before launch,
    yet the creatives driving this value rarely share in the upside. Anders Frostenson
    argues this imbalance is both a fairness and business model problem, calling for
    a shift where brand is treated not as polish but as strategic infrastructure,
    with creatives earning equity alongside their impact.


    [**AI might be the best thing to happen to design communication (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fuxdesign.cc%2Fai-might-be-the-best-thing-to-happen-to-design-communication-61797a00c32e%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/01000198320e9372-6447a883-5b53-4547-81ae-091f66939b8a-000000/m7DieF1cajehm_LvQg-dxNGwLG9aTNTOGAsT25muNUw=415)


    The rise of AI tools like ChatGPT is pushing designers to move beyond instinct
    and articulate their creative decisions with clarity, turning intuition into structured
    language. While initially seen as a threat, AI is ironically helping designers
    strengthen verbal communication—a skill long undervalued in design—enabling them
    to better explain, defend, and scale their work across disciplines.

    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**AI Compliance: A Core Product Competency You Shouldn''t Skip (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fblog.logrocket.com%2Fproduct-management%2Fai-compliance-core-product-competency-you-shouldnt-skip%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/01000198320e9372-6447a883-5b53-4547-81ae-091f66939b8a-000000/0_ZbdMQfdUA3CNumckPGwLroPM82nSZBPsOfssLEcEU=415)


    AI regulation has evolved from a legal afterthought into a core product competency.
    The EU AI Act establishes tier-based obligations that will phase in from February
    2025 through August 2027. Product managers must now integrate compliance into
    sprints through risk-tier assessments, bias audits, and transparency features
    while treating these requirements as competitive differentiators rather than friction.
    Teams that incorporate governance into their development process from the outset
    will iterate more efficiently and establish lasting user trust in regulated markets.


    [**Why Your Product Feels Boring and How Gamification Can Fix It (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fuxplanet.org%2Fwhy-your-product-feels-boring-and-how-gamification-can-fix-it-635b2028090e%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/01000198320e9372-6447a883-5b53-4547-81ae-091f66939b8a-000000/TrpYcrgRQ3Jg-nNVy1bCcFeEUPfdDWavPt-v5Bq6mQg=415)


    Product designers face intense competition in today''s AI-accelerated development
    landscape, where user retention is more important than initial acquisition. Gamification
    strategies, such as daily challenges, streaks, monthly contests, leaderboards,
    and achievement systems, can transform boring products by building habits and
    maintaining engagement without feeling forced. The key lies in selecting appropriate
    elements that match user journeys and business goals, starting small with one
    or two features before expanding based on tracked impact.

    # TLDR Design 2025-07-23


    # **News & Trends**


    [**Figma''s Dylan Field will cash out about \$60M in IPO, with Index, Kleiner,
    Greylock, Sequoia all selling, too (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ftechcrunch.com%2F2025%2F07%2F21%2Ffigmas-dylan-field-will-cash-out-about-60m-in-ipo-with-index-kleiner-greylock-sequoia-all-selling-too%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/0100019837373873-e211cf05-c2ef-42d0-82a8-5ff89ceb60c6-000000/z26dDF7WanivK8ELT8oga-uisIXmCVcLmUPjLH8QjHU=415)


    Figma''s IPO is unusual in that existing shareholders will sell nearly twice as
    many shares as the company itself. Founder Dylan Field alone is set to cash out
    over \$62 million while still retaining 74% voting control thanks to supervoting
    shares. Major investors like Sequoia and Greylock are also selling significant
    portions, signaling strong expected demand. If the offering prices above the \$25–\$28
    range, it could become 2025''s largest IPO to date.

    The iPhone 17 is set to introduce Apple''s most dramatic design overhaul in years,
    featuring a new model, the iPhone 17 Air, a redesigned camera for the Pro version,
    and a striking, light-reactive color inspired by iOS 26''s "Liquid Glass" aesthetic.
    This iridescent finish marks a bold shift from Apple''s traditionally conservative
    color choices, signaling a renewed push to "Think Different" amid recent criticisms.

    [**We asked creatives how they look after themselves. Here''s what they said (8
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.creativeboom.com%2Ftips%2Fwe-asked-creatives-how-they-look-after-themselves-heres-what-they-said%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/0100019837373873-e211cf05-c2ef-42d0-82a8-5ff89ceb60c6-000000/CYL_5wNUohjfkpYDb9CVdxdbbEwWvzH5gqNLO6ZfyL4=415)


    Creatives are finding it increasingly difficult to maintain well-being in the
    high-pressure 2020s, but many are turning to nature, movement, sleep, creative
    play, and intentional downtime to avoid burnout. Ahead of International Self-Care
    Day, artists and designers shared personal strategies—from setting boundaries
    to prioritizing fun and connection—reminding us that self-care isn''t a luxury,
    but a vital part of sustaining a healthy creative life.


    [**Why UX Designers Should Care About Model Context Protocol (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fuxdesign.cc%2Fwhy-ux-designers-should-care-about-model-context-protocol-24d34b02c1c9%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/0100019837373873-e211cf05-c2ef-42d0-82a8-5ff89ceb60c6-000000/f-bAWzTU0syRMHvf9LpcSu1IUCM84KHpBMp98hjsAe0=415)


    The Model Context Protocol (MCP) enables AI systems to communicate with external
    tools and data sources, allowing users to accomplish complex tasks across multiple
    applications through a single conversation, rather than manually switching between
    isolated apps. UX designers must evolve from designing individual applications
    to creating intelligent workflows where AI orchestrates tasks across connected
    systems, requiring new design patterns like conductor interfaces and intent-based
    navigation. This shift represents a fundamental change in digital experience design,
    offering designers who understand MCP-enabled workflows significant career advantages
    as the industry moves toward more connected, AI-powered user experiences.


    [**The Death of Accountability: Why No One Owns Their Mistakes Anymore (5 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fuxplaybook.org%2Farticles%2Fwhy-teams-fail-accountability-responsibility-guide%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/0100019837373873-e211cf05-c2ef-42d0-82a8-5ff89ceb60c6-000000/vWz2mloRFYMmEe7S2-jYKflpFce6VWb7hRQL9LoiLio=415)


    Modern workplaces suffer from an accountability crisis where leaders and team
    members dodge responsibility, blame others, and prioritize self-preservation over
    honesty. This culture creates toxic environments where quality people clean up
    others'' mistakes while finger-pointers get promoted, leading to decreased project
    quality, eroded trust, and organizational dysfunction. Building accountability
    requires leaders to model ownership of mistakes, establish clear responsibilities,
    document decisions, and reward honesty while actively discouraging blame-shifting
    behaviors.

    # TLDR Information Security 2025-07-24


    # **Attacks & Vulnerabilities**


    [**Major European Healthcare Network Discloses Security Breach (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.bleepingcomputer.com%2Fnews%2Fsecurity%2Fmajor-european-healthcare-network-discloses-security-breach%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983c96e553-06932fdb-48ea-4d7b-b021-cc663ec763c2-000000/8vylD-53gEPNHNG6YyKCQIwKKJFAJi143TTYDixflBU=415)


    AMEOS Group, an operator of a Central European healthcare network, suffered a
    security breach that may have exposed customer, employee, and partner information.
    In response to the breach, AMEOS has shut down all IT systems and terminated all
    external and internal network connections while it responds to the incident. AMEOS
    has stated that it doesn''t currently have evidence of any data being leaked,
    but it is continuing to investigate.


    [**3.5M Records Exposed in Australian Global Fashion Brand Data Breach (4 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.vpnmentor.com%2Fnews%2Freport-sabo-breach%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983c96e553-06932fdb-48ea-4d7b-b021-cc663ec763c2-000000/ANrof9K3H_s3bRaH2RapIySR_ZIcZJddYoUmWauEySw=415)


    Jeremiah Fowler discovered an unprotected, unencrypted, and publicly exposed database
    containing over 3.5 million PDFs belonging to the Australian fashion brand SABO.
    The files contain PII, including names, physical addresses, email addresses, phone
    numbers, and other personal information corresponding to retail and corporate
    customers. Some of the PDFs contain multiple orders, suggesting that the number
    of affected individuals may be higher than 3.5 million.


    [**US nuclear weapons agency reportedly breached in Microsoft SharePoint attacks
    (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.theverge.com%2Fnews%2F712080%2Fmicrosoft-sharepoint-hack-us-nuclear-weapons-agency%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983c96e553-06932fdb-48ea-4d7b-b021-cc663ec763c2-000000/iEPmFbpdbUBCNp8NlA3_OMsnXVvAxZW_IP9DdaCRGmY=415)


    Chinese government-affiliated hackers exploited a Microsoft SharePoint vulnerability
    affecting 50+ organizations, including the National Nuclear Security Administration.
    The zero-day flaw enables remote access to on-premises SharePoint versions, allowing
    attackers to steal documents and sensitive information.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**Mythic C2 with EarlyBird Injection and Defender Evasion (10 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fxbz0n.sh%2Fblog%2Fmythic-c2-early-bird-defender-evasion%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983c96e553-06932fdb-48ea-4d7b-b021-cc663ec763c2-000000/w3IbV1YVZE95AMJRDzvwVpDaOLhFcaaGYHzgR4Lz4O8=415)


    This post walks through a demo setup of the Mythic C2 framework that uses redirectors
    to disguise itself as legitimate WordPress traffic. The redirectors use a legitimately
    registered domain and certificates and use Nginx to offer WordPress as a front
    end, as well as an api subdomain that forwards traffic to the C2 server and a
    dl subdomain that disguises payloads as font files. The setup also utilizes the
    EarlyBird Injection technique, where the loader executes code before the target
    process is fully initialized, both in its loader and through string obfuscation
    to employ evasion during installation. The post concludes with a discussion of
    further enhancements, such as ensuring domain age before weaponizing it and detection
    mechanisms for this setup.


    [**What to know about ToolShell, the SharePoint threat under mass exploitation
    (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Farstechnica.com%2Fsecurity%2F2025%2F07%2Fwhat-to-know-about-toolshell-the-sharepoint-threat-under-mass-exploitation%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983c96e553-06932fdb-48ea-4d7b-b021-cc663ec763c2-000000/1V4Q8d2PwbLJH-NDrxT2dc80mZLaQFLrs9woezLmkO8=415)


    A critical SharePoint vulnerability (CVE-2025-53770), dubbed "ToolShell," is being
    mass-exploited by Chinese government groups, affecting over 400 systems, including
    the US National Nuclear Security Administration. The flaw allows unauthenticated
    remote code execution, credential theft, and data exfiltration. Microsoft patched
    it on Saturday, but it is being exploited on any company that has not updated
    their SharePoint.


    [**Choosing the VPN That''s Right for You (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fssd.eff.org%2Fmodule%2Fchoosing-vpn-thats-right-you%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983c96e553-06932fdb-48ea-4d7b-b021-cc663ec763c2-000000/__4fRDAhLZJRwKMviSI9zPBbSt8q20RPDOW-mxUtKFw=415)


    VPNs mainly serve two purposes: bypassing internet censorship and remote access
    to corporate networks, despite being marketed as security tools. They hide your
    IP and encrypt traffic, but don''t ensure anonymity (Tor is better), don''t fully
    secure public Wi-Fi (most traffic is HTTPS), and shift data from your ISP to the
    VPN provider. When choosing one, review the provider''s business model, data practices,
    encryption protocols (prefer OpenVPN or WireGuard), and verify claims through
    third-party audits.


    # **Launches & Tools**


    [**golem (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2F20urc3%2Fgolem%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983c96e553-06932fdb-48ea-4d7b-b021-cc663ec763c2-000000/Wm3g1tMKhAHPhMttGaA9_mIqxX1_sKKpBLLQn_GWeao=415)


    golem automates C/C++ vulnerability scans by combining Semgrep rule scans, LLVM
    call-graph and CFG slicing, and AI-driven context analysis to flag potential security
    issues, generate graph artifacts, and produce a detailed, prioritized audit report.


    [**Faraday (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Finfobyte%2Ffaraday%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983c96e553-06932fdb-48ea-4d7b-b021-cc663ec763c2-000000/PWSJEKU98Kfpynfm_bLlKZH22VgL3LFcN34D-CiAjko=415)


    Faraday is an open-source vulnerability management platform designed to centralize
    vulnerability data and automate scanners.


    [**Lumo AI (Product Launch)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fproton.me%2Fblog%2Flumo-ai%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983c96e553-06932fdb-48ea-4d7b-b021-cc663ec763c2-000000/HA7ah_9K2COu3vhXxyzefee-O_nT4M9_OHR5RjWxsLs=415)


    Proton''s Lumo AI uses open-source models, zero-access encryption, and doesn''t
    train on user data, emphasizing privacy-focused development.

    The UK government proposes banning public sector organizations (NHS, councils,
    and schools) and critical infrastructure from paying ransomware criminals, aiming
    to make them less attractive targets. The Cyber Resilience Bill will impose daily
    fines of £100,000 for security failures. Private companies must still report their
    intentions to pay ransoms to authorities.

    China has launched a voluntary national online ID service aimed at centralizing
    citizen identity verification and reducing the collection of private company data.
    While officials claim it enhances privacy, critics argue that it strengthens government
    surveillance capabilities, as authorities can revoke digital certificates and
    effectively erase users'' entire online presence.

    # TLDR Web Dev 2025-07-25


    # **Articles & Tutorials**


    [**Policy Zones: How Meta enforces purpose limitation at scale in batch processing
    systems (22 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fengineering.fb.com%2F2025%2F07%2F23%2Fsecurity%2Fpolicy-zones-meta-purpose-limitation-batch-processing-systems%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/5yZXBRd3JQz28_XJsRZeQnoZFCvUyPl74NHZRKNlW_0=415)


    Meta developed Privacy Aware Infrastructure (PAI) and Policy Zones to enforce
    purpose limitations on data in large-scale batch processing systems. Policy Zones
    uses runtime enforcement and SQL parsing to track and control data flow across
    Meta''s data warehouse, integrating with millions of data flows daily and performing
    trillions of user consent checks per hour. Meta provides tools like Policy Zones
    Manager (PZM) to help engineers use Policy Zones.


    [**Cursor makes developers less effective? (11 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fblog.pragmaticengineer.com%2Fcursor-makes-developers-less-effective%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/MIjrmQOvPUM8_FYaouIyQ0EGhoVnsgNICWoMjODpTqI=415)


    A study by METR found that developers using AI tools like Cursor took 19% longer
    to complete tasks, despite expecting a 24% speedup. This slowdown was attributed
    to increased time spent on promoting, waiting for the AI, reviewing its output,
    and IDE overhead, negating time saved on coding, research, and testing. However,
    the study showed that the learning curve for AI development tools is steep, with
    more experienced users potentially seeing productivity gains.


    [**React Router and React Server Components: The Path Forward (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fremix.run%2Fblog%2Freact-router-and-react-server-components%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/4UwxQEdc9qjsY9GBIV8Hn206PKPiMLffefeY5Ueh6II=415)


    React Router is evolving to use React Server Components (RSC) for better data
    handling, streaming UI, and code splitting. The integration of RSC makes React
    Router''s architecture easier to use and understand.


    # **Opinions & Advice**


    [**How Anthropic teams use Claude Code (27 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.anthropic.com%2Fnews%2Fhow-anthropic-teams-use-claude-code%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/X6M6RNoJ1hQIuD4C1q65vdsd-465dO8Gbk_mebUI9Gg=415)


    Anthropic''s internal teams are using Claude Code to transform workflows, automate
    tasks, and bridge skill gaps, boosting productivity across various departments.
    The teams use Claude Code for tasks like debugging infrastructure, rapid prototyping,
    generating tests, synthesizing documentation, and even building complex applications
    in unfamiliar languages. This leads to faster feature implementation, improved
    code quality, better cross-functional collaboration, and lots of time savings
    across teams.


    [**Use Your Type System (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.dzombak.com%2Fblog%2F2025%2F07%2Fuse-your-type-system%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/N1IPLMnA16DJwKjBHVazfH8EwyM_BETtWLYCawqbQ6s=415)


    Use distinct types for simple values like IDs, integers, and strings to prevent
    bugs caused by type mixing in code. This is shown with examples from a weather
    calculation library (libwx) written in Go, where custom types for temperature
    units prevent accidental misuse. Using the type system in this way reduces errors
    and improves code clarity.


    [**Code review is part of your job (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FjQPWyZ/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/hfZl4Yyhjt2uqvisRVJhzY5G9pkPIC8rRhbLayc1leA=415)


    Code review is an essential part of a developer''s job and being a good teammate.
    Neglecting code reviews burdens teammates and slows down the team''s overall progress.


    # **Launches & Tools**


    [**Positron (Website)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fpositron.posit.co%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/7kOLAb_dkfJaUbZYT2MOclTX0ZghWlVEf7COFtJubco=415)


    Positron is a free, next-generation data science IDE. It''s an extensible and
    polyglot tool designed for coding, data exploration, and reproducible authoring.


    [**Nia (Website)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.trynia.ai%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/bE_KkOmSXSWXmPN0Zbn9EJvwZvwiOvR29kHiH4JOxdk=415)


    Nia is an MCP server that helps provide additional context to coding agents. It
    indexes lots of documentation and codebases, improving agent understanding and
    capabilities by up to 27%, as seen with Cursor. Nia integrates with any IDE via
    MCP, offers usage tracking and billing, and is accessible through API, CLI, and
    AI code editors.


    [**Reagraph (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Freaviz%2Freagraph%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/qRKMqI558Bcfye_KiOX3ztAceYDChavj91zT8P8aQc4=415)


    Reagraph is a high-performance React library for visualizing network graphs using
    WebGL. It has features like node sizing, light/dark themes, pathfinding, various
    layouts, and customizable styling.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**React Server Components: How We Got Here (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.epicreact.dev%2Freact-server-components-how-we-got-here-zcuxn%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/Hxh5Ui-ZoOs7WcEGnTibyTJEimYO1m1gS8lVjRDcozY=415)


    In the context of web dev, Multi-Page Applications provide simplicity but have
    a poor user experience, while Single-Page Applications (SPAs) improve UX but introduce
    network management complexity and lost progressive enhancement. Frameworks like
    Remix attempt to restore progressive enhancement to SPAs, but still have compositional
    limitations. React Server Components are a big leap because they restore component-based
    composition, remove custom network management code, and combine the best features
    of previous approaches for simpler, more performant web apps.


    [**Surprising no one, new research says AI Overviews cause massive drop in search
    clicks (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Farstechnica.com%2Fai%2F2025%2F07%2Fresearch-shows-google-ai-overviews-reduce-website-clicks-by-almost-half%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/T6tx50Lk0v6AozGAvMP57ecoJZV1t7RHYGxlWCmlxwQ=415)


    A new Pew Research Center study revealed that Google''s AI Overviews reduced clicks
    to websites from search results pages. The study found that click-through rates
    dropped by nearly half when AI Overviews were present, with only 1% of overviews
    leading to clicks on the sources cited. Additionally, users are more likely to
    end their browsing session after viewing an AI Overview.


    [**Intel CEO Letter to Employees (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmorethanmoore.substack.com%2Fp%2Fintel-ceo-letter-to-employees%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/Qnlnyi8g4ZW4H2oq9OY8SBUDAk-Zanrez1mhC-d084k=415)


    In a letter to employees, Intel CEO Lip-Bu Tan announced Q2 2025 revenue exceeding
    expectations, but also big cost-cutting measures. These measures include a 15%
    workforce reduction, streamlining management, halting foundry projects in Germany
    and Poland, and consolidating assembly/test operations. Intel will refocus its
    foundry strategy on customer-driven demand, revitalizing the x86 ecosystem, and
    refine its AI strategy towards inference and agentic AI.

    [**PSA: SQLite WAL checksums fail silently and may lose data (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Favi.im%2Fblag%2F2025%2Fsqlite-wal-checksum%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/s7TKwN78oX-kqUqwffrZxSjSodwUhWFmWMQ4Ksd-xpQ=415)


    SQLite''s Write-Ahead Logging (WAL) mode, while offering checksums, silently drops
    valid data frames following a detected checksum error during index rebuilds after
    unclean shutdowns, potentially leading to data loss without any error notification.


    [**There is no memory safety without thread safety (10 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.ralfj.de%2Fblog%2F2025%2F07%2F24%2Fmemory-safety.html%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/010001984156f646-c5bbd698-13b6-4aea-9988-2cd458506693-000000/gZuB-Q5HOsgBs2OwdTK_GSSRYt5YxXaSorOkyX6XSlw=415)


    Memory safety is often conflated with thread safety - the real property devs should
    focus on is the absence of Undefined Behavior.

    OpenAI CEO Sam Altman predicts programmer salaries will skyrocket despite AI due

    # TLDR Data 2025-07-21


    # **Deep Dives**


    [**Debugging the One-in-a-Million Failure: Migrating Pinterest''s Search Infrastructure
    to Kubernetes (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmedium.com%2Fpinterest-engineering%2Fdebugging-the-one-in-a-million-failure-migrating-pinterests-search-infrastructure-to-kubernetes-bef9af9dabf4%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/xGtd5yYRHLvdrJYl5HRLWuPyFNRHqronwD4LqBxiIZA=414)


    Pinterest''s migration of its search infrastructure to Kubernetes revealed a rare
    issue where one in a million search requests took 100 times longer due to an interaction
    between the memory-intensive search system and a container monitoring process.
    Disabling cAdvisor''s working set size estimation with a one-line change resolved
    the performance regression.


    [**Build a Data Lakehouse with Apache Iceberg, Polaris, Trino, and MinIO (9 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmedium.com%2F@gilles.philippart%2Fbuild-a-data-lakehouse-with-apache-iceberg-polaris-trino-minio-349c534ecd98%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/ig47CbDHSLEMB060P8s5ig_EYud-H69Slhujuee2Ppc=414)


    You can build a local, self-managed LakeHouse by pairing MinIO for S3-compatible
    storage, Apache Iceberg for open table formats, Polaris as the Iceberg REST catalog,
    and Trino for distributed SQL queries. Running entirely in Docker, this stack
    requires no cloud accounts or Hadoop dependencies, just open-source components
    wired together via Polaris''s REST interface. Iceberg ensures transactional reliability
    and schema evolution, Polaris centralizes metadata, Trino delivers sub-second
    analytics, and MinIO provides cost-free, local object storage.


    [**Delta Lake Transaction Logs Explained (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmedium.com%2Fcapital-one-tech%2Fdelta-lake-transaction-logs-explained-6b5f036e64e2%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/dGnv_QRBV7Wpvgv-AXYr97cl19iwktjsELsjSioNmT4=414)


    Delta Lake''s transaction log, stored in the _delta_log directory as JSON files,
    records every operation (insert, update, and delete) on a Delta table, ensuring
    ACID compliance, schema enforcement, and time travel capabilities. Each transaction
    log entry details changes like added or removed Parquet files to enable efficient
    metadata handling for large-scale data lakes.


    [**Leveraging Multimodal LLMs for Shopify''s Global Catalogue: Recap of Expo Talk
    at ICLR 2025 (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fshopifyengineering.myshopify.com%2Fblogs%2Fengineering%2Fleveraging-multimodal-llms%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/S00n9WbwdkQJP-GKVTaDUlE-0EEkx-7itkZxuz0L9nc=414)


    Shopify''s Global Catalogue uses multimodal Large Language Models (LLMs) to unify
    and standardize product data across millions of merchants, processing 40 million
    daily inferences to enhance search, recommendations, and conversational commerce.
    By fine-tuning open-source models like LlaVA 1.5 7B, LLaMA 3.2 11B, and Qwen2VL
    7B, Shopify achieves high accuracy and cost efficiency while addressing challenges
    like data fragmentation and multilingual product listings.


    # **Opinions & Advice**


    [**Data Lineage for MLOps (OpenLineage, DataHub, Metaflow, Airflow) (70 minute
    video)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv=OF7AoOC7W6c%26utm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/YaZVcZqWFYvb4IXc4jsA_AnUg8bcTSu1XyumalLKe8M=414)


    Data lineage is evolving from a “nice to have” into a critical component of modern
    data infrastructure. It is vital for trust, compliance, debugging, and reliable
    AI/ML workflows. Data outages often stem from silent data quality issues, not
    model drift. Lineage is increasingly essential for both operational resilience
    and regulatory pressure.


    [**Iceberg Table Corruption and Data Loss in the Wild: Part 1 (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.ryft.io%2Fblog%2Ficeberg-table-corruption-and-data-loss-in-the-wild-part-1%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/660ZX44m7ggUe_E2sSlgA4GKdGrNPol7rszYPKbktjc=414)


    A bug in Apache Iceberg caused silent data loss and table corruption by allowing
    data files to be overwritten during ingestion without indication. Critical exceptions
    arose when querying, revealing issues with the expected Parquet file signature
    and invalid S3 file ranges, highlighting the importance of continuous monitoring
    for data integrity in streaming pipelines.


    [**Embedding User-Defined Parquet Indexes (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdatafusion.apache.org%2Fblog%2F2025%2F07%2F14%2Fuser-defined-parquet-indexes%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/icu9_A5ziSx5KGz4qvqwRlMyb8QLo48lPxsqJ7Q7ESc=414)


    Standard Parquet statistics (min/max, null counts, and Bloom filters) often fail
    to prune files when predicates target high-cardinality columns. By leveraging
    Parquet''s extensible footer metadata and offset-based addressing, you can embed
    arbitrary index structures (such as per-file distinct-value lists, HyperLogLog
    sketches, or precomputed aggregates) directly into the file body without breaking
    compatibility with existing readers.


    # **Launches & Tools**


    [**Flink HTTP Full Cache Connector (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdatanutshell.com%2Fposts%2Fflink_http_full_cache_connector%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/F9bYwpRioB9vxRb3LGW6Vj9Htb1p5ztjClHzA436A8Q=414)


    The Flink HTTP Full Cache Connector preloads infrequently changing reference data
    from external HTTP endpoints into Flink state at startup, then serves asynchronous
    lookup joins with sub-millisecond latency in both Table/SQL and DataStream APIs.
    By caching entire datasets up front and refreshing only on configuration changes,
    it eliminates per-event HTTP calls, reducing external dependencies and ensuring
    consistent, low-latency enrichments for streaming applications.


    [**Cocoindex (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fcocoindex-io%2Fcocoindex%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/4mj5iRMe3MOaHl7iE7FYeFWUU9oB6tAc3KZ8EmB83lE=414)


    CocoIndex introduces a pure data flow programming model where data is immutable,
    transformations are fully traceable, and side effects are eliminated. Unlike in
    traditional workflow orchestrators that obscure data and increase pipeline complexity,
    data is the primary unit of composition, enabling transparent auditing, simplified
    debugging, and automatic downstream updates on source changes.


    [**DuckDB GSheets (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fevidence-dev%2Fduckdb_gsheets%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/LWa5Cis1s20xJuomeoyd55BOcD2N7eMtc1OgqLCDXxs=414)


    This GitHub repository offers a DuckDB extension that enables data engineers to
    read from and write to Google Sheets using SQL, streamlining data manipulation
    and integration workflows. Key features include seamless SQL access to Google
    Sheets, facilitating data extraction and analysis directly within DuckDB. This
    tool is particularly relevant for data engineers seeking to enhance their ETL
    processes by leveraging spreadsheet data efficiently.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**From Linear Regression to XGBoost: A Side-by-Side Performance Comparison (6
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmachinelearningmastery.com%2Ffrom-linear-regression-to-xgboost-a-side-by-side-performance-comparison%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/TcZnXtNm25JFzmRqT0vSyJva4SYvMjdOuc8GEWOVC8E=414)


    Linear regression provides a simple, interpretable baseline for regression tasks
    but struggles with non-linear patterns, while XGBoost, using decision tree ensembles,
    significantly improves prediction accuracy by modeling complex relationships.
    On the housing dataset, XGBoost reduced RMSE by 30% and increased R² from 0.64
    to 0.83 compared to linear regression.


    [**Using Generative AI to Accelerate Data Product Development (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmedium.com%2Fquantumblack%2Fusing-generative-ai-to-accelerate-data-product-development-9816e2f3ad2c%3Futm_source=tldrdata/1/010001982c7a30f0-8de40a08-28f6-41ad-bf4d-c5efe464095d-000000/65d7poryvvZbH1Lf8nPZBzcdX16Y2eTGXkKtfkfhh-o=414)


    AI for Data Products (AI4DP) by QuantumBlack leverages generative AI to accelerate
    and automate the creation of high-quality, reusable data products, reducing engineering
    time by up to 80%. It eliminates delays and ensures rigorous governance by grounding
    outputs in source schemas and automating critical tasks like schema design, pipeline
    construction, and quality enforcement.

- cleaned_md: 'Amazon jumps onto the enterprise agent hype train.


    It’s Wednesday. At last week’s AWS Summit in Manhattan, Amazon execs detailed
    how they’re moving all-the-rage AI agents from the proof-of-concept stage to “real-world
    production use cases.” Tech Brew’s Patrick Kulp was on the ground at the event
    to collect all the details.


    In today’s edition:


    - [Amazon jumps onto the enterprise agent hype train](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C6X?mblid=5212accaac00&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
