    # AI


    ## [Taking action](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C6X?mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    [![AWS logo at a conference](https://cdn.sanity.io/images/bl383u0v/production/092fabb7cc86fad7fb792994bbc41b1a153f652b-6048x4032.jpg?w=668&q=70&auto=format)](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C6X?mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    *Noah Berger/Getty Images*


    No, it’s not a TikTok aesthetic that involves dressing like a spy: AgentCore is
    a new toolkit from Amazon’s cloud arm designed to help companies build and deploy
    [AI agents](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BYL?mblid=df44e40ee456&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).


    With these autonomous systems [billed as the next big thing](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/rH5?mblid=4fc64eac61b1&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    in AI, companies everywhere are itching to [create some of their own](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/AcD?mblid=f8de0d616f2e&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).
    But like all generative AI projects, [moving from experiments](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/t95?mblid=2114f3789f31&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    to full-fledged production can be daunting.


    Amazon Bedrock AgentCore is the latest in a [long line](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/tbZ?mblid=042ffe0087ea&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    of new products from tech giants aimed at easing that process. The platform has
    tools for managing memory, observability, helping agents access other digital
    services and the web at large, running generated code, and coordinating between
    agents.


    Amazon announced AgentCore, along with a new agent marketplace and a [coding tool
    called Kiro](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C6-?mblid=fb3be29c6d46&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy),
    at its AWS Summit in Manhattan last week.


    “There are a bunch of missing pieces that make it really difficult \[to] move
    from \[proofs of concept] that are sitting in laptops to agents in real-world
    production use cases,” Swami Sivasubramanian, VP of AWS Agentic AI, said on stage
    at the event.


    [**Keep reading here**](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C6X?mblid=b58c97c4cdab&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).—PK


    # GREEN TECH


    ## [Storage unit](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C6Y?mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    [![Energy storage station](https://cdn.sanity.io/images/bl383u0v/production/89f52782d6c3a4ffb854e18253b1ed5105197893-5272x3948.jpg?w=668&q=70&auto=format)](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C6Y?mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    *Young777/Getty Images*


    The electric vehicle market is on [shaky ground](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BDJ?mblid=dd25bef78cc1&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    amid cooling demand and the looming expiration of federal incentives.


    Flexibility could be the name of the game for EV sector players in the coming
    months and years—and a new deal between General Motors and battery recycler Redwood
    Materials may point to a promising opportunity: energy storage.


    In a July 16 news release, the two companies announced a non-binding memorandum
    of understanding “to accelerate deployment of energy storage systems using both
    new [US-manufactured batteries from GM](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/BY2?mblid=cd762825c41a&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    and second-life battery packs from GM electric vehicles.”


    GM touted the deal as “a significant step toward taking GM’s advanced battery
    technology beyond EVs.” The automaker already had been sending used EV battery
    materials to Redwood under an existing agreement.


    GM has its own burgeoning energy business, which in October [launched](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C72?mblid=3b870825ae55&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)
    a stationary energy storage unit for EVs dubbed “PowerBank.” The product allows
    users to transfer and store energy from the grid. Other automakers, like Tesla,
    also offer energy storage products.


    **Data center demand:** Driving the agreement, according to GM and Redwood executives,
    is the surging demand for electricity, in part from a proliferation of new data
    centers.


    [**Keep reading here**](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C6Y?mblid=94eb02a9af8a&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).—JG


    # GREEN TECH


    ## [Hyperlocal](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C6Z?mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    [![A smoky view of the suburbs in Oregon](https://cdn.sanity.io/images/bl383u0v/production/ca4d7b42bc5096393db8601d8eacb785e3fb098b-2560x1920.jpg?w=668&q=70&auto=format)](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C6Z?mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy)


    *Melinda Gray/Getty Images*


    Frequent wildfires and other severe weather events in Oregon often leave communities
    at the end of power lines without electricity. Now, thanks to two new state laws,
    tribes, municipalities, and third-party developers looking to set up and own microgrids
    in rural areas will soon have the legal and regulatory framework to do so.


    Governor Tina Kotek recently signed House Bill 2065, which requires public utilities
    to provide groups needing microgrids in their area with the required information,
    and House Bill 2066, which calls on the state’s Public Utility Commission to “establish
    a regulatory framework for allowing the ownership, deployment, and use of microgrids
    and community microgrids within the service territories of electric companies,”
    into law. Both are the first of their kind in the country.


    “Red tape should never get in the way of technology that could mean the difference
    between fast, efficient electricity restoration and delays and risk when power
    outages strike,” Kotek said in a statement. “These new laws will help bring more
    microgrids online faster and deliver cost savings to consumers in every part of
    the state.”


    Prior to these laws, entities hoping to build and own their own microgrids faced
    legal hurdles and bureaucratic bottlenecks when they tried to set them up, Sustainable
    Northwest President Dylan Kruse told Tech Brew. Sustainable Northwest is a clean
    tech and regenerative farming nonprofit that helped draft both bills and will
    help create the regulatory framework.


    [**Keep reading here**](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C6Z?mblid=3f21439cd9f9&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy).—TC

    citing data from XDI. That number is expected to jump to nearly 27% by 2050.

    The problem is that the moment you use it, the boundary between tool and collaborator,
    even author, begins to blur.”—[Meghan O’Rourke](https://links.morningbrew.com/c/C7a?mblid=17b66ac482c6&mbcid=40800710.390134&mid=858c9b623cc2711c5f02e0f39af85262&mbuuid=1CAffDM1mBsqW8DsMz3ifDsy),

    # TLDR Design 2025-07-25


    # **News & Trends**


    [**Transform Your Photos Into Videos and Remix Your Pics in Google Photos (3 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fblog.google%2Fproducts%2Fphotos%2Fphoto-to-video-remix-create-tab%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001984185b2af-c4f6d004-38bc-4e93-ba07-9657043939ad-000000/g4n0XBoaccXWhGpCFTSeQQv0looFne25LAQRRroeQjk=415)


    Google Photos announced new creative tools that transform static images into six-second
    videos and artistic remixes using AI technology. The photo-to-video feature, powered
    by Veo 2, rolls out today, while Remix transforms pictures into anime and comic
    styles. A new Create tab, arriving in August, will centralize all creative features,
    including safety measures such as digital watermarks.


    [**Build with Your Team, Not Around Them: Real-time Collaboration in Webflow is
    Here (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwf-blog-2021.webflow.io%2Fblog%2Freal-time-collaboration%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001984185b2af-c4f6d004-38bc-4e93-ba07-9657043939ad-000000/x9VIx0HVM7LFsvMdN1gwVMuy6dr3YWct5Nb2u4BV1nk=415)


    Webflow has launched real-time collaboration in private beta, enabling entire
    website teams, including designers, developers, and marketers to work simultaneously
    on the same page without handoffs or delays. This feature streamlines workflows,
    reduces bottlenecks, and enables faster, more integrated project delivery, with
    updates syncing instantly and providing visibility into who is working on what.


    [**Meta''s Neural Interface Wristband Reads Your Muscle Signals to Control Computers
    (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.yankodesign.com%2F2025%2F07%2F23%2Fmetas-neural-interface-wristband-reads-your-muscle-signals-to-control-computers%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001984185b2af-c4f6d004-38bc-4e93-ba07-9657043939ad-000000/Bf4Gool5Q3Tv8I_bJ2NCqTzWLC4GSOT7rniFxl1Vh1A=415)


    Meta has developed a neural interface wristband that utilizes surface electromyography
    to detect electrical signals from muscle movements, enabling users to control
    computers without physical contact. This breakthrough challenges traditional wearable
    design by eliminating setup friction, enhancing accessibility, and introducing
    new interaction models that could influence the future of AR, computing, and health
    tech.


    # **Opinions & Tutorials**


    [**Protect Your Creativity from Idea Killers (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwhydesignishard.substack.com%2Fp%2Fprotect-your-creativity-from-idea%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001984185b2af-c4f6d004-38bc-4e93-ba07-9657043939ad-000000/CbNvKCtxMd3U1bYXfXJtQRBc4dSLVKTkA2eF1-uYMrI=415)


    "Idea killers" are statements that prevent organizational change despite often
    containing poor logic. Common examples include "we tried that before" and "we
    don''t do that here," typically said by those in positions of power. The solution
    involves preparing counterarguments and asking questions to examine the value
    of ideas rather than allowing dismissive statements.


    [**A Holistic Framework for Shared Design Leadership (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Falistapart.com%2Farticle%2Fan-holistic-framework-for-shared-design-leadership%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001984185b2af-c4f6d004-38bc-4e93-ba07-9657043939ad-000000/gC8RFfYvy9vGWL8InLdHTxFFhaudfEiyQr0SibtpldM=415)


    A Design Manager and a Lead Designer may approach the same problem from different
    angles—people and psychology vs. craft and execution—but both are essential parts
    of a healthy, high-performing design team. By embracing their overlapping responsibilities
    and aligning around shared goals across three “systems” (nervous, muscular, and
    circulatory), they can create a resilient, strategically aligned team that produces
    excellent, sustainable design work.


    [**How to sell the European Accessibility Act to your boss (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fuxdesign.cc%2Fhow-to-sell-the-european-accessibility-act-to-your-boss-993d4116c56c%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001984185b2af-c4f6d004-38bc-4e93-ba07-9657043939ad-000000/F8gxykmsJ0dl9v3ya9jZ1Nk3UEvIg55m-0HGnsF8urE=415)


    As of June 28, the European Accessibility Act (EAA) made it legally mandatory
    for businesses selling in the EU to meet accessibility standards—or risk hefty
    fines from multiple member states. Beyond legal compliance, accessibility improves
    user experience, expands your potential customer base, and enhances product quality
    for everyone, making it a smart business decision, not just a moral one.

    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**The Product Triad: Design''s Role (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.nngroup.com%2Farticles%2Fthe-product-triad-designs-role%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001984185b2af-c4f6d004-38bc-4e93-ba07-9657043939ad-000000/PcesAjSXz_SvxRYxJ3h-rYWfLXNPKh3ObtwVEdhmIwY=415)


    The product triad organizes Agile product teams with one representative each from
    design, product management, and engineering working as equal partners. Based on
    IDEO''s Desirable-Viable-Feasible framework, effective triads collaborate across
    all three aspects rather than maintaining siloed ownership. Designers contribute
    beyond just desirability by understanding business objectives, conducting user
    research, and collaborating closely with engineering to ensure feasible implementation.


    [**Standards Launches New Site And Is Quietly Building the Internet''s Brand Backbone
    (1 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fabduzeedo.com%2Fstandards-launches-new-site-and-quietly-building-internets-brand-backbone%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001984185b2af-c4f6d004-38bc-4e93-ba07-9657043939ad-000000/v0UXcdq8GdnxYpCvq9UT3b671fb8RL-hSRiVrLrHU1k=415)


    Design software startup Standards has launched a new site showcasing published
    brand systems from top companies like Cash App, Mailchimp, and The Obama Foundation,
    marking a major milestone in its journey from a niche archival project to a fast-growing
    design platform. Born from the success of reissuing iconic style guides, Standards
    now serves over 1,000 companies, with 300%+ MRR growth—all while remaining fully
    bootstrapped.


    [**Fairphone 6 Introduces Modular Add-Ons and Next-Level Repairability (4 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdesign-milk.com%2Ffairphone-6-introduces-modular-add-ons-and-next-level-repairability%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdesign/1/010001984185b2af-c4f6d004-38bc-4e93-ba07-9657043939ad-000000/LCk5TQIbujMIJ3yIa9LLh3892JQlDUl--y5-OmB7g2Y=415)


    The Fairphone 6 continues the company''s mission to challenge disposable tech
    culture by offering a modular, repairable smartphone with a refined design, user-swappable
    parts, and solid mid-range performance. With features like a removable battery,
    upgradeable components, and at least five years of software support, it aims to
    extend device lifespan and empower users—proving that sustainability and usability
    can go hand in hand.

    # TLDR DevOps 2025-07-23


    # **News & Trends**


    [**The 2025 Docker State of Application Development Report (10 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.docker.com%2Fblog%2F2025-docker-state-of-app-dev%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019837077f98-7c53d3ee-2955-42c7-85bd-522cfdecaf81-000000/7wFapc0QWAdWMBoO_Z6JCGUGaI85lLqIBUngqKbzuAM=415)


    AI adoption is rising but uneven across industries, with IT leading both in usage
    and strategy. Meanwhile, security is now a shared responsibility, with most organizations
    keeping it in-house and involving developers, DevOps, and team leads. Despite
    better tools and cloud-native workflows, developers still face bottlenecks in
    time estimation, task planning, and pull-request reviews.


    [**Enhancing GKE data protection with cross-project backup and restore (5 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fcloud.google.com%2Fblog%2Fproducts%2Fstorage-data-transfer%2Fbackup-for-gke-supports-cross-project-backup-and-restore%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019837077f98-7c53d3ee-2955-42c7-85bd-522cfdecaf81-000000/YEprqSyFFBfUsKGpu0dk8qld9FnqrVwpGKHgSs6q3SI=415)


    Google Kubernetes Engine now supports cross-project backup and restore, enabling
    centralized management of backups across multiple Google Cloud projects with improved
    security and disaster recovery. This capability enhances operational workflows
    by allowing environment seeding, cloning, and delegated restore access while maintaining
    strict separation of duties for compliance.


    [**Shutdown season - the Q2 2025 Internet disruption summary (16 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fblog.cloudflare.com%2Fq2-2025-internet-disruption-summary%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019837077f98-7c53d3ee-2955-42c7-85bd-522cfdecaf81-000000/ifB4GLGpGGtgUYr8I4ULhrCfCc-axy4qzKBLSc5yoxM=415)


    In Q2 2025, Cloudflare observed government-directed Internet shutdowns in Libya,
    Iran, Iraq, Syria, and Panama, a reversal from Q1 when no shutdowns were seen.
    A major power outage in Spain and Portugal also disrupted connectivity. Cyberattacks
    targeted a Russian provider, knocking the network offline for 10 hours after reaching
    70.07 Gbps.


    # **Opinions & Tutorials**


    [**Observability for containerized workloads: How to run Grafana Beyla as a sidecar
    in Amazon ECS (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgrafana.com%2Fblog%2F2025%2F07%2F09%2Fobservability-for-containerized-workloads-how-to-run-grafana-beyla-as-a-sidecar-in-amazon-ecs%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019837077f98-7c53d3ee-2955-42c7-85bd-522cfdecaf81-000000/5AKqZ18SYgNu6E7rVyMqWJcXy9N1MKq63lqAqC54F4Q=415)


    Grafana Beyla can be deployed as a sidecar in Amazon ECS on EC2 to enable eBPF-based
    auto-instrumentation for containerized applications without requiring code changes.
    This setup uses Grafana Alloy to collect and forward telemetry data to Grafana
    Cloud to improve observability and simplify tracing.


    [**Prometheus Labels: Understanding and Best Practices (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.cncf.io%2Fblog%2F2025%2F07%2F22%2Fprometheus-labels-understanding-and-best-practices%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019837077f98-7c53d3ee-2955-42c7-85bd-522cfdecaf81-000000/fzqSZgqoHKngWaxlc-SJuBmyuYUw7IOppkcUGgG9aYA=415)


    Prometheus labels add context to metrics and facilitate filtering and aggregations.
    The labels enrich metrics with metadata, improving visibility across services
    and environments, and enable the use of PromQL for generating queries and custom
    dashboards.


    # **Resources & Tools**


    [**helm unittest (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fhelm-unittest%2Fhelm-unittest%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019837077f98-7c53d3ee-2955-42c7-85bd-522cfdecaf81-000000/Cv26c-f-8Rr-uHBBJbG066E0dT93v83AR7NUOTbf_T4=415)


    A unit test framework for Kubernetes Helm charts, written as a Helm plugin, allows
    users to validate charts using YAML. The helm unittest plugin is inspired by helm-template
    and jest, with snapshot testing and printing format borrowed from the latter.
    It includes features like JsonPath support, document selectors, and schema support
    in popular IDEs.


    [**kubectl-ai (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2FGoogleCloudPlatform%2Fkubectl-ai%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019837077f98-7c53d3ee-2955-42c7-85bd-522cfdecaf81-000000/UXBtvhHBVJYiany_TBgbGuxD5TSN1Jw_n9FeuT0QQcE=415)


    kubectl-ai, an AI-powered Kubernetes assistant, translates user intent into Kubernetes
    operations via integration with AI models from Gemini, VertexAI, Azure OpenAI,
    OpenAI, Grok, and local LLMs.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Deploying Azure Service Groups with Terraform AzAPI (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fluke.geek.nz%2Fazure%2Fservice-groups-terraform-azapi%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019837077f98-7c53d3ee-2955-42c7-85bd-522cfdecaf81-000000/TtXIV0IdbHmMsWr2Z6V3ItmPQvQQvfa86e_T2k09_6U=415)


    Microsoft Azure now offers Service Groups in limited public preview, enabling
    flexible, application-centric grouping of resources across subscriptions without
    altering existing RBAC or policy structures. Using Terraform AzAPI, users can
    create nested, hierarchical service groups to organize resources by teams, projects,
    or services for improved visibility, cost tracking, and operational management.


    [**Quicksilver v2: evolution of a globally distributed key-value store (Part 1)
    (14 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fblog.cloudflare.com%2Fquicksilver-v2-evolution-of-a-globally-distributed-key-value-store-part-1%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019837077f98-7c53d3ee-2955-42c7-85bd-522cfdecaf81-000000/Y-AqMeAsAcKuQok3Th222Sy3p5jH347UmNRuGVhoVBU=415)


    Quicksilver v1.5 introduces a proxy-replica architecture to reduce disk usage
    across Cloudflare''s global network by splitting key-value store roles into full-data
    replicas and persistent cache-based proxies, enabling up to 50% space savings
    while laying groundwork for future scalability. To maintain consistency and performance,
    the system implements multiversion concurrency control, sliding window caching,
    negative lookup optimizations, and a dynamic discovery mechanism.


    [**Debugging the One-in-a-Million Failure: Migrating Pinterest''s Search Infrastructure
    to Kubernetes (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmedium.com%2Fpinterest-engineering%2Fdebugging-the-one-in-a-million-failure-migrating-pinterests-search-infrastructure-to-kubernetes-bef9af9dabf4%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019837077f98-7c53d3ee-2955-42c7-85bd-522cfdecaf81-000000/J2euRda77v2kGvvIKd4H9mpHUBGwssEnKwEvi12cR44=415)


    Pinterest engineers migrating their Manas search infrastructure to Kubernetes
    discovered that cAdvisor, a container monitoring tool, caused significant latency
    spikes due to its memory usage tracking. The issue was resolved by disabling cAdvisor''s
    working set size estimation, a feature that scans the kernel''s page structures
    and clears access bits, as the process conflicted with Manas'' memory-intensive
    search operations. This fix unblocked the Kubernetes migration and improved platform
    stability for memory-bound systems at Pinterest.

    TODO comments aren''t always meant to be completed—they often serve as contextual
    breadcrumbs, capturing the author''s thought process, known limitations, or possible
    improvements.


    [**Automating Away Claude''s Bad Habits with Hooks (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwriteaheadblogg.ing%2Fposts%2Fclaude-hooks-auto-fix-trailing-whitespace%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/0100019837077f98-7c53d3ee-2955-42c7-85bd-522cfdecaf81-000000/QBDogQV7Co70EHtXRQCUOeE-VT8pWSykigA3qqMfmsI=415)


    Claude Code''s new Hooks feature enables automatic code cleanup by running shell
    commands after specific actions, such as file edits.'

    \ Explained in 1 Diagram\n\n---\n\n## System Design Interview – BIGGEST Mistakes\
    \ to Avoid\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/youtube/w_728,c_limit/l_youtube_play_qyqt8q,w_120/OvufRkoD-D0)](https://substack.com/redirect/f7ae2e28-f475-4085-ab23-2bf2dc53d601?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \n---\n\n## 12 MCP Servers You Can Use in 2025\n\n[![Image](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!qWiX!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2Fa38920cb-0942-42a8-957c-35ad76801954_3389x4096.jpeg\
    \ \"Image\")](https://substack.com/redirect/435a6244-0523-4451-9ec3-ff15ee77f251?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \nMCP (Model Context Protocol) is an open standard that simplifies how AI models,\
    \ particularly LLMs, interact with external data sources, tools, and services.\
    \ An MCP server acts as a bridge between these AI models and external tools. Here\
    \ are the top MCP servers:\n\n1.  File System MCP Server  \n    Allows the LLM\
    \ to directly access the local file system to read, write, and create directories.\n\
    2.  GitHub MCP Server  \n    Connects Claude to GitHub repos and allows file updates,\
    \ code searching.\n3.  Slack MCP Server  \n    MCP Server for Slack API, enabling\
    \ Claude to interact with Slack workspaces.\n4.  Google Maps MCP Server  \n  \
    \  MCP Server for Google Maps API.\n5.  Docker MCP Server  \n    Integrate with\
    \ Docker to manage containers, images, volumes, and networks.\n6.  Brave MCP Server\
    \  \n    Web and local search using Brave’s Search API.\n7.  PostgreSQL MCP Server\
    \  \n    An MCP server that enables LLM to inspect database schemas and execute\
    \ read-only queries.\n8.  Google Drive MCP Server  \n    An MCP server that integrates\
    \ with Google Drive to allow reading and searching over files.\n9.  Redis MCP\
    \ Server  \n    MCP Server that provides access to Redis databases.\n10. Notion\
    \ MCP Server  \n    This project implements an MCP server for the Notion API.\n\
    11. Stripe MCP Server  \n    MCP Server to interact with the Stripe API.\n12.\
    \ Perplexity MCP Server  \n    An MCP Server that connects to Perplexity’s Sonar\
    \ API for real-time search.\n\nOver to you: Which other MCP Server will you add\
    \ to the list?\n\n---\n\n## MCP Versus A2A Protocol\n\nThe Model Context Protocol\
    \ (MCP) connects AI agents to external data sources, such as databases, APIs,\
    \ and files, via an MCP server, thereby enriching their responses with real-world\
    \ context.\n\n[![Image](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!lwlx!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F63d80727-6cb7-456a-a71f-ef8d8ae4aa7b_2360x2770.png\
    \ \"Image\")](https://substack.com/redirect/e64cc629-3912-4b85-87d1-f8961c72e5e2?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \nGoogle’s Agent-to-Agent (A2A) Protocol enables AI agents to communicate and\
    \ collaborate, allowing them to delegate tasks, share results, and enhance each\
    \ other’s capabilities.\n\nMCP and A2A can be combined into a holistic architecture.\
    \ Here’s how it can work:\n\n1. Each AI agent (using tools like Langchain with\
    \ GPT or Claude) connects to external tools via MCP servers for data access.\n\
    2. The external tools can comprise cloud APIs, local files, web search, or communication\
    \ platforms like Slack.\n3. Simultaneously, the AI agents can communicate with\
    \ one another using the A2A protocol to coordinate actions, share intermediate\
    \ outputs, and solve complex tasks collectively.\n\nThis architecture enables\
    \ both rich external context (via MCP) and decentralized agent collaboration (via\
    \ A2A).\n\nOver to you: What else will you add to understand the MCP vs A2A Protocol\
    \ capabilities?\n\n---\n\n## How can Cache Systems go wrong?\n\nThe diagram below\
    \ shows 4 typical cases where caches can go wrong and their solutions.\n\n[![Image](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!y_iB!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F5791931d-46af-4ea2-bffe-5fea406baab3_3000x3900.jpeg\
    \ \"Image\")](https://substack.com/redirect/17b8335d-891b-41ea-8b3c-ac255ff8561b?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \n1. Thunder herd problem  \n   This happens when a large number of keys in the\
    \ cache expire at the same time. Then the query requests directly hit the database,\
    \ which overloads the database.\n\n   There are two ways to mitigate this issue:\
    \ one is to avoid setting the same expiry time for the keys, adding a random number\
    \ in the configuration; the other is to allow only the core business data to hit\
    \ the database and prevent non-core data to access the database until the cache\
    \ is back up.\n\n2. Cache penetration  \n   This happens when the key doesn’t\
    \ exist in the cache or the database. The application cannot retrieve relevant\
    \ data from the database to update the cache. This problem creates a lot of pressure\
    \ on both the cache and the database.\n\n   To solve this, there are two suggestions.\
    \ One is to cache a null value for non-existent keys, avoiding hitting the database.\
    \ The other is to use a bloom filter to check the key existence first, and if\
    \ the key doesn’t exist, we can avoid hitting the database.\n\n3. Cache breakdown\
    \  \n   This is similar to the thunder herd problem. It happens when a hot key\
    \ expires. A large number of requests hit the database.\n\n   Since the hot keys\
    \ take up 80% of the queries, we do not set an expiration time for them.\n\n4.\
    \ Cache crash  \n   This happens when the cache is down and all the requests go\
    \ to the database.\n\n   There are two ways to solve this problem. One is to set\
    \ up a circuit breaker, and when the cache is down, the application services cannot\
    \ visit the cache or the database. The other is to set up a cluster for the cache\
    \ to improve cache availability.\n\nOver to you: Have you met any of these issues\
    \ in production?\n\n---\n\n## 8 System Design Concepts Explained in 1 Diagram\n\
    \n[![Image](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!aYrc!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F4e52d277-d633-405c-a419-16ec2b74ad02_2360x3114.png\
    \ \"Image\")](https://substack.com/redirect/42bada10-a1ed-4c2b-b1b6-0f1e37b12c9f?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \nNon-functional requirements define the quality attributes of a system that ensure\
    \ it performs reliably under real-world conditions. Some key NFRs, along with\
    \ the implementation approach, are as follows:\n\n1. Availability with Load Balancers\
    \  \n   Availability ensures that a system remains operational and accessible\
    \ to users at all times. Using load balancers distributes traffic across multiple\
    \ service instances to eliminate single points of failure\n2. Latency with CDNs\
    \  \n   Latency refers to the time delay experienced in a system’s response to\
    \ a user request. CDNs reduce latency by caching content closer to users.\n3.\
    \ Scalability with Replication  \n   Scalability is the system’s ability to handle\
    \ increased load by adding resources. Replication distributes data across multiple\
    \ nodes, enabling higher throughput and workload.\n4. Durability with Transaction\
    \ Log  \n   Durability guarantees that once data is committed, it remains safe\
    \ even in the event of failure. Transaction logs persist all operations, allowing\
    \ the system to reconstruct the state after a crash.\n5. Consistency with Eventual\
    \ Consistency  \n   Consistency means that all users see the same data. Eventual\
    \ consistency allows temporary differences, but synchronizes replicas over time\
    \ to a consistent state.\n6. Modularity with Loose Coupling and High Cohesion\
    \  \n   Modularity promotes building systems with well-separated and self-contained\
    \ components. Loose coupling and high cohesion help achieve the same.\n7. Configurability\
    \  \n   Configurability allows a system to be easily adjusted or modified without\
    \ altering core logic. Configuration-as-Code manages infra and app settings via\
    \ version-controlled scripts.\n8. Resiliency with Message Queues  \n   Resiliency\
    \ is a system’s ability to recover from failures and continue operating smoothly.\
    \ Message queues decouple components and buffer tasks, enabling retries.\n\nOver\
    \ to you: Which other NFR or strategy will you add to the list?\n"

    # TLDR Fintech 2025-07-21


    # **News & Trends**


    [**OpenAI working on payment checkout system within ChatGPT (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2Fy0fDuE/1/010001982d1ddf35-a0275da8-976a-44a4-a048-e7ee3cbb9f4e-000000/zBc5yVpIGbBYyR3CdAVJzWAiIb6GCo65KpcwQBRuKMQ=414)


    OpenAI is reportedly building a native checkout experience inside ChatGPT that
    would let users make purchases from third-party vendors directly within the chatbot.
    The move could position ChatGPT as a transactional platform, not just a conversational
    one, enabling a more seamless blend of shopping and AI assistance. This could
    create new revenue opportunities for developers and OpenAI alike.


    [**Jack Dorsey''s Block is set to join S&P 500 index, replacing Hess (2 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ffinancialpost.com%2Fpmn%2Fbusiness-pmn%2Fjack-dorseys-block-is-set-to-join-sp-500-index-replacing-hess%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001982d1ddf35-a0275da8-976a-44a4-a048-e7ee3cbb9f4e-000000/b3DNy4gQYPk-LP-bq7sbi6F2OcKosdGVdhN09jPg6BU=414)


    Digital payments firm Block will be added to the S&P 500 index, replacing energy
    company Hess as of July 24. The shakeup follows Chevron''s acquisition of Hess,
    which is expected to close soon. Block''s inclusion marks a symbolic win for fintech,
    signaling growing acceptance of newer tech-driven firms in traditional financial
    benchmarks.


    [**Stripe acquires real-time payments startup Orum (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Fposts%2Fmarcelvanoost_%25F0%259D%2598%25BD%25F0%259D%2599%258D%25F0%259D%2599%2580%25F0%259D%2598%25BC%25F0%259D%2599%2586%25F0%259D%2599%2584%25F0%259D%2599%2589%25F0%259D%2599%2582-stripes-buying-spree-activity-7352353875221184512-K_IB%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001982d1ddf35-a0275da8-976a-44a4-a048-e7ee3cbb9f4e-000000/gBTJcQq_wY5Y9vBpD3l7hd9LtSQupgRKuQWeyMaPmHI=414)


    Stripe has acquired Orum, a New York-based fintech startup that specializes in
    fast, intelligent payment routing using machine learning APIs. Orum''s platform
    helps move money across various payment rails—ACH, RTP, credit cards, and potentially
    blockchain—reducing settlement times to under 24 hours. The deal follows Stripe''s
    broader M&A momentum, including its recent buys of Privy and Bridge, as it sharpens
    its edge in the real-time payments space.


    # **Deep Dives & Reports**


    [**The rise of vertical fintech: Tailwinds, opportunities, and AI-driven acceleration
    (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmedium.com%2F@dawncapitalteam%2Fdawn-deep-dive-ai-and-vertical-fintech-strategies-2a7a027fbd51%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001982d1ddf35-a0275da8-976a-44a4-a048-e7ee3cbb9f4e-000000/XWJRkKy4Ow7KCBFMYNfMBmnREvuCaH6CbmDbHn3fzbA=414)


    Vertical fintech is entering its breakout phase as industries demand tailored
    financial products and workflows. Companies like Cedar, WeTravel, and Cloover
    are expanding from niche offerings into full financial operating systems by embedding
    payments, credit, and software tightly within vertical-specific workflows. AI
    is driving faster product expansion and unlocking underserved markets such as
    construction, logistics, and healthcare, where complex high-value financial flows
    create strong moats for vertical players.


    [**Apps are dying. Agents are buying (20 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.fintechbrainfood.com%2Fp%2Fagents-are-buying%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001982d1ddf35-a0275da8-976a-44a4-a048-e7ee3cbb9f4e-000000/d3C2HnzyhNZlZoe62oxJkjLj282YOO21tG2bOqcbSow=414)


    Agentic commerce—where AI agents handle discovery, purchase, and payments—will
    reshape fintech and commerce. Apps dissolve into “liquid software,” checkouts
    become invisible, and merchants face discovery challenges as SEO shifts to AEO
    (agent experience optimization). This post explores Visa''s intelligent commerce,
    MCP servers (like Ogment AI), security risks, and whether this is the Nokia WAP
    era or the iPhone moment for AI-driven commerce. The bull case: a platform shift
    10x bigger than mobile.


    [**GENIUS Passed Into Law. Now What? (15 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ffintechbusinessweekly.substack.com%2Fp%2Fgenius-passed-into-law-now-what%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001982d1ddf35-a0275da8-976a-44a4-a048-e7ee3cbb9f4e-000000/PpV3gl-8jJ2j2d2wXu8RCIwzYi78YRZB6VD6hpSiU6E=414)


    President Trump capped off “Crypto Week” on Friday by signing the GENIUS Act into
    law, describing it as an “exciting new frontier.” The measure creates a dual federal
    and state licensing and oversight framework for “payment stablecoins.” Trump''s
    signature on GENIUS passes it into law, kicking off an implementation period that
    will take 18 months or until 120 days after the date on which primary federal
    stablecoin regulators issue any final implementation regulations, whichever comes
    first. It is expected that GENIUS will become effective around November 2026.

    than 700 AI applications and is leaning on the technology to enhance internal
    operations, fraud detection, and client services.


    [**FDIC proposes inflationary adjustments (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.cbh.com%2Finsights%2Falerts%2Ffdic-proposes-inflationary-adjustments%2F%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001982d1ddf35-a0275da8-976a-44a4-a048-e7ee3cbb9f4e-000000/AlsT-4YPKsbtTFb1pcczy0kvUB1igEkasWIdbIWFPog=414)


    The FDIC is planning to raise several monetary thresholds tied to inflation in
    an effort to modernize outdated regulatory benchmarks. The move is designed to
    keep compliance requirements proportional to a bank''s size and complexity, offering
    targeted relief to smaller institutions. The FDIC estimates this proposal could
    potentially lighten regulatory burdens for over 1,500 community banks—especially
    important given that, over the past 20 years, the total number of banks has dropped
    by 50%, with banks under $500 million in assets declining by 27.6% while larger
    banks have grown by over 75%.


    [**JPMorgan found yet another revenue stream - your bank data (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinas.substack.com%2Fi%2F168804289%2Fjpmorgan-found-yet-another-revenue-stream-your-bank-data%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001982d1ddf35-a0275da8-976a-44a4-a048-e7ee3cbb9f4e-000000/1wGfggYfgv71B_-jYT5Cb62PJs7uaNJXPqilc6I299c=414)


    Banking giant JPMorgan Chase just shook the entire financial technology landscape
    by implementing fees for FinTech companies seeking access to customer bank account
    data. This marks the end of an era where such access has traditionally been provided
    at no cost, fundamentally altering the economic foundation upon which many FinTech
    services operate.

- cleaned_md: "![](https://eotrx.substackcdn.com/open?token=eyJtIjoiPDIwMjUwNzIyMTUzMDQ0LjMuODBiYzY0MzFiZTA3MGQxMUBtZzIuc3Vic3RhY2suY29tPiIsInUiOjM0OTczODE2MywiciI6InN1bWl0dXAuZGV2QGdtYWlsLmNvbSIsImQiOiJtZzIuc3Vic3RhY2suY29tIiwicCI6MTY4NTAwNTgyLCJ0IjoibmV3c2xldHRlciIsImEiOiJldmVyeW9uZSIsInMiOjgxNzEzMiwiYyI6InBvc3QiLCJmIjp0cnVlLCJwb3NpdGlvbiI6InRvcCIsImlhdCI6MTc1MzE5OTA5NywiZXhwIjoxNzU1NzkxMDk3LCJpc3MiOiJwdWItMCIsInN1YiI6ImVvIn0.qusd9k6vVX9Z3mQp08FE9BoVngBLrG6aSvksIUn7dus)\n\
    \nNubank adopted a foundation model-based approach, which has already been transforming\
    \ domains like natural language processing and computer vision.\n\n# [How Nubank\
    \ Uses AI Models to Analyze Transaction Data for 100M Users](https://substack.substack.com/app-link/post?publication_id=817132&post_id=168500582&utm_source=post-email-title&utm_campaign=email-post-title&isFreemail=true&r=5s83oz&token=eyJ1c2VyX2lkIjozNDk3MzgxNjMsInBvc3RfaWQiOjE2ODUwMDU4MiwiaWF0IjoxNzUzMTk5MDk2LCJleHAiOjE3NTU3OTEwOTYsImlzcyI6InB1Yi04MTcxMzIiLCJzdWIiOiJwb3N0LXJlYWN0aW9uIn0.OgICzf8hUBDTv28JQGS5__6FUH3LYqzQ-PQu5wWomgU)\n\
    \n[ByteByteGo](https://substack.com/@bytebytego399569)\n\nJul 22\n\n*Disclaimer:\
    \ The details in this post have been derived from the articles shared online by\
    \ the Nubank Engineering Team. All credit for the technical details goes to the\
    \ Nubank Engineering Team. The links to the original articles and sources are\
    \ present in the references section at the end of the post. We’ve attempted to\
    \ analyze the details and provide our input about them. If you find any inaccuracies\
    \ or omissions, please leave a comment, and we will do our best to fix them.*\n\
    \nUnderstanding customer behavior at scale is one of the core challenges facing\
    \ modern financial institutions. With millions of users generating billions of\
    \ transactions, the ability to interpret and act on this data is critical for\
    \ offering relevant products, detecting fraud, assessing risk, and improving user\
    \ experience.\n\nHistorically, the financial industry has relied on traditional\
    \ machine learning techniques built around tabular data. In these systems, raw\
    \ transaction data is manually transformed into structured features (such as income\
    \ levels, spending categories, or transaction counts) that serve as inputs to\
    \ predictive models.\n\nWhile this approach has been effective, it suffers from\
    \ two major limitations:\n\n- Manual feature engineering is time-intensive and\
    \ brittle, often requiring domain expertise and extensive trial-and-error.\n-\
    \ Generalization is limited. Features designed for one task (for example, credit\
    \ scoring) may not be useful for others (for example, recommendation or fraud\
    \ detection), leading to duplicated effort across teams.\n\nTo address these constraints,\
    \ Nubank adopted a foundation model-based approach, which has already been transforming\
    \ domains like natural language processing and computer vision. Instead of relying\
    \ on hand-crafted features, foundation models are trained directly on raw transaction\
    \ data using self-supervised learning. This allows them to automatically learn\
    \ general-purpose embeddings that represent user behavior in a compact and expressive\
    \ form.\n\nThe objective is ambitious: to process trillions of transactions and\
    \ extract universal user representations that can power a wide range of downstream\
    \ tasks such as credit modeling, personalization, anomaly detection, and more.\
    \ By doing so, Nubank aims to unify its modeling efforts, reduce repetitive feature\
    \ work, and improve predictive performance across the board.\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!rEVm!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F241aae8d-64f2-495a-8f27-016704d60f18_1600x989.png)](https://substack.com/redirect/51b3efb9-0ad0-42d6-b6f2-55c800340c4e?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \nIn this article, we look at Nubank’s system design for building and deploying\
    \ these foundation models. We will trace the complete lifecycle from data representation\
    \ and model architecture to pretraining, fine-tuning, and integration with traditional\
    \ tabular systems.\n\n## Overall Architecture of Nubank’s System\n\nNubank’s foundation\
    \ model system is designed to handle massive volumes of financial data and extract\
    \ general-purpose user representations from it. These representations, also known\
    \ as embeddings, are later used across many business applications such as credit\
    \ scoring, product recommendation, and fraud detection.\n\nThe architecture is\
    \ built around a transformer-based foundation model and is structured into several\
    \ key stages, each with a specific purpose.\n\n### 1 - Transaction Ingestion\n\
    \nThe system starts by collecting raw transaction data for each customer. This\
    \ includes information like the transaction amount, timestamp, and merchant description.\
    \ The volume is enormous, covering trillions of transactions across more than\
    \ 100 million users.\n\nEach user has a time-ordered sequence of transactions,\
    \ which is essential for modeling spending behavior over time. In addition to\
    \ transactions, other user interaction data, such as app events, can also be included.\n\
    \n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!o3JM!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2Fcefc71aa-6f72-4242-8006-0e35dc8aa70f_1600x936.png)](https://substack.com/redirect/4a93d655-9ca3-448c-b5b4-7b332c1c24ee?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \n### 2 - Embedding Interface\n\nBefore transactions can be fed into a transformer\
    \ model, they need to be converted into a format the model can understand. This\
    \ is done through a specialized encoding strategy. Rather than converting entire\
    \ transactions into text, Nubank uses a hybrid method that treats each transaction\
    \ as a structured sequence of tokens.\n\nEach transaction is broken into smaller\
    \ elements:\n\n- Amount Sign (positive or negative) is represented as a categorical\
    \ token.\n- Amount Bucket is a quantized version of the transaction amount (to\
    \ reduce numeric variance).\n- Date tokens such as month, weekday, and day of\
    \ month are also included.\n- Merchant Description is tokenized using standard\
    \ text tokenizers like Byte Pair Encoding.\n\nSee the diagram below:\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!ihmX!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2Fe0e62654-f1b8-4fb8-824d-5df21c3ab543_1600x1096.png)](https://substack.com/redirect/70602b15-6144-4820-b57f-512dbca0f4f9?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \nThis tokenized sequence preserves both the structure and semantics of the original\
    \ data, and it keeps the input length compact, which is important because attention\
    \ computation in transformers scales with the square of the input length.\n\n\
    ### 3 - Transformer Backbone\n\nOnce transactions are tokenized, they are passed\
    \ into a transformer model. Nubank uses several transformer variants for experimentation\
    \ and performance optimization.\n\nThe models are trained using self-supervised\
    \ learning, which means they do not require labeled data. Instead, they are trained\
    \ to solve tasks like:\n\n- Masked Language Modeling (MLM), where parts of the\
    \ transaction sequence are hidden and the model must predict them.\n- Next Token\
    \ Prediction (NTP), where the model learns to predict the next transaction in\
    \ the sequence.\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!3j9N!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2Fd840ca23-0b13-4457-8687-0749e66a7ee7_1600x998.png)](https://substack.com/redirect/2e6c3af4-28c1-4908-a3aa-5a8074bdfb72?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \nMore on these in later sections. The output of the transformer is a fixed-length\
    \ user embedding, usually taken from the final token's hidden state.\n\n### 4\
    \ - Self-Supervised Training\n\nThe model is trained on large-scale, unlabeled\
    \ transaction data using self-supervised learning objectives. Since no manual\
    \ labeling is required, the system can leverage the full transaction history for\
    \ each user. The models learn useful patterns about financial behavior, such as\
    \ spending cycles, recurring payments, and anomalies, by simply trying to predict\
    \ missing or future parts of a user’s transaction sequence. As a simplified example,\
    \ the model might see “Coffee, then Lunch, then…”. It tries to guess “Dinner”.\n\
    \nThe size of the training data and model parameters plays a key role. As the\
    \ model scales in size and the context window increases, performance improves\
    \ significantly. By constantly guessing and correcting itself across billions\
    \ of transactions, the model starts to notice patterns in how people spend money.\n\
    \nFor instance, switching from a basic MLM model to a large causal transformer\
    \ with optimized attention layers resulted in a performance gain of over 7 percentage\
    \ points in downstream tasks.\n\n### 5 - Downstream Fine-Tuning and Fusion\n\n\
    After the foundation model is pre-trained, it can be fine-tuned for specific tasks.\
    \ This involves adding a prediction head on top of the transformer and training\
    \ it with labeled data. For example, a credit default prediction task would use\
    \ known labels (whether a customer defaulted) to fine-tune the model.\n\nTo integrate\
    \ with existing systems, the user embedding is combined with manually engineered\
    \ tabular features. This fusion is done in two ways:\n\n- Late Fusion uses models\
    \ like LightGBM to combine embeddings and tabular data, but the two are trained\
    \ separately.\n- Joint Fusion trains the transformer and the tabular model together\
    \ in an end-to-end fashion using a deep neural network, specifically the DCNv2\
    \ architecture.\n\nMore on these in a later section.\n\n### 6 - Centralized Model\
    \ Repository\n\nTo make this architecture usable across the company, Nubank has\
    \ built a centralized AI platform.\n\nThis platform stores pretrained foundation\
    \ models and provides standardized pipelines for fine-tuning them. Internal teams\
    \ can access these models, combine them with their features, and deploy fine-tuned\
    \ versions for their specific use cases without needing to retrain everything\
    \ from scratch.\n\nThis centralization accelerates development, reduces redundancy,\
    \ and ensures that all teams benefit from improvements made to the core models.\n\
    \n## Transforming Transactions into Model-Ready Sequences\n\nTo train foundation\
    \ models on transaction data, it is critical to convert each transaction into\
    \ a format that transformer models can process.\n\nThere are two main challenges\
    \ when trying to represent transactions for use in transformer models:\n\n- **Mixed\
    \ data types:** A single transaction includes structured fields (like amount and\
    \ date) and textual fields (like the merchant name). This makes it harder to represent\
    \ consistently using either a pure text or a pure structured approach.\n- **High\
    \ cardinality and cold-start issues:** Transactions can be extremely diverse.\
    \ Even simple changes like different merchant names, locations, or amounts result\
    \ in new combinations. If each unique transaction is treated as an individual\
    \ token, the number of tokens becomes enormous. This leads to two problems:\n\n\
    \  - The embedding table grows too large to train efficiently.\n  - The model\
    \ cannot generalize to new or rare transactions it has not seen before, which\
    \ is known as the cold-start problem.\n- To address these challenges, multiple\
    \ strategies were explored for turning a transaction into a sequence of tokens\
    \ that a transformer can understand.\n\n### Approach 1: ID-Based Representation\
    \ (from Recommender Systems)\n\nIn this method, each unique transaction is assigned\
    \ a numerical ID, similar to techniques used in sequential recommendation models.\
    \ These IDs are then converted into embeddings using a lookup table.\n\nWhile\
    \ this approach is simple and efficient in terms of token length, it has two major\
    \ weaknesses:\n\n- The total number of unique transaction combinations is extremely\
    \ large, making the ID space impractical to manage.\n- If a transaction was not\
    \ seen during training, the model cannot process it effectively. This makes it\
    \ poorly suited for generalization and fails under cold-start conditions.\n\n\
    ### Approach 2: Text-Is-All-You-Need\n\nThis method treats each transaction as\
    \ a piece of natural language text. The transaction fields are converted into\
    \ strings by joining the attribute name and its value, such as \"description=NETFLIX\
    \ amount=32.40 date=2023-05-12\", and then tokenized using a standard NLP tokenizer.\n\
    \nThis representation can handle arbitrary transaction formats and unseen data,\
    \ which makes it highly generalizable.\n\nHowever, it comes at a high computational\
    \ cost.\n\nTransformers process data using self-attention, and the computational\
    \ cost of attention increases with the square of the input length. Turning structured\
    \ fields into long text sequences causes unnecessary token inflation, making training\
    \ slower and less scalable.\n\n### Approach 3: Hybrid Encoding Scheme (Chosen\
    \ by Nubank)\n\nTo balance generalization and efficiency, Nubank developed a hybrid\
    \ encoding strategy that preserves the structure of each transaction without converting\
    \ everything into full text.\n\nEach transaction is tokenized into a compact set\
    \ of discrete fields:\n\n- **Amount Sign Token:** One token represents whether\
    \ the transaction is positive (like a deposit) or negative (like a purchase).\n\
    - **Amount Bucket Token:** The absolute value of the amount is placed into a quantized\
    \ bucket, and each bucket is assigned its token. This reduces the range of numeric\
    \ values into manageable categories.\n- **Date Tokens:** Separate tokens are used\
    \ for the month, day of the month, and weekday of the transaction.\n- **Description\
    \ Tokens:** The merchant description is tokenized using a standard subword tokenizer\
    \ like Byte Pair Encoding (BPE), which breaks the text into common fragments.\
    \ This allows the model to recognize patterns in merchant names or transaction\
    \ types.\n\nBy combining these elements, a transaction is transformed into a short\
    \ and meaningful sequence of tokens. See the diagram below:\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!OxR2!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2Fef4b0a84-b6d7-4901-80dc-16c60cab34af_1600x1077.png)](https://substack.com/redirect/18322d1d-094a-4518-985a-58425db876f9?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \nThis hybrid approach retains the key structured information in a compact format\
    \ while allowing generalization to new inputs. It also avoids long text sequences,\
    \ which keeps attention computation efficient.\n\nOnce each transaction is tokenized\
    \ in this way, the full transaction history of a user can be concatenated into\
    \ a sequence and used as input to the transformer. Separator tokens are inserted\
    \ between transactions to preserve boundaries, and the sequence is truncated at\
    \ a fixed context length to stay within computational limits.\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!i8e1!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F81afa1ff-e0f9-4fcf-8ce5-22937b0b9067_1600x964.png)](https://substack.com/redirect/9ce0ea7c-c8ac-49b0-9f0d-3f5f305ecb16?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \n## Training the Foundation Models\n\nOnce transactions are converted into sequences\
    \ of tokens, the next step is to train a transformer model that can learn patterns\
    \ from this data.\n\nAs mentioned, the Nubank engineering team uses self-supervised\
    \ learning to achieve this, which means the model learns directly from the transaction\
    \ sequences without needing any manual labels. This approach allows the system\
    \ to take full advantage of the enormous volume of historical transaction data\
    \ available across millions of users.\n\nTwo main objectives are used:\n\n- **Next\
    \ Token Prediction (NTP):** The model is trained to predict the next token in\
    \ a transaction sequence based on the tokens that came before it. This teaches\
    \ the model to understand the flow and structure of transaction behavior over\
    \ time, similar to how language models predict the next word in a sentence.\n\
    - **Masked Language Modeling (MLM):** In this method, some tokens in the sequence\
    \ are randomly hidden or “masked,” and the model is trained to guess the missing\
    \ tokens. This forces the model to understand the surrounding context and learn\
    \ meaningful relationships between tokens, such as the connection between the\
    \ day of the week and spending type or between merchant names and transaction\
    \ amounts.\n\nSee the diagram below:\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!-w7o!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F92bcf49a-c2b6-4358-be46-16a291b09d42_1600x1592.png)](https://substack.com/redirect/e6f2c804-ad27-43e9-9273-5df80876df28?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \n## Blending Sequential Embeddings with Tabular Data\n\nWhile foundation models\
    \ trained on transaction sequences can capture complex behavioral patterns, many\
    \ financial systems still rely on structured tabular data for critical features.\n\
    \nFor example, information from credit bureaus, user profiles, or application\
    \ forms often comes in tabular format. To make full use of both sources (sequential\
    \ embeddings from the transformer and existing tabular features), it is important\
    \ to combine them in a way that maximizes predictive performance.\n\nThis process\
    \ of combining different data modalities is known as fusion.\n\nNubank explored\
    \ two main fusion strategies: late fusion, which is easier to implement but limited\
    \ in effectiveness, and joint fusion, which is more powerful and trains all components\
    \ together in a unified system.\n\nSee the diagram below:\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!KJPb!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2Fcc6ba7bc-7ca5-40dd-a19e-de49cda7ed43_1600x983.png)](https://substack.com/redirect/6176e0d1-eddb-4ad6-b863-eac341352188?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \n### Late Fusion (Baseline Approach)\n\nIn the late fusion setup, tabular features\
    \ are combined with the frozen embeddings produced by a pretrained foundation\
    \ model. Think of it like taking the “frozen feeling” from the pre-trained model\
    \ (embeddings) and combining it with the checklist of facts such as age, credit\
    \ score, profile details, and so on.\n\nThese combined inputs are then passed\
    \ into a traditional machine learning model, such as LightGBM or XGBoost. While\
    \ this method is simple and leverages well-established tools, it has an important\
    \ limitation.\n\nSince the foundation model is frozen and trained separately,\
    \ the embeddings do not adapt to the specific downstream task or interact meaningfully\
    \ with the tabular data during training. As a result, there is no synergy between\
    \ the two input sources, and the overall model cannot fully optimize performance.\n\
    \n### Joint Fusion (Proposed Method)\n\nTo overcome this limitation, Nubank developed\
    \ a joint fusion architecture.\n\nThis approach trains the transformer and the\
    \ tabular model together in a single end-to-end system. By doing this, the model\
    \ can learn to extract information from transaction sequences that complements\
    \ the structured tabular data, and both components are optimized for the same\
    \ prediction task.\n\nTo implement this, Nubank selected DCNv2 (Deep and Cross\
    \ Network v2) as the architecture for processing tabular features. DCNv2 is a\
    \ deep neural network specifically designed to handle structured inputs. It combines\
    \ deep layers with cross layers that capture interactions between features efficiently.\n\
    \nSee the diagram below:\n\n[![](https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!iu7B!,w_1100,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F0d7434cb-a5e1-4a06-bd89-e3775a966771_1600x980.png)](https://substack.com/redirect/0dcabd9d-999a-491a-9192-410a5e11a464?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    \n## Conclusion\n\nNubank’s initiative to use foundational models represents a\
    \ significant leap forward in how financial institutions can understand and serve\
    \ their customers. By moving away from manually engineered features and embracing\
    \ self-supervised learning on raw transaction data, Nubank has built a modeling\
    \ system that is both scalable and expressive.\n\nA key part of this success lies\
    \ in how the system has been integrated into Nubank’s broader AI infrastructure.\
    \ Rather than building isolated models for each use case, Nubank has developed\
    \ a centralized AI platform where teams can access pretrained foundation models.\
    \ These models are trained on massive volumes of user transaction data and are\
    \ stored in a shared model repository.\n\nTeams across the company can choose\
    \ between two types of models based on their needs:\n\n- Embedding-only models,\
    \ which use the user representation generated from transaction sequences.\n- Blended\
    \ models, which combine these embeddings with structured tabular features using\
    \ the joint fusion architecture.\n\nThis flexibility is critical.\n\nSome teams\
    \ may already have strong tabular models in place and can plug in the user embeddings\
    \ with minimal changes. Others may prefer to rely entirely on the transformer-based\
    \ sequence model, especially for new tasks where historical tabular features are\
    \ not yet defined.\n\nThe architecture is also forward-compatible with new data\
    \ sources. While the current models are primarily trained on transactions, the\
    \ design allows for the inclusion of other user interaction data, such as app\
    \ usage patterns, customer support chats, or browsing behavior.\n\nIn short, Nubank’s\
    \ system is not just a technical proof-of-concept. It is a production-ready solution\
    \ that delivers measurable gains across core financial prediction tasks.\n\n**References:**\n\
    \n- [Understanding Our Customer’s Finances Through Foundation Models](https://substack.com/redirect/76854868-778b-4aa4-b5be-ebe4ff082c87?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    - [Defining an Interface between Transaction Data and Foundational Models](https://substack.com/redirect/63bd17e2-6c3f-416d-b9bd-fa8756a94014?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\
    - [Fine-Tuning Transaction User Models](https://substack.com/redirect/850472c7-e74d-4381-88da-2050a9637f2e?j=eyJ1IjoiNXM4M296In0.tGNGSdtmlCx12UO5VTFY50vjzjDXKZsMTxKEYVZUdc8)\n\

    # **Big Tech & Startups**


    [**Elon Musk gives key update on plans for Tesla Diner outside of LA (3 minute
    read)**](https://www.teslarati.com/elon-musk-gives-key-update-on-plans-tesla-diner-outside-los-angeles/#google_vignette?utm_source=tldrnewsletter)


    Tesla''s Supercharger Diner in Los Angeles is now open to the public. Anyone,
    not just Tesla owners, can stop by to experience the Diner and movie theater.
    The location features 80 Superchargers, two movie screens, and a full-service
    24/7 diner that serves a wide variety of locally sourced food. Elon Musk says
    that the company plans to establish these types of experiences in major cities
    around the world, as well as at Supercharger sites on long-distance routes.


    [**Advanced version of Gemini with Deep Think officially achieves gold-medal standard
    at the International Mathematical Olympiad (4 minute read)**](https://simonwillison.net/2025/Jul/21/gemini-imo/#atom-everything?utm_source=tldrnewsletter)


    A team from Google Gemini achieved a gold medal result on this year''s International
    Mathematics Olympiad (IMO), achieving the exact same score as OpenAI: 35/42. OpenAI
    claims its model had not been optimized for IMO questions. Google''s model was
    trained with a curated corpus of high-quality solutions to mathematics problems
    and general hints and tips on how to approach IMO problems. Neither team used
    tools or internet access to help solve problems.


    # **Science & Futuristic Technology**


    [**AI Comes Up with Bizarre Physics Experiments. But They Work (11 minute read)**](https://www.quantamagazine.org/ai-comes-up-with-bizarre-physics-experiments-but-they-work-20250721/?utm_source=tldrnewsletter)


    AI hasn''t yet led to new discoveries in physics, but it''s becoming a powerful
    tool across the field. It is helping researchers to design experiments and find
    nontrivial patterns in complex data. AI has already been used to design novel
    experimental protocols that improve upon the work of human physicists. There is
    huge potential for language models to be useful in helping automate the construction
    of hypotheses.


    [**China starts building world''s biggest hydropower dam (3 minute read)**](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/jul/21/china-starts-building-world-biggest-hydropower-dam-yarlung-tsangpo-river-tibet?utm_source=tldrnewsletter)


    China has started building a hydropower megadam on the Yarlung Tsangpo River.
    The dam has drawn criticism from India, Bangladesh, Tibetan groups, and environmentalists
    - the Yarlung Tsangpo is in Tibetan territory, and it flows through India and
    Bangladesh. Damming it could affect millions of people downstream. The project
    will create five cascade hydropower stations that will produce an estimated 300
    million megawatts of electricity annually.

    [**A Friendly Introduction to SVG (17 minute read)**](https://www.joshwcomeau.com/svg/friendly-introduction-to-svg/?utm_source=tldrnewsletter)


    SVGs can be intimidating, but they can do so many cool things. This post talks
    about the most important SVG fundamentals, shows readers why SVGs are so cool,
    and shares a few tricks they can try straight away. No prior experience with SVG
    is needed for this post, but it does assume readers are familiar with web development
    fundamentals like HTML, CSS, and JavaScript. The post covers basic shapes, scalable
    SVGs, presentational attributes, and more.


    [**Pogocache (GitHub Repo)**](https://github.com/tidwall/pogocache?utm_source=tldrnewsletter)


    Pogocache is a fast caching software focused on low latency and CPU efficiency.
    It is optimized to scale to many cores, giving developers the best single-threaded
    and multithreaded performance. Pogocache minimizes server load, energy usage,
    and overall cost to operate by using the fewest CPU cycles per request. It supports
    Memcache, Valkey/Redis, HTTP, and Postgres wire protocols, allowing for the use
    of system tools and numerous client libraries.

- cleaned_md: 'Gen Alpha are shaping culture early through strong influence on family
    purchases and a growing sense of autonomy. They are spending more time offline


    # TLDR Marketing 2025-07-23


    # **News & Trends**


    [**Gen Alpha unfiltered: A deep dive into the minds, values, and behaviors of
    the youngest generation (15 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.gwi.com%2Freports%2Fgen-alpha%2Fexplore%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983707573b-e755fecb-f727-476e-9488-b8aba53eed32-000000/FR6Mk1WhOfbIruWifXhuL1J1rTLTawm9B70Y5bwbRkw=415)


    Gen Alpha are shaping culture early through strong influence on family purchases
    and a growing sense of autonomy. They are spending more time offline, favoring
    real-world activities and physical toys, and showing greater interest in collaborative
    and creative gaming like Roblox, which has doubled in use since 2021. Girls are
    aiming higher in careers like law and medicine, but fewer boys believe they can
    do anything, revealing a growing confidence gap. Social media use is increasingly
    passive, with kids scrolling more and posting less, while influencer marketing
    is overtaking traditional advertising, even for food choices. Despite not holding
    the purse strings, many Gen Alpha kids, especially 8-11-year-olds, have decision-making
    power and are already active consumers, especially in ecommerce and virtual spending.


    [**How and Why Teens Use AI Companions (15 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.commonsensemedia.org%2Fsites%2Fdefault%2Ffiles%2Fresearch%2Freport%2Ftalk-trust-and-trade-offs_2025_web.pdf%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983707573b-e755fecb-f727-476e-9488-b8aba53eed32-000000/XWANGxspSfg23cA76RlVTvHkFWOdSg91ED5Rl3RjFkY=415)


    AI companions on platforms like Character.AI, Replika, and CHAI have created new
    digital social spaces where 72% of teens have tried them for chatting, emotional
    support, role-playing, entertainment, and advice. Teens use AI companions because
    they find them entertaining, are curious about the technology, value their constant
    availability, and appreciate the nonjudgmental interaction that lets them share
    things they wouldn''t tell friends or family. Many platforms allow easy access
    for users as young as 13. However, one-third of teens report feeling uncomfortable
    with AI responses.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**5 B2B social media strategies for SaaS launches (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Fposts%2Fcarmen-vicente_how-2b2b-ugcPost-7353458107580059649-QFxG%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983707573b-e755fecb-f727-476e-9488-b8aba53eed32-000000/xUiZ02q8zR09yyzm-RHr23eCtpdihUW3PGLb5zIoXSU=415)


    The Gorgias team used 5 social tactics tailored for B2B to drive a 200% boost
    in engagement during launch week. They spotlighted the people behind the product
    to humanize AI content, diversified post formats with carousels, videos, and text
    to appeal to different preferences, and created ready-to-use assets for employees
    to amplify reach. They also lightly referenced trending content without relying
    on it, and enforced a one-week, no-links-on-LinkedIn policy to prioritize reach
    over immediate conversion.


    [**How Brands Can Use Uncertainty To Create Relevance (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fbrandingstrategyinsider.com%2Fhow-brands-can-use-uncertainty-to-create-relevance%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983707573b-e755fecb-f727-476e-9488-b8aba53eed32-000000/ma4XbK4MQjGyWL1CMNIPXebATGT7youzzi1Md1CJwRQ=415)


    Due to a growing hunger for truth and confidence, consumers are turning to brands
    that can offer credible guidance and emotional support in a time of deep uncertainty.
    Traditional networks of trust, like family, community, and journalism, have weakened,
    creating space for AI to act as a surrogate source of authority, offering recommendations
    that often sound empathetic and informed. This shift raises the importance of
    consistent brand messaging across digital environments, where large language models
    are shaping public narratives based on the content they find.


    # **Resources & Tools**


    [**Skool (Tool)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.skool.com%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983707573b-e755fecb-f727-476e-9488-b8aba53eed32-000000/gLqsBE5BEeCwZVRvFcR2LARJ3R0J-RJdlNpqBPfnT-I=415)


    Skool is a community and course platform similar to Facebook Groups but built
    for creators and coaches who want a focused, ad-free space. It combines discussion
    forums, course hosting, progress tracking, and payments in one place, without
    relying on third-party tools. Members can interact, learn, and engage without
    the distractions of social media, making it ideal for those building paid or private
    communities.


    [**Goodbye, Featured Snippets: How SERP Features Have Evolved in the AI Era (3
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fahrefs.com%2Fblog%2Fhow-serp-features-have-evolved-in-the-ai-era%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983707573b-e755fecb-f727-476e-9488-b8aba53eed32-000000/kOEuhYfEjSqFu10s51M26Flm65KLJhh6dAfq558trZ4=415)


    AI Overviews surged from 3.93% to 27.43% visibility between January and June,
    while Featured snippets dropped from 15.41% to 5.53%. Sitelinks saw the largest
    gain, rising from 8.44% to 84.95%, likely due to changes in how Google displays
    Scroll-to Sitelinks. Other features that declined sharply include Shopping, Paid
    results, and Paid Sitelinks, all dropping more than 50%. Knowledge Cards, AI Overview
    Sitelinks, and Question SERP features also increased in visibility, though less
    dramatically.


    [**Instagram tests frame-specific like counts for carousel posts (1 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.socialsamosa.com%2Fnews-2%2Finstagram-frame-specific-like-counts-carousel-posts-9518653%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983707573b-e755fecb-f727-476e-9488-b8aba53eed32-000000/MSTDNFbUS8XeXUUw3Ofx1SbjZxBkMEAqGAEZsHkN-uU=415)


    Instagram is testing a feature that shows like counts for each individual frame
    in a carousel post. The likes are tied to the frame visible when the user taps
    the like button, offering more detailed engagement insights, though not guaranteed
    to reflect frame-specific intent. This update follows Instagram''s ongoing focus
    on carousels, which tend to outperform single-image posts due to higher interaction
    and resurfacing by the algorithm.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Grab your popcorn: How movie fandom impacts buying behavior (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FKEAG7q/1/010001983707573b-e755fecb-f727-476e-9488-b8aba53eed32-000000/wf9ppx-gZ1usIxLVu5g89-umXKBG1K-SBe_i431q9CE=415)


    Movie fandom influences buying behavior by creating emotional connections that
    last beyond the initial viewing. Amazon Ads and Crowd DNA identified 5 stages
    of engagement, from pre-release excitement to long-term community involvement,
    giving brands multiple points to connect with fans. Theatergoers seek immersive
    experiences, while at-home viewers value comfort and nostalgia, often pairing
    movies with food and related products.


    [**How Kraft Heinz leans into culture to create marketing wins (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.warc.com%2Fcontent%2Ffeed%2Fhow-kraft-heinz-leans-into-culture-to-create-marketing-wins%2Fen-GB%2F10761%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983707573b-e755fecb-f727-476e-9488-b8aba53eed32-000000/yuclSQxGnHlUeDE76pQpBZj-tOSphVkzEg4qG1HscGo=415)


    Kraft Heinz stands out by hijacking cultural moments. It partners with figures
    like music producer Mustard, parodies events like the Indy 500 with hot dog cars,
    and generates billions of earned impressions. The company taps into brand, cultural,
    and consumer truths to fuel creative ideas, prioritizing organic engagement and
    fast, iterative collaboration. By listening to consumers and reacting quickly,
    such as with A1''s meme or Jet-Puffed''s egg carton packaging, it drives both
    conversation and product sellouts.
