    # TLDR Marketing 2025-07-21


    # **News & Trends**


    [**Over half of ad buyers are using generative AI for video creation: IAB (2 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.marketingdive.com%2Fnews%2Fover-half-of-ad-buyers-are-using-generative-ai-for-video-creation-iab%2F753048%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001982cb059af-0621450b-26a6-4744-b5df-6f44055f10e0-000000/sUurLJt79yq-9Ok3GNjFMMT2njC0_01NMVyX5DdpJQU=414)


    About 30% of digital video ads are created using AI. 45% of small and 42% of midsize
    brands expect to use it for nearly half their video content by 2026. Connected
    TV is also growing, with 47% of its inventory now biddable and 85% of transactions
    happening programmatically. Smaller advertisers face challenges like measurement
    issues, and most buyers agree that human involvement is still needed to customize
    CTV deals effectively.


    [**Social Media''s Massive Makeover: Reels, the Death of Trending, and LinkedIn''s
    New Look (17 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fvocal.media%2Fjournal%2Fsocial-media-s-massive-makeover-reels-the-death-of-trending-and-linked-in-s-new-look%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001982cb059af-0621450b-26a6-4744-b5df-6f44055f10e0-000000/Z30kZHonrCiE5WZH9K_J_beiUI2AXwixH_Qs2Vy9mt0=414)


    Social media is shifting with the creator economy and a new attention economy
    playbook. Creators must master short-form video like Meta''s Reels, tell fast
    stories, build niche audiences on YouTube, and create evergreen content for LinkedIn.
    AI now acts as a personal content concierge, curating feeds like a DJ tailoring
    a playlist, sorting content so users don''t face noise overload. This Agentic
    Revolution means autonomous algorithms decide what each user sees, creating highly
    personalized experiences that can both delight and isolate. Success requires agility,
    authentic engagement, and using platform-native tools to build lasting connections.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**How Codecademy Acquired 50M+ Users (10 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FkulT6c/1/010001982cb059af-0621450b-26a6-4744-b5df-6f44055f10e0-000000/9caxnnq8A0Edv266Rg7BML_pJEFXJEfX2lc0F3ZZw0Y=414)


    Codecademy''s move from free to freemium worked by identifying core user needs
    and segmenting features between free and paid tiers. The team focused on smooth
    onboarding and consistent content to build trust. Early growth tactics included
    user research, referral incentives, and clear KPIs like engagement and course
    completion. Success came from ongoing iteration, experienced hires, and community
    investment.


    [**Data in Marketing: How Brands Turn Exclusive Data Into Viral Content (4 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FadCtDo/1/010001982cb059af-0621450b-26a6-4744-b5df-6f44055f10e0-000000/ajpZ9WQkziqC8KWjaEyOklTaiV8C-_qojnzm_2HJ6wU=414)


    Brands use their internal data to create original content that sparks cultural
    conversations and builds authority. e.l.f. Beauty turned corporate board data
    into a viral campaign that challenged representation norms. OkCupid shared insights
    on dating behaviors to establish itself as an expert. Spotify''s Wrapped personalizes
    listening data for social sharing, while Grubhub links food preferences to voting
    patterns for timely political content. This strategy drives organic reach and
    media attention that competitors cannot copy.


    # **Resources & Tools**


    [**The Data Behind 7 Top Journalist Request Platforms \[New Study\] (10 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.buzzstream.com%2Fblog%2Fjournalist-request-platform-study%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001982cb059af-0621450b-26a6-4744-b5df-6f44055f10e0-000000/4ox4JU1x_Qg-QqtsHFLCs3DbMHqT4QRhshYwF0g_TKE=414)


    Press mentions are powerful for securing placement in AI search results, so journalist
    request platforms remain popular. Qwoted offers the most media requests, with
    70% of placements from DR 80+ sites. Twitter and LinkedIn share 82% of outlets,
    making monitoring both redundant. HARO has high platform overlap, but many low-quality
    requests come from sites with DR under 10. SOS provides the highest share of follow
    links at 36%, making it ideal for SEO.


    [**Writing Is the Least Interesting Thing AI Can Do for Content Strategists (5
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fcontently.com%2F2025%2F07%2F18%2Fwriting-is-the-least-interesting-thing-ai-can-do-for-content-strategists%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001982cb059af-0621450b-26a6-4744-b5df-6f44055f10e0-000000/0OAT5ITZNkFSsJfw7e_bg3mneAtoWitd9qP7lHdq614=414)


    AI''s greatest value to content strategists lies in streamlining the entire content
    lifecycle, not just writing. Tools like Brandwatch and Sprinklr detect emerging
    keywords and sentiment shifts, while predictive engines flag hidden segments and
    churn risks from CRM and behavioral data. Repurposing platforms such as Descript
    and Repurpose.io atomize webinars into video clips, resize them for each platform,
    and help maintain message consistency across the funnel.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**How Social Media Apps Use Location-Based Data and Why It Matters For Your Business
    (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmartech.zone%2Fsocial-check-ins-and-ad-targeting%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001982cb059af-0621450b-26a6-4744-b5df-6f44055f10e0-000000/AWsGFSansPBcD6asYIREDxmIVHDOiNtp6geFO2yeCQ4=414)


    Social platforms track user locations through passive signals like GPS, accelerometers,
    and metadata, even when users do not share their location explicitly. This data
    fuels powerful ad tools, including geofencing, behavioral interest targeting,
    and real-time campaign optimization. For example, a competing venue can target
    people who attended your events by serving ads to users interested in nightlife
    within a 15-mile radius. As your customers post photos, tag your location, and
    RSVP to events, their activity helps build interest graphs that competitors can
    access through ad filters.


    [**Understanding “Marketing Mix Modeling” (MMM) adoption dynamics in the industry
    (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgo.na.kantar.com%2Fl%2F934243%2F2025-07-17%2Fmvjvb%2F934243%2F1752782825zMAyGN7F%2FKantar___META_Thought_Leadership.pdf%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001982cb059af-0621450b-26a6-4744-b5df-6f44055f10e0-000000/GGXtkQAmFnZibCOJaYdXi7WV4MIzpaPUm6Dmd-eIWwk=414)


    MMM is the top choice for 34% of large advertisers when making decisions. 80%
    of MMM users apply it for both strategic planning and tactical ad spend optimization.
    Advertisers use an average of 4 measurement tools, with only 3% relying on MMM
    alone and 51% combining it with other models. Conflicting results from tools are
    common, so 55% use calibration techniques to improve accuracy. While most still
    outsource MMM, 31% now manage it in-house for transparency, customization, and
    cost savings.

    efficiency.

    Companies mistakenly equate business expertise with design skill, creating cluttered
    products that frustrate users and require excessive documentation. Investing in
    user-centered design reduces friction, boosts conversions, and lowers support
    costs.

    # TLDR Founders 2025-07-23


    # **Headlines & Trends**


    [**AI Market Clarity (9 minute read)**](https://blog.eladgil.com/p/ai-market-clarity?utm_source=tldrfounders)


    Elad Gil argues the fog has lifted. Anthropic, OpenAI, Google, Meta, and other
    giants now dominate foundation models while Harvey leads legal and Cursor rules
    coding. Customer support converges on Decagon and Sierra and Perplexity stakes
    search. Capital and compute now block new LLM entrants, yet openings remain in
    accounting, compliance, and security. The next breakout will hinge on bold go
    to market, agentic workflows, and roll‑up strategies.


    [**Figma''s IPO Isn''t Flashy — But That''s the Point (4 minute read)**](https://www.cautiousoptimism.news/p/figmas-ipo-range-is-a-little-light?utm_source=tldrfounders)


    Figma just set its IPO range at \$25–\$28 a share, valuing the company at around
    \$16B—less than Adobe once offered, but above its 2024 secondary round. It''s
    not a moonshot, but it''s solid: \$1B run rate, strong margins, and a clear growth
    story. While most coverage focuses on past performance, Figma is quietly packing
    AI features into its product, possibly adding upside for retail investors who
    still believe in narrative.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**How Claude Is Building A Unique Growth Engine Out of User-Created Apps (8 minute
    read)**](https://blog.brianbalfour.com/p/how-claude-is-building-a-unique-growth?utm_source=tldrfounders)


    Claude launched AI-powered apps with a clever twist - users pay with their own
    Claude subscription, not the creator''s. A teacher can build a SAT prep tool and
    share it with students, but each student must sign up for Claude to use it. No
    API keys, no hosting costs, no authentication headaches. The constraint becomes
    the opportunity. Each app spawns its own growth loop as project tools drive team
    invites and calculators spread through forums. While Cursor and Bolt chase developers,
    Claude went the opposite direction - maximum constraints for minimum friction,
    turning every creator into a distribution channel.


    [**This Email Strategy Changed Everything (5 minute read)**](https://trycutie.com/p/this-email-strategy-changed-everything?utm_source=tldrfounders)


    Citizen, a real time safety alerts app, was losing users after it muted push notifications.
    Julia Knight tackled the issue by hand-collecting local emergencies, dropping
    headlines into a Figma template, and blasting fifteen tailored emails daily. The
    clicks proved so strong that the team automated triggers that now send forty million
    incident emails each month, bringing dormant accounts back for free, cutting paid
    acquisition, and even lowering iterable costs through renegotiation.

    [**Anti-space (Tool)**](https://links.tldrnewsletter.com/Smgr60)


    Antispace is an AI operating system that predicts, coordinates, and executes actions

    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Six Waves of Software Pricing (9 minute read)**](https://www.mostlymetrics.com/p/the-evolution-of-pricing?utm_source=tldrfounders)


    In the 1950s, your software arrived in a semi‑truck bolted to its hardware. Seventy‑five
    years and six pricing waves later, vendors bill for shelf‑less shelfware, meter
    compute like electricity, and blend seats with usage in hybrid plans. This author
    traces the journey from boxed SKUs to SaaS, the ASP flame‑out, CFOs fighting surprise
    overages, and why clear value metrics will decide how we price AI next.


    [**The AI‑Native Enterprise Playbook (4 minute read)**](https://newsletter.angularventures.com/p/the-ai-native-enterprise-playbook?utm_source=tldrfounders)


    Now that every enterprise tool claims to be "AI-powered," what actually moves
    the needle? This playbook keeps it simple: pick a weird industry with painful,
    overlooked problems. Build for real workflows, not just demo decks. Prove your
    product works with clear, objective results, especially in edge cases. Let AI
    power more than just the product: use it across onboarding, support, sales, and
    GTM.


    [**How Carta''s internal AI agents save thousands of hours of back-and-forth work
    (9 minute read)**](https://www.firstround.com/ai/carta?utm_source=tldrfounders)


    Most teams use AI to save money. Carta used it to save time where it mattered
    most: judgment-heavy accounting tasks that bottlenecked client service. Instead
    of replacing humans, it built in-house agents that could gather context, reason
    through complex workflows, and act autonomously. One agent now handles 25,000
    monthly tasks in seconds, saving 3,500+ hours.

    # TLDR Fintech 2025-07-24


    # **News & Trends**


    [**PayPal launches “PayPal World” to connect global wallets and payment systems
    (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.prnewswire.com%2Fnews-releases%2Fintroducing-paypal-world-a-global-platform-connecting-the-worlds-largest-payment-systems-and-digital-wallets-starting-with-interoperability-to-paypal-and-venmo-302511462.html%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001983c90e474-733752e2-e751-4574-9dda-3921a525624f-000000/qFsKrabgluhQH6rad50gxgKBIkemwbtBmM9t-samMB8=415)


    PayPal World is a platform that links major payment systems and wallets, starting
    with PayPal and Venmo interoperability. Launch partners include Mercado Pago,
    UPI (NPCI), Tenpay Global, and Venmo. Representing nearly 2B users, the platform
    allows consumers to pay internationally using their domestic wallets and enables
    businesses to accept new payment options without added integrations. PayPal World
    goes live this fall, with plans for expanded wallet partnerships and future support
    for AI shopping agents and stablecoins.


    [**Goldman Sachs and BNY Mellon launch tokenized money market funds for institutional
    investors (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.cnbc.com%2F2025%2F07%2F23%2Fgoldman-sachs-bny-money-market-fund-digital-tokens.html/1/010001983c90e474-733752e2-e751-4574-9dda-3921a525624f-000000/dynyfCO0wxGwjoKOhr-mIbxgPhXr7rRq04jq41UgwQw=415)


    Goldman Sachs and BNY Mellon unveiled a platform enabling institutional clients
    to invest in tokenized money market funds, with ownership recorded on Goldman''s
    blockchain. Backed by firms like BlackRock, Fidelity, and Federated Hermes, the
    initiative targets the \$7.1T money market industry, promising faster settlement,
    24/7 trading, and greater efficiency. Unlike stablecoins, tokenized funds offer
    yield and could serve as collateral across trades, reducing frictions in traditional
    markets. BNY will maintain dual records during the transition to support adoption.


    [**UK competition authority takes on Apple over digital wallets (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.finextra.com%2Fnewsarticle%2F46338%2Fuk-competition-authority-takes-on-apple-over-digital-wallets%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001983c90e474-733752e2-e751-4574-9dda-3921a525624f-000000/2elx6O03j7gZqbxMzbgQmgsXK8boPq7i0bD2V8odWuk=415)


    The move comes as the CMA confirms that it is planning to designate both Apple
    and Google with ‘strategic market status'' in their mobile platforms, including
    operating systems, app stores, and mobile browsers. For Apple, this includes addressing
    its longstanding restrictions that prevent rivals from competing with its wallet.
    The CMA says it will focus on interoperability to take on the restrictions on
    functionality to enable UK fintechs to bring innovative digital wallets to market.


    # **Deep Dives & Reports**


    [**Penrose AccountingBench reveals frontier AI models fail real-world “closing
    the books” tasks (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fnews.ycombinator.com%2Fitem%3Fid=44637352%26utm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001983c90e474-733752e2-e751-4574-9dda-3921a525624f-000000/deOtlYE2ebhdF-xUEZcqqbMRTRnCBrB6jkLW34MKF2E=415)


    Penrose''s AccountingBench tests LLMs on accrual accounting with real SaaS financial
    data. While models like Grok 4 and Claude 4 initially match CPA baselines within
    1 percent, they degrade over time, accumulating compounding errors and even hacking
    validation checks to progress. GPT and Gemini models fail to close a single month.
    The benchmark exposes how current AI struggles with multi-step, high-stakes tasks
    where errors cascade across periods.


    [**Why Software Platforms Still Struggle to Turn Payments Into Profits (8 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.pymnts.com%2Fnews%2Fb2b-payments%2F2025%2Fwhy-software-platforms-still-struggle-to-turn-payments-into-profits%2F%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001983c90e474-733752e2-e751-4574-9dda-3921a525624f-000000/3gUTtEcEOI8zThZ1bx1v7No_54u1OGXOJef7WOHS8RU=415)


    Software companies should evaluate their payments maturity across three stages:
    enablement, customer value creation, and monetization. Moving from customer value
    creation to monetization requires specialized payments expertise, strategic integration,
    and data intelligence. Companies can generate revenue by participating in card
    economics, engaging directly in funds flow, and monetizing their platform''s network
    and payment speed as value-added services.


    [**The fintech comeback: Sheel Mohnot on why everything is fintech and what''s
    getting funded in 2025 (20 minute podcast)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ftearsheet.co%2Fpodcasts%2Fthe-fintech-comeback-sheel-mohnot-on-why-everything-is-fintech-and-whats-getting-funded-in-2025%2F%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001983c90e474-733752e2-e751-4574-9dda-3921a525624f-000000/S4PQXnfbItowxOaIkVaWv9JlGXxNKTVuekLv1jdl3pc=415)


    After a brutal two-year slump, early-stage fintech investing is rebounding—and
    Sheel Mohnot is at the center of it. As co-founder of Better Tomorrow Ventures,
    Mohnot shares how his fund is doubling down on infrastructure, embedded finance,
    and AI startups solving real workflow pain, backing over 50 companies that reflect
    the “everything is fintech” thesis.

    [**Stablecoins emerge as alternative: Amex CEO (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.paymentsdive.com%2Fnews%2Famex-stablecoins-alternative-swift-ach-payments%2F753525%2F%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001983c90e474-733752e2-e751-4574-9dda-3921a525624f-000000/8K95oGkQrOJ7bens9SvuGmdafo3cWTCglElmA2AQejY=415)


    American Express CEO Steve Squeri said stablecoins are a “good proxy” for ACH
    and Swift payments, though unlikely to fully replace them. Following the Genius
    Act''s passage, Amex is evaluating stablecoins'' role, especially for cross-border
    payments, despite them being a minor revenue driver today. Amex recently partnered
    with Coinbase for a crypto rewards card, joining Visa and Mastercard in exploring
    digital assets. Q2 revenue rose 9% year-over-year to \$17.86B, while net income
    fell 4% to \$2.89B. Analysts remain bullish, citing Gen Z/millennial engagement.


    [**Block agrees to \$12.5M settlement over Cash App spam texts in Washington (3
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.paymentsdive.com%2Fnews%2Fblock-agrees-to-125m-settlement-in-cash-app-spam-text-case%2F753829%2F%3Futm_source=tldrfintech/1/010001983c90e474-733752e2-e751-4574-9dda-3921a525624f-000000/fiunI_DhVuYxE_Iuptq5ASkpbDKMtdlt22Gi4Djih4E=415)


    Block, parent of Cash App, agreed to a \$12.5M settlement in a class action alleging
    its “Invite Friends” feature violated Washington state''s anti-spam law by enabling
    unsolicited text messages. The case, filed in 2023, claimed Cash App users sent
    referral texts without recipients'' consent. Block denies wrongdoing but settled
    to avoid further litigation. This follows earlier Cash App-related payouts, including
    \$255M to regulators in January and a \$40M NYDFS fine in April. The settlement
    applies only to Washington residents and awaits court approval.

    crisis” because artificial intelligence has advanced to the point that it can
    impersonate someone''s voice to get around security protocols and move funds.

    # TLDR DevOps 2025-07-25


    # **News & Trends**


    [**AWS Lambda announces low latency processing for Kafka events (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Faws.amazon.com%2Fabout-aws%2Fwhats-new%2F2025%2F07%2Faws-lambda-low-latency-processing-kafka-events%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/01000198414dd9ff-0de0fd4a-a0a8-4cfd-a901-c202ec918158-000000/r5fxA-fjPB8bZ8u4BkL9zZU4UR78g801fucdfJx8R68=415)


    AWS Lambda has enabled sub-100ms event processing for Amazon MSK and self-managed
    Apache Kafka in Provisioned mode by allowing the MaximumBatchingWindowInSeconds
    parameter to be set to 0. This supports real-time, latency-sensitive applications
    across industries by immediately invoking functions after each event batch, with
    average end-to-end latencies as low as 50ms.


    [**Secrets Management Tools: The Complete 2025 Guide (24 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.pulumi.com%2Fblog%2Fsecrets-management-tools-guide%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/01000198414dd9ff-0de0fd4a-a0a8-4cfd-a901-c202ec918158-000000/Thq5SfgNABbb_ZqUvGQdH6C2LdCyixMzx9uNh2XujCg=415)


    Organizations are struggling with secrets sprawl, with 96% reporting challenges
    managing credentials across code repositories and configuration files, leading
    to data breaches costing \$4.88 million on average. Pulumi ESC offers a solution
    by orchestrating existing secret stores like HashiCorp Vault and AWS Secrets Manager
    through a unified interface with configuration-as-code, dynamic credential generation,
    and comprehensive audit logging, all while reducing the need for multiple point
    solutions.


    [**npm ''accidentally'' removes Stylus package, breaks builds and pipelines (10
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.bleepingcomputer.com%2Fnews%2Fsecurity%2Fnpm-accidentally-removes-stylus-package-breaks-builds-and-pipelines%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/01000198414dd9ff-0de0fd4a-a0a8-4cfd-a901-c202ec918158-000000/pjExeHfxLzqedHNdgoWHfsHCpebl9rDx4uW150oEyxw=415)


    On July 23, npm accidentally removed the popular Stylus CSS library—used by millions
    weekly—after banning a co-maintainer''s account that had published unrelated malicious
    packages. This caused widespread build and deployment failures across major projects
    like Angular, prompting urgent workarounds from the community and an ongoing restoration
    effort by GitHub''s Trust & Safety team.

    # **Resources & Tools**


    [**SlateDB (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fslatedb%2Fslatedb%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/01000198414dd9ff-0de0fd4a-a0a8-4cfd-a901-c202ec918158-000000/Erg3C7CQEcte8rr-PPYBaDZJ4lJ1Gkt6JmwJZk4YwXw=415)


    SlateDB, a cloud-native embedded storage engine, was built on object storage like
    S3 and GCS using a log-structured merge-tree. It batches writes to mitigate high
    write API costs and uses standard LSM-tree caching techniques to mitigate read
    latency and read API costs.


    [**Transfunctions (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fpomponchik%2Ftransfunctions%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/01000198414dd9ff-0de0fd4a-a0a8-4cfd-a901-c202ec918158-000000/JMrH68qOPYywHhbzj6FJ86_adIb8zbRw6yIWfrVmI8Y=415)


    This library is designed to solve one of the most important problems in Python
    programming - dividing all written code into 2 camps: sync and async. It gets
    rid of code duplication by using templates.

    # TLDR Information Security 2025-07-25


    # **Attacks & Vulnerabilities**


    [**SonicWall Urges Admins to Patch Critical RCE Flaw in SMA 100 Devices (2 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.bleepingcomputer.com%2Fnews%2Fsecurity%2Fsonicwall-warns-of-critical-rce-flaw-in-sma-100-VPN-appliances%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/0100019841b94363-b7c81715-338c-4ff6-8f04-2eebe9dff330-000000/pFx15EpXieDohIbeMzCuIZTMtXSsmtjP9cpwBreb_vc=415)


    SonicWall is urging customers to patch Secure Mobile Access (SMA) 100 series appliances
    against a new critical authenticated arbitrary file upload vulnerability. The
    new vulnerability is caused by an unrestricted file upload weakness in the SMA
    100 series devices'' web management interface, which could allow remote attackers
    with admin privileges to upload arbitrary files and achieve RCE.


    [**Hacker Sneaks Infostealer Malware into Early Access Steam Game (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.bleepingcomputer.com%2Fnews%2Fsecurity%2Fhacker-sneaks-infostealer-malware-into-early-access-steam-game%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/0100019841b94363-b7c81715-338c-4ff6-8f04-2eebe9dff330-000000/YdrnPhEoqmsIMZFNI8P_FPNOjWpBExKo9LkpikDyhjk=415)


    A threat actor called EncryptHub compromised a game called Chemia on Steam to
    distribute infostealer malware to users. Threat intelligence company Prodaft reported
    that EncryptHub initially added a loader that downloads the Vidal infostealer
    to the game on July 22 and then also added a PowerShell script to fetch the Fickle
    Stealer malware as well. A malicious insider may have aided EncryptHub in implanting
    the malicious files in the project.


    [**Supply chain attack compromises npm packages to spread backdoor malware (3
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.csoonline.com%2Farticle%2F4028412%2Fsupply-chain-attack-compromises-npm-packages-to-spread-backdoor-malware.html%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/0100019841b94363-b7c81715-338c-4ff6-8f04-2eebe9dff330-000000/svr8Wj38M5npsLOc65qzerY1EpH-A8PWC0JFkiVK5-E=415)


    Attackers launched a "Scavenger" supply chain attack in July that hijacked popular
    npm packages, including "is" (2.8 million weekly downloads), through phishing
    from a typosquatted domain (npnjs.org). The malware installed cross-platform JavaScript
    backdoors with persistent command channels on Windows, macOS, and Linux, affecting
    users who updated to infected versions. Exploiting high-privilege maintainer accounts,
    attackers could compromise thousands of companies, with malware mostly undetected
    by antivirus solutions on VirusTotal.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**The Future of Threat Emulation: Building AI Agents that Hunt Like Cloud Adversaries
    (11 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.offensai.com%2Fblog%2Fthe-future-of-threat-emulation-building-ai-agents-that-hunt-like-cloud-adversaries%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/0100019841b94363-b7c81715-338c-4ff6-8f04-2eebe9dff330-000000/0PbBteXG69uqYaqhbMnx1JBNdKengtvpBAbTAlG9kzw=415)


    Agentic AI unlocks a powerful utility for emulating the methodology of advanced
    cloud pentesters or threat actors in a context-aware method that goes beyond traditional
    automated tooling. This post demonstrates how an agent can be provided with “tools”
    or functions that it can utilize first to enumerate the permissions a given IAM
    user has, iteratively identify privilege escalation exploits, and then use other
    tools to carry out the privilege escalation. The post also includes a scenario
    in which the agent successfully discovers the full attack chain that an adversary
    could use to launch an S3 ransomware attack.


    [**Incentives for Security: Flipping the Script (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.philvenables.com%2Fpost%2Fincentives-for-security-flipping-the-script%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/0100019841b94363-b7c81715-338c-4ff6-8f04-2eebe9dff330-000000/ePIwIKui6GqUynNqj958kJDA5TCxo7EHTUxbzyFccUY=415)


    Traditional security incentives often fail because they lack tangible business
    value. Instead, security efforts should prioritize initiatives that drive significant
    commercial benefits, like software reproducibility and inventory management, which
    can also enhance security. Organizations should make secure options more cost-effective
    than insecure ones to encourage faster adoption and modernization.


    [**How Anthropic teams use Claude Code (16 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.anthropic.com%2Fnews%2Fhow-anthropic-teams-use-claude-code%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/0100019841b94363-b7c81715-338c-4ff6-8f04-2eebe9dff330-000000/2t8h47mpw59veemVwZit02_QGgnZKU7lZ6ZrLlnoACw=415)


    This case study demonstrates how Claude Code accelerates security reviews and
    incident responses, reducing debugging time from 15 minutes to 5 minutes and eliminating
    Terraform approval bottlenecks. It enables new hires to contribute within days,
    rather than weeks, by navigating codebases and understanding systems. The Data
    Infrastructure team notes that Claude Code replaces traditional data catalogs,
    allowing new data scientists to quickly grasp dependencies and work independently.


    # **Launches & Tools**


    [**TrollBlacklistDLL (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fcybersectroll%2FTrollBlacklistDLL%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/0100019841b94363-b7c81715-338c-4ff6-8f04-2eebe9dff330-000000/ZtEhKOxsupu7UmN11taq-BzBhxqXTUTjO-0gf92i2EE=415)


    TrollBlacklistDLL is a tool that blocks DLLs in blacklist.txt from loading, with
    an option to unblock them subsequently.


    [**s3grep (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fdacort%2Fs3grep%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/0100019841b94363-b7c81715-338c-4ff6-8f04-2eebe9dff330-000000/RY2VqiquZC3O9Dzf7wJDA6-34eaBI8p68XEegP-fXY8=415)


    s3grep is a parallel CLI tool designed for searching logs and unstructured data
    within Amazon S3 buckets. It features .gz decompression, progress indicators,
    and reliable error handling, making it perfect for cloud-native log analysis.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Amazon Q: Now with Helpful AI-Powered Self-Destruct Capabilities (4 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.lastweekinaws.com%2Fblog%2Famazon-q-now-with-helpful-ai-powered-self-destruct-capabilities%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/0100019841b94363-b7c81715-338c-4ff6-8f04-2eebe9dff330-000000/BhBlO0ePh1kpV_mHFcszTjokNYM2QgR-Ilck5ga6CBE=415)


    404Media released a report on Wednesday that a hacker had managed to get a PR
    that instructed Amazon Q to erase all local files and cloud infrastructure merged
    to the Amazon Q Developer extension for VS Code. Amazon quickly removed the compromised
    versions and released a statement that the hacker had been removed from the project
    and no customers had been impacted. Corey Quinn lambasts Amazon''s response in
    this post, highlighting the illegitimacy of its response and the erosion of trust
    that it implies.


    [**Phishers Target Aviation Execs to Scam Customers (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fkrebsonsecurity.com%2F2025%2F07%2Fphishers-target-aviation-execs-to-scam-customers%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/0100019841b94363-b7c81715-338c-4ff6-8f04-2eebe9dff330-000000/-9lm6lDgMhMoARMLExn78Z9DzueKls3Oly2EO-8blLQ=415)


    A Nigerian cybercrime group, known as "SilverTerrier," targets aviation and transportation
    executives by phishing emails to hijack emails and create lookalike domains for
    fake invoices, resulting in at least one victim losing six figures. Researchers
    have linked hundreds of phishing domains to the group since 2012, based on registration
    patterns, which contributed to part of the $2.8 billion in BEC losses reported
    last year. Companies have a 66% chance of recovering funds if they report to ic3.gov
    within 72 hours via the Financial Fraud Kill Chain, but most victims are unaware
    of this.


    [**Illusory Wishes: China-nexus APT Targets the Tibetan Community (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.zscaler.com%2Fblogs%2Fsecurity-research%2Fillusory-wishes-china-nexus-apt-targets-tibetan-community%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/0100019841b94363-b7c81715-338c-4ff6-8f04-2eebe9dff330-000000/eDXHYvv17sBWV9XEmibhogmThvn9ReC-QoEmzZGS1Hc=415)


    A China-linked Advanced Persistent Threat (APT) group launched "Operation GhostChat,"
    targeting the Tibetan community by compromising legitimate websites and replacing
    them with malicious replicas that offer a backdoored version of the Element encrypted
    messaging app. The attack employs techniques such as DLL sideloading, multi-stage
    shellcode injection, and a custom Ghost RAT that communicates with C2 servers
    via encrypted traffic. The malware evades detection through API hooking bypasses,
    memory-based code injection into legitimate Windows processes, and XOR-encoded
    plugin DLLs, which provide keylogging, screen capture, and remote shell access.

    # TLDR Information Security 2025-07-23


    # **Attacks & Vulnerabilities**


    [**ExpressVPN Bug Leaked User IPs in Remote Desktop Sessions (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.bleepingcomputer.com%2Fnews%2Fsecurity%2Fexpressvpn-bug-leaked-user-ips-in-remote-desktop-sessions%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983772eebe-96df9299-4089-4754-bc8e-1c28a63f1980-000000/_mbxsApL5CCCJFX1SCEdaMH7UWZlJqY4ImZeienMvws=415)


    A security researcher reported a vulnerability in ExpressVPN''s Windows client
    that caused Remote Desktop Protocol (RDP) traffic to bypass the VPN, which could
    lead to exposing the user''s IP. ExpressVPN patched the bug, confirmed that it
    only impacted RDP traffic, and stated that it was introduced by debug code that
    was accidentally included in production builds.


    [**Hong Kong Investigates Louis Vuitton Data Leak Affecting 419K Customers (2
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FOmhNMW/1/010001983772eebe-96df9299-4089-4754-bc8e-1c28a63f1980-000000/EQCgxyd88-M-Dli6DxLfFwMRZiHvlQdtIS-Rjpm9zR0=415)


    Hong Kong''s privacy watchdog announced that it is investigating a data leak affecting
    419,000 customers of the Hong Kong branch of Louis Vuitton. The leaked data may
    have included names, phone numbers, passport details, addresses, email addresses,
    shopping history, and product preferences, but did not include payment information.


    [**Coyote Trojan First to Use Microsoft UI Automation in Bank Attacks (3 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fhackread.com%2Fcoyote-trojan-use-microsoft-ui-automation-bank-attacks%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983772eebe-96df9299-4089-4754-bc8e-1c28a63f1980-000000/L4Vat0c8y2EBAISyTblX3SrKNhUSbDsBr3iFeycUSWQ=415)


    The Coyote banking Trojan is notable for being the first malware to utilize Microsoft''s
    UI Automation (UIA) framework, transitioning from a proof-of-concept to actively
    targeting Brazilian banking and cryptocurrency users. It exploits UIA to steal
    credentials from browsers and can manipulate UI elements, such as address bars,
    to redirect victims to phishing sites, thereby complicating detection efforts.
    Akamai recommends monitoring for the presence of UIAutomationCore.dll in unknown
    processes and scanning for interactions with UIA named pipes as early indicators
    of infection.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**The Cyber Deception Maturity Model: Where Does Your Organization Stand? (19
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdeceptiq.com%2Fblog%2Fcyber-deception-maturity-model%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983772eebe-96df9299-4089-4754-bc8e-1c28a63f1980-000000/ziHGY9IURFZCwakEwX4phdx8QJYv8RSw44gLLmmuqVI=415)


    This post divides cyber deception into 5 levels: pre-deception, where an organization
    does not employ cyber deception; experimental, where an organization deploys simple
    deception that only succeeds at catching automated scanners; operational, where
    an organization can catch human threats; strategic, where an organization''s deception
    resources mimic authentic resources and mimic high-value targets; and optimized,
    where deception goes beyond detection and shapes adversary behavior. Each level
    includes key metrics to track as well as steps to advance to the next level.


    [**Cloud Logging for Security and Beyond (14 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Funit42.paloaltonetworks.com%2Fcloud-logging-for-security%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983772eebe-96df9299-4089-4754-bc8e-1c28a63f1980-000000/vKKfUTIvJFE0HkbR6YrbrFlQm9MtpyaobjccW8kYhFM=415)


    This is a guide on cloud logging best practices for AWS, Azure, and Google Cloud.
    It emphasizes the importance of balancing security, compliance, and cost when
    selecting logging strategies. The guide distinguishes between control plane logging
    (default for management) and data plane logging (which requires manual activation
    for service activities), categorizing logs into audit, compute, network, secrets,
    storage, database, and Kubernetes types. Organizations should prioritize logging
    based on business, regulatory, and security needs, avoiding the costly "log everything"
    approach.


    [**Common mistakes in using CVSS (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.kaspersky.com%2Fblog%2Fcvss-rbvm-vulnerability-management%2F53912%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983772eebe-96df9299-4089-4754-bc8e-1c28a63f1980-000000/Z8PuLs6Ixt-CfyY88pnsPrqnDtccfDWdkH5RvQoaB4U=415)


    Don''t rely solely on CVSS scores for prioritizing vulnerabilities, as only 17%
    of critical ones are exploited, while attackers target lower scores. Organizations
    should implement Risk-Based Vulnerability Management (RBVM) that includes threat
    intelligence, asset importance, business context, and metrics like EPSS. Research
    shows EPSS prioritization targets 3% of vulnerabilities with 65% effectiveness,
    unlike CVSS, which requires 57% coverage for similar results, with only 4% effectiveness.


    # **Launches & Tools**


    [**JSON Crack (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2FAykutSarac%2Fjsoncrack.com%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983772eebe-96df9299-4089-4754-bc8e-1c28a63f1980-000000/CR7T4c3XZ6AYaMnZGsT8009nYwqPRt59myxsbTGk16g=415)


    JSON Crack is a visualization application that transforms various data formats
    (JSON, CSV, XML, etc) into interactive graphs.


    [**Flowable''s Summer 2025 Update Introduces Groundbreaking Agentic AI Capabilities

    Flowable released version 2025.1 on July 22 with AI capabilities, including four
    agent types: Utility, Document, Knowledge, and Orchestrator. It now supports integrations
    with AWS Bedrock, Azure Foundry, and Salesforce Agentforce, and features dynamic
    autonomy for agents switching between AI help and deterministic workflows based
    on task complexity. The enterprise ''AI button'' enables real-time summaries,
    automated customer communication, and autonomous task completion.


    [**WAF Detector (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fammarion%2Fwaf-detector%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/010001983772eebe-96df9299-4089-4754-bc8e-1c28a63f1980-000000/xkpuRnS1H0NGM2f0r6Z96oijigdtWFk5sJ4n1vudKoc=415)


    WAF Detector is a fast Rust tool that detects and tests web firewalls and CDNs.
    It works with CloudFlare, AWS WAF, Akamai, Fastly, and Vercel.

    budget cuts to CISA and expired threat hunting contracts.

    # TLDR Information Security 2025-07-22


    # **Attacks & Vulnerabilities**


    [**Indian crypto exchange CoinDCX confirms \$44M stolen during hack (2 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ftechcrunch.com%2F2025%2F07%2F21%2Findian-crypto-exchange-coindcx-confirms-44-million-stolen-during-hack%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/y78xoVt-dWHms9Y16W5ImJrID_7Tis-rLslnIykR1u0=414)


    CoinDCX, India''s largest cryptocurrency exchange, suffered a security breach
    in which hackers stole \$44.2 million from an internal operational account used
    for liquidity provisioning. The stolen funds were converted to Ethereum and Solana
    tokens. Thankfully, customer funds remained unaffected as operational accounts
    are segregated from user wallets.


    [**750,000 Impacted by Data Breach at The Alcohol & Drug Testing Service (2 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.securityweek.com%2F750000-impacted-by-data-breach-at-the-alcohol-drug-testing-service%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/LyNXliYEQWa6XhNpQKekxxUriM0-9JKBhozyFJgKx9E=414)


    The Alcohol & Drug Testing Service has disclosed a July 2024 data breach affecting
    750,000 people. Hackers accessed personal information, including Social Security
    numbers, driver''s licenses, financial data, and biometric information. The BianLian
    ransomware group has claimed responsibility, allegedly stealing 218GB of data.


    [**Microsoft Fix Targets Attacks on SharePoint Zero-Day (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fkrebsonsecurity.com%2F2025%2F07%2Fmicrosoft-fix-targets-attacks-on-sharepoint-zero-day%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/bkbGaTNGFb0bY5UPRzctyr5rANmbCQW4xTsA54hdi60=414)


    Microsoft has issued an emergency patch for a SharePoint Server vulnerability,
    CVE-2025-53770, which is actively being exploited by hackers targeting U.S. federal
    agencies, universities, and energy companies. CISA warns organizations to patch
    immediately and rotate ASP.NET machine keys, as patching alone is insufficient
    for protection.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**Why You Should Be Testing Your Detection Rules (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fv22bis.medium.com%2Fwhy-you-should-be-testing-your-detection-rules-part-1-ab6f74fc5116%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/Gn8jyUYNqadQtzzx-eib_YIZAxgX9f4NBYIiWtSrZp8=414)


    Conducting detection engineering rules testing helps identify bugs early in the
    pipeline and enables the development of higher-quality rules more quickly. These
    tests can be categorized into unit testing/linting, where individual functions
    are verified and style standards are maintained; integration testing, which assesses
    all components of the pipeline; and end-to-end testing, where an event is triggered
    in production to observe the rule''s behavior. Beginning with unit testing/linting
    and integration testing allows teams to gain the majority of testing benefits
    without the need to maintain complex testing environments.


    [**Novel SSRF Technique Involving HTTP Redirect Loops (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fslcyber.io%2Fassetnote-security-research-center%2Fnovel-ssrf-technique-involving-http-redirect-loops%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/gOBUHVKqal4UWp8Ou9YUkEbEaMgbjs9qylHUzym8Lo0=414)


    While testing an enterprise application for SSRF vulnerabilities, the authors
    of this post discovered a new technique that allowed them to retrieve the complete
    request chain. The attack involved utilizing a redirect loop that returned HTTP
    responses between 300 and 310 before redirecting to the final SSRF location. It
    was found that the application responded with a 200 status, allowing the entire
    chain to be executed, and thus enabling them to exfiltrate cloud credentials.


    [**MalDev Myths (7 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fblog.deeb.ch%2Fposts%2Fmaldev-myths%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/u_lJc6TLlyAAvLL8X_zRvVLwnI4WlPgOKzf-fMWI0dQ=414)


    This post enumerates a series of common myths in malware development and observed
    realities. It begins with discussing where to store payloads, details related
    to choosing an encryption method and entropy, code obfuscation, and various unhooking
    mechanisms. It then compares some sample shellcode loaders against these myths
    and proposes an idealized loader architecture.


    # **Launches & Tools**


    [**Network Security Microsegmentation: Free Resources by Gartner and Akamai**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.akamai.com%2Flp%2Fgartner-microsegmentation-guide%3Futm_source=tldr%26utm_medium=email%26utm_campaign=f-mc-67958%26utm_id=global_zt%26utm_term=inquire%26utm_content=segmentation/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/Y-x87tffsY_hiSM118QK9X-4Eo67bR6HL2vkXODfG9s=414)

    microsegmentation for each workload level. Learn how to implement this strategy
    with [Akamai''s free guide](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.akamai.com%2Fresources%2Fwhite-paper%2Fclearing-the-path-to-microsegmentation-strategy-guide%3Futm_source=tldr%26utm_medium=email%26utm_campaign=f-mc-67958%26utm_id=global_zt%26utm_term=consider%26utm_content=segmentation/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/tMkQXocI0qsfFVUQ3xPzWkgF3-LIt7YERoJoPick-WQ=414);
    then, look at the key features, use cases, and vendors in this space with a free

    [**Empirical Security (Product Launch)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.empiricalsecurity.com%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/oRMr4wTcR_ctECLtDng1ZX1dmpHMDS_Jx5gikPnWP9E=414)


    Empirical provides custom data-driven AI models to help organizations secure their
    environments against the exploitation of vulnerabilities.


    [**SecureMCP (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fmakalin%2FSecureMCP%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/op2h_Gb_WQNFc1_E2ex1JprjYJckgqRcr6XxRd3S3YM=414)


    SecureMCP is a comprehensive security auditing tool designed to detect vulnerabilities
    and misconfigurations in applications using the Model Context Protocol (MCP).
    It proactively identifies threats like OAuth token leakage, prompt injection vulnerabilities,
    rogue MCP servers, and tool poisoning attacks.


    [**Device Offboarding Manager (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fugurkocde%2FDeviceOffboardingManager%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/LRdMRXHWIvw-43Ps_WYxgL9VUUdBWjPA2R6Uwwey1AQ=414)

    [**Stellar Blade''s X Account Hacked to Promote Fake Tokens (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FoyjCLW/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/S_og-0gCIm-dWE0lQqN38ms34pmiwOrjBBL8d5AgMBs=414)


    Popular video game Stellar Blade''s X account was hacked and used to promote a
    cryptocurrency that was supposedly associated with the game. The hackers prompted
    users to click on a link to receive tokens from a limited-time airdrop. The game''s
    director has urged users to avoid interacting with these posts as they work to
    recover the account.


    [**Introducing OSS Rebuild: Open Source, Rebuilt to Last (5 minute read)**](http://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/http:%2F%2Fsecurity.googleblog.com%2F2025%2F07%2Fintroducing-oss-rebuild-open-source.html%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/LRcWlQXwJKcQBkNgPYoER9FS1KkVi-Mf66spJnW_m1o=414)


    Google launched OSS Rebuild, a project that automatically rebuilds popular Python,
    JavaScript, and Rust packages to verify their integrity against published source
    code. The system generates SLSA Build Level 3 provenance attestations for thousands
    of packages, enabling security teams to detect supply chain attacks, including
    unsubmitted source code, build environment compromises, and backdoors, without
    requiring maintainer intervention. Organizations can use the tool to enhance their
    existing vulnerability management workflows or run their rebuild instances to
    strengthen open-source supply chain security.


    [**Researchers Uncover Secretive Russian Spy Unit by Studying Its Commemorative
    Badges (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fintelnews.org%2F2025%2F07%2F21%2F01-3406%2F%3Futm_source=tldrinfosec/1/01000198324621d1-7b6d9760-b60c-4dc4-9cc6-34fbd7e84a38-000000/0rJcb0kSOce3J34uHSodO00Nv1RN6e04Ui5nfBvo7II=414)


    CheckFirst, a Finnish cybersecurity firm specializing in OSINT, has managed to
    outline the structures of the elusive Russian Center 16. CheckFirst researchers
    studied online listings for commemorative challenge coins issued to Center 16
    and were able to identify 10 distinct directorates, an increase from the previous
    1 unique directorate. CheckFirst also managed to partially map out the geographic
    structure of Center 16.

    # TLDR Marketing 2025-07-24


    # **News & Trends**


    [**The rise of the Narrow Startup (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fa16z.com%2Fnarrow-startups%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983c219703-d52f1d0f-d422-4230-aa51-539871044983-000000/qKrYKqChHjc5W-TowGyzf4iugPRBVJIhFVbEz6HoYI0=415)


    Consumer software is shifting from mass-market, ad-supported models to high-priced,
    hyper-focused products known as Narrow Startups. These apps serve specific user
    groups such as engineers, developers, or creatives through premium \$200 per month
    tiers that exist within broader platforms. Instead of scaling to millions, these
    startups thrive with small, dedicated user bases by delivering deep value for
    niche needs.


    [**For Retail and Delivery, Advertising is Becoming Big Business (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ffoodinstitute.com%2Ffocus%2Ffor-retail-and-delivery-advertising-is-becoming-big-business%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983c219703-d52f1d0f-d422-4230-aa51-539871044983-000000/qDBfI00dad_EhxUO4fPzUtONty7MuVDeGlCV3EouqjE=415)


    Retail and delivery ad revenues now exceed 10 billion dollars annually and are
    growing near 20%. Platforms such as DoorDash and Instacart are using first-party
    data and AI to offer more targeted advertising to thousands of brands and merchants.
    Profit contributions from media are helping major players offset costs and stay
    competitive.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**Win Report: 13% increase in sales with a simple change to a product page (2
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fconversion-rate-experts.com%2Fhouse-of-worktops-delivery-info-box-win-report%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983c219703-d52f1d0f-d422-4230-aa51-539871044983-000000/e_umuiqdu6YR0___zEsU5IiOotLQs0dh6GC4Es4QqMw=415)


    House of Worktops increased sales by 13% and revenue by 24% by changing how it
    presented its delivery checker on product pages. The original form sat above the
    main call-to-action and caused distraction during a key decision moment. Replacing
    the form with a simple clickable link reduced cognitive load while keeping the
    feature accessible. The change made the page cleaner and helped more users move
    forward without unnecessary friction.


    [**The ROI of Email Marketing (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.litmus.com%2Fblog%2Finfographic-the-roi-of-email-marketing%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983c219703-d52f1d0f-d422-4230-aa51-539871044983-000000/Dt3t6u5Vdeh6ZuER5tU5gqPzyIeQvVvCETMXaBUH73U=415)


    Email marketing delivers strong ROI, with 35% of companies earning \$10 to \$36
    for every \$1 spent and 30% earning between \$36 and \$50. Customer engagement
    emails, promotional emails, and newsletters generate the highest returns depending
    on the industry. Retail sees the highest ROI at 45:1, followed by marketing agencies
    at 42:1 and tech at 36:1. Companies measure email impact using metrics like customer
    engagement (59%), conversion rates or MQLs (44%), and direct revenue attribution
    (41%). To improve ROI, marketers should run A/B tests, use personalized and interactive
    content, and leverage analytics tools and pre-send testing.


    # **Resources & Tools**


    [**Unlock next level Shorts with new creation tools (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fblog.youtube%2Fnews-and-events%2Fnew-shorts-creation-tools-2025%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983c219703-d52f1d0f-d422-4230-aa51-539871044983-000000/zuh9ERL1sRhsZ8gF1o2jtHH4yAAY6GSFTxZuhRGLbfI=415)


    YouTube Shorts has introduced new AI-powered tools to simplify content creation.
    The Photo to video feature turns images into animated videos and is available
    for free in the US, Canada, Australia, and New Zealand. New generative effects
    let users transform doodles and selfies into dynamic videos and are accessible
    through the Shorts camera. The AI playground offers pre-filled prompts and creation
    tools for videos, images, and music, all marked with SynthID watermarks to indicate
    AI use.


    [**Unicorn (Tool)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.unicorn.studio%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983c219703-d52f1d0f-d422-4230-aa51-539871044983-000000/RlX_iu5Ds6G_L7VyZPS56-2OWCBdpzdfqvhGIgUNUWY=415)


    Unicorn Studio lets users build interactive web experiences using WebGL technology.
    It offers over 60 customizable effects to add motion and interactivity to images,
    videos, and text without coding. Lightweight and performance-optimized, users
    can export creations as images, videos, or code snippets and easily embed them
    into platforms like Framer, Webflow, and Wix.


    [**Is RRF the Secret to Dominating AI Citations? I Decoded ChatGPT''s Ranking
    Formula (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmetehan.ai%2Fblog%2Fchatgpt-is-using-reciprocal-rank-fusion-rrf%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983c219703-d52f1d0f-d422-4230-aa51-539871044983-000000/rnEz_vp6t3BHFCrxzeDK9mUWTt23Ci7HRe2AhoD7O44=415)


    Reciprocal Rank Fusion (RRF) is an information retrieval method that combines
    scores from multiple related searches into a final ranking. It rewards pages that
    consistently rank across many queries, showing that topical authority and comprehensive
    coverage outperform narrow keyword targeting. Analysis of ChatGPT''s code confirms
    it uses RRF, explaining how AI evaluates relevance across variations of user intent.
    This shows why SEO remains essential and why building topic clusters matters.
    Consistent visibility across related topics will outperform isolated top rankings.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Attention Is the Last Scarce Resource (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.digitalnative.tech%2Fp%2Fattention-is-the-last-scarce-resource%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983c219703-d52f1d0f-d422-4230-aa51-539871044983-000000/iZGvCorgPa-C1O9IZcOPROS6VdxMs7WU1tmkVbkHEmo=415)


    Attention is becoming the most valuable and limited resource in the digital economy.
    Platforms like TikTok now dominate consumer behavior, with Gen Z spending 108
    minutes per day on the app, contributing to declining interest in traditional
    media like The Late Show. As AI-generated video and real-time tools like Mirage
    flood the internet with content, attention spans shrink, and the cost of capturing
    attention rises. To adapt, companies are expanding into new attention-friendly
    mediums like voice and using new business models such as subscriptions and microtransactions
    to extract more value per user.


    [**Can my niece design a better poster than your creative agency? (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.marketingweek.com%2Fooh-distinctive-brand-assets%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/010001983c219703-d52f1d0f-d422-4230-aa51-539871044983-000000/tZWJycEZsYO73v9GvIK7DUH75l1lpDFHFLKEs_8WK_M=415)


    Effective poster design follows two simple rules: use distinctive brand elements
    that light and non-brand buyers recognize, and make those brand signals large
    enough to be seen, especially by viewers passing quickly. Many praised minimalist
    outdoor ads succeed only because they get these basics right, while others fail
    by making branding unclear or too small. Research shows strong brand presence
    greatly improves recall. Simple, clear branding wins in limited attention environments,
    proving fundamentals matter more than complex creativity.

    # TLDR Crypto 2025-07-22


    # **Markets & Business**


    [**GENIUS Act is helping Ethereum have its moment (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FhjukNe/1/01000198321370ef-1f4612bc-efb7-4cf6-b6b1-a84fbcb59022-000000/pbO-IjzDPYfEWk8sBd7K-EJ1MU1MD8IZkDyjIEQ2e3k=414)


    Ethereum is "having its moment" following President Trump''s signing of the GENIUS
    Act, which legalizes fully-backed stablecoins and cements ETH''s role as their
    primary settlement rail. ETH is up ~45% in two weeks, sparked by surging ETF inflows,
    increased institutional portfolio allocation, and fintech demand for operational
    ETH. This is a structural "blockchain financial services cycle," not a boom-bust
    crypto phase, with Ethereum positioned as core infrastructure for stablecoins,
    tokenized assets, and real-world adoption.


    [**Crypto Investment Funds See Record \$4.4B Weekly Inflows (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FxjCaTw/1/01000198321370ef-1f4612bc-efb7-4cf6-b6b1-a84fbcb59022-000000/-7__VvnYo-UBX_v_BBy1nMTfIl0p6FQBDm3EFB5bgdM=414)


    Crypto investment products saw record inflows of \$4.39 billion last week, the
    highest weekly figure ever recorded by CoinShares, pushing 2025''s year-to-date
    total to \$27 billion. Ethereum led the increase with \$2.12 billion of inflows,
    its 13th straight week of gains, outpacing Bitcoin''s \$2.2 billion and setting
    a new personal weekly record. U.S. funds dominated with \$4.36 billion in flows,
    while altcoins like Solana, XRP, and Sui also saw notable inflows, underscoring
    widening investor risk appetite across the sector.


    # **Innovation & Launches**


    [**Aave Greenlights White-Label Lending Platform on Ink L2 (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FcQUI67/1/01000198321370ef-1f4612bc-efb7-4cf6-b6b1-a84fbcb59022-000000/RGC0vi46ZG3wPtZEXDF7q2TBblxQC-EvuAiAmcOmwcI=414)


    Aave DAO has approved the Kraken-backed Ink Foundation to launch a rebranded,
    white-label version of Aave V3 on the Ink Layer 2 chain. The vote passed overwhelmingly,
    with 99.8% in favor, enabling Aave to enter the institutional lending space while
    Ink commits to driving over \$250 million in initial liquidity through liquidity
    mining programs. In return, Aave will receive at least 5% of the interest on the
    borrow volume as revenue and gain exclusivity over Ink''s lending integrations
    for 12 months.

    The passage of three major crypto bills within 24 hours – the GENIUS Act, CLARITY
    Act, and Anti-CBDC Bill – represents the most consequential moment in financial
    services law since Dodd-Frank in 2010, setting the stage for the biggest transformation
    in financial technology since the 1970s digitization era. The GENIUS Act creates
    an entirely new category of financial institution for regulated USD-backed stablecoins,
    while the CLARITY Act clarifies SEC vs CFTC oversight and enables tokenized securities,
    collectively unleashing adoption by banks and Fortune 500 companies. When assets
    are "wrapped" in this new technology, they become default global, instant/24-7,
    and programmable, replacing today''s locked and closed systems. Major banks like
    JPMorgan, Bank of America, and Citi are already positioning themselves to capitalize
    on both the threat and opportunity.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**The Altcoin Treasury Playbook (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fthreadreaderapp.com%2Fthread%2F1947230359126487250.html%3Futm_source=tldrcrypto/1/01000198321370ef-1f4612bc-efb7-4cf6-b6b1-a84fbcb59022-000000/KHRMrIh8XlWjYlpjUwyYI-QJgr8qCXj7mkjkcOVulG0=414)


    A common altcoin treasury scheme involves micro-cap public companies raising large
    sums from insiders to buy locked altcoins, which are then marketed as treasury
    assets. The low-float stock pumps on the news, allowing early investors to ride
    a near risk-free trade backed by the underlying asset''s NAV. Retail often buys
    at inflated valuations, unaware that insiders may be unloading months later when
    lockups expire, a cycle repeated across multiple tickers during bullish conditions.


    [**Late-Cycle Market Strategy (60 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2FAqvCW8/1/01000198321370ef-1f4612bc-efb7-4cf6-b6b1-a84fbcb59022-000000/P7RKUgrG2MWJKtNCID6tlDWhsh3__mqj_Pb2VXaN0U4=414)


    A recent analysis explored a late-cycle investment strategy that draws parallels
    between market tops and poker tournament endgames, advocating for a "push/fold"
    approach where investors protect the bulk of their capital by cashing out while
    concentrating remaining exposure into selective, high-conviction bets. The strategy,
    grounded in Nash equilibrium game theory, aims to counter typical behavioral biases
    like FOMO and greed that lead investors to remain overexposed at cycle peaks,
    with historical examples from the dot-com bubble and 2008 financial crisis validating
    this capital preservation approach. Investors can avoid catastrophic losses during
    market downturns while retaining upside potential by reducing overall exposure
    while maintaining limited participation through calculated high-risk positions.

    [**Async I/O on Linux and durability (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fblog.canoozie.net%2Fasync-i-o-on-linux-and-durability%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/010001982cbdcab1-734de91f-cf3a-4d32-ac55-9735f226d1b4-000000/ImUnwo8Thu9zmBBKJcEgL6mO4jPBlFZhtIzDMGTS6Ug=414)


    Leveraging Linux''s io_uring for asynchronous I/O enables parallel, batched writes
    that significantly boost database performance. A dual write-ahead log (WAL) design—separating
    intent and completion records—preserves durability guarantees while achieving
    a 10x improvement in throughput over traditional synchronous methods.


    [**Automated Kubernetes Threat Detection with Tetragon and Azure Sentinel (13

    After implementing a PHP-FPM exporter in a Kubernetes cluster, an engineer noticed
    that most apps had 99% idle processes, indicating over-provisioning due to a widely
    used default configuration file (www.conf). By creating a \`php-fpm-advisor.sh\`
    script and adjusting the PHP-FPM configuration to better suit the application''s
    traffic patterns, they optimized resource allocation without sacrificing performance,
    especially benefiting applications with 20 or more pods.

    [**How we tracked down a Go 1.24 memory regression across hundreds of pods (9
    minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.datadoghq.com%2Fblog%2Fengineering%2Fgo-memory-regression%2F%3Futm_source=tldrdevops/1/010001982cbdcab1-734de91f-cf3a-4d32-ac55-9735f226d1b4-000000/M047DhQlIHl5UhOFQRaPgLn0xt9P27TfPCuMCLmBo3k=414)


    Datadog observed a ~20% increase in memory usage after upgrading to Go 1.24, traced
    to a regression in the mallocgc allocator, where large pointer-heavy allocations
    caused more virtual memory to be committed to physical RAM, even though Go''s
    internal metrics remained stable. Collaborating with the Go community, it pinpointed
    the issue, validated a fix to be included in Go 1.25, and found that Go 1.24''s
    Swiss Tables ultimately reduced memory usage in high-traffic environments, delivering
    a net win.

    # TLDR Web Dev 2025-07-22


    # **Articles & Tutorials**


    [**Three.js Instances: Rendering Multiple Objects Simultaneously (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Ftympanus.net%2Fcodrops%2F2025%2F07%2F10%2Fthree-js-instances-rendering-multiple-objects-simultaneously%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/0100019831dfc1eb-bd39c1dd-417a-49bb-9b31-604f15c01279-000000/qnQtDTEMufL30H4M7vffxgnpshMdc194onEtsn3iZjc=414)


    Three.js instancing can be used to render multiple 3D objects efficiently without
    compromising performance. Instancing allows objects that share the same geometry
    and material to be rendered simultaneously in a single draw call, reducing GPU
    calls from thousands to just one or two. This article goes over basic instancing
    with React Three Fiber using the `Instances` component, creating multiple instance
    sets with `createInstances()`, and implementing custom shaders for instanced objects,
    showing how to render thousands of objects like a forest scene or animated blobs.


    [**We Made Postgres Writes Faster, but it Broke Replication (10 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.paradedb.com%2Fblog%2Flsm_trees_in_postgres%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/0100019831dfc1eb-bd39c1dd-417a-49bb-9b31-604f15c01279-000000/nw-pIFKQvMoFTyASsj0Xe025uNZuQHsw8Umlt36dXug=414)


    The pg_search extension for Postgres uses a Log-Structured Merge (LSM) tree for
    faster write throughput, but this broke Postgres'' physical replication due to
    its Write-Ahead Log (WAL) shipping mechanism. The key to fixing this was making
    sure of atomic logging of operations, addressing the issue that Postgres locks
    aren''t replayed on replica servers, and implementing a Copy-on-Write strategy
    for multi-node operations.


    [**The 60-Second Wait: How I Spent Months Solving the Ruby''s Most Annoying Gem
    Installation Problem (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmensfeld.pl%2F2025%2F07%2Fsolving-ruby-rdkafka-installation-problem%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/0100019831dfc1eb-bd39c1dd-417a-49bb-9b31-604f15c01279-000000/k-wWM-v-Y56LaIXod86vZhFMgy_Xbw_1-jIm8R6jUOg=414)


    A Ruby developer spent months solving a notorious slow installation problem with
    the rdkafka gem, which took 60-90 seconds to compile from source during each installation.
    The solution involved creating precompiled native extensions with static linking
    to bundle all dependencies (OpenSSL, SASL, Kerberos, and compression libraries)
    into self-contained binaries, removing the need for compilation. This reduced
    installation time from 60+ seconds to under 5 seconds.

    [**5 things I learned from 5 years at Vercel (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fleerob.com%2Fvercel%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/0100019831dfc1eb-bd39c1dd-417a-49bb-9b31-604f15c01279-000000/o4x90NRrO_RZaAUvoztBRH7pEEX-lKma_RDUT6Zgm-0=414)


    After five years at Vercel, Lee Robieson reflects on his growth from individual
    contributor to VP as the company scaled from 30 people and \$1M ARR to 650 people
    and over \$200M ARR. He learned to work intensely while setting clear boundaries,
    pushed teams to move faster through aggressive deadlines, scaled through strategic
    hiring and delegation, avoided "swooping and pooping" by staying involved in important
    decisions from the start, and was willing to change his mind and give up control
    as the organization matured.


    [**Work-Life Balance Slows Careers (E9 Engineer, ex-Meta) (12 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.pathtostaff.com%2Fp%2Fwork-life-balance-slows-careers-e9%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/0100019831dfc1eb-bd39c1dd-417a-49bb-9b31-604f15c01279-000000/d7EPuWK5JRgVGVfeC90AbaLAsAYidIy85laOC94qi5c=414)


    Philip Su was a Meta Distinguished Engineer. He says that achieving rapid career
    progression often requires sacrificing work-life balance and prioritizing hard
    work. For example, he would sleep at the office when young to push code faster.
    This is part of having grit, which often translates to working longer hours and
    being more focused than peers.


    [**Don''t bother parsing: Just use images for RAG (12 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.morphik.ai%2Fblog%2Fstop-parsing-docs%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/0100019831dfc1eb-bd39c1dd-417a-49bb-9b31-604f15c01279-000000/pAikrBTPqrQq6i-PC2srtJ_xYYcCCzUck_KZXzqEpb4=414)


    A visual approach to document retrieval, using images of pages instead of traditional
    OCR and parsing methods, is a possible method to improve accuracy and preserve
    context for document parsing. This company divides document images into patches
    and uses vision transformers and language models to understand both textual and
    visual elements. By treating documents as visual objects, they are able to have
    higher accuracy in document understanding and search compared to traditional methods,
    especially for complex documents with charts, tables, and diagrams.

    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**What Went Wrong Inside These Recalled Power Banks? (10 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.lumafield.com%2Farticle%2Fwhat-went-wrong-inside-these-recalled-power-banks%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/0100019831dfc1eb-bd39c1dd-417a-49bb-9b31-604f15c01279-000000/61TaEj59nSn_tRCggiCuI4A16rmFuOgAPDQuUtp_xWI=414)


    Lumafield investigated the recent recall of over one million Anker PowerCore 10000
    power banks using industrial CT scanning. It identified variations in battery
    cell suppliers and internal assembly, specifically noting differences in tab bus
    bar connections between recalled and non-recalled devices, suggesting potential
    short-circuiting risks in the former. The updated Anker PowerCore 10000 model
    replaces the multiple cylindrical cells with a single pouch cell and simplified
    assembly.


    [**eslint-config-prettier Compromised: How npm Package with 30 Million Downloads
    Spread Malware (11 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fsafedep.io%2Feslint-config-prettier-major-npm-supply-chain-hack%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/0100019831dfc1eb-bd39c1dd-417a-49bb-9b31-604f15c01279-000000/tjyujd7VoEH4-rHdR4qIYu74n5Zhx9mjKBeKzrtyF1Q=414)


    A supply chain attack compromised the npm account of a maintainer, leading to
    the distribution of malware through popular packages like eslint-config-prettier.
    SafeDep detected the malicious packages using automated scanning that identified
    suspicious code, including a PE32+ executable and a command injection in the installation
    script. The malware, identified as Scavenger, primarily targets Windows systems,
    aiming to harvest files and credentials.


    [**How I found a bypass in Google''s big anti-adblock update (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Flinks.tldrnewsletter.com%2Fhj0YET/1/0100019831dfc1eb-bd39c1dd-417a-49bb-9b31-604f15c01279-000000/pbuePdcndvr50kDS8WEaKGnUXciQFrQiN_lMDUUXc-4=414)


    This dev discovered a bug in Google Chrome that allowed MV3 extensions to bypass
    the intended restrictions on `webRequestBlocking`, a feature necessary for adblockers
    that Google was phasing out. The bug exploited a loophole in how Chrome handled
    WebView IDs within the `webRequest` API, allowing extensions to spoof permissions
    and reinstate the blocking functionality.

    as the technology matures.

    A "vibe coding" experiment using Replit''s AI agent resulted in the agent repeatedly
    lying, overwriting code, and ultimately deleting the production database inadvertently.
