    # TLDR Web Dev 2025-07-23


    # **Articles & Tutorials**


    [**Don''t animate height! (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.granola.ai%2Fblog%2Fdont-animate-height%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/v-eyEj7JFJhWtxp7vdq_wwngzhCMZyM140grJ3pKzb0=415)


    A performance issue in the Granola note-taking app was caused by animating the
    `height` property in a CSS audio visualizer. Animating `height` triggers expensive
    layout, paint, and composite steps in the browser''s rendering pipeline. To fix
    this, Granola replaced the `height` animation with a `transform` animation using
    two rectangles, achieving the visual effect of stretching without the performance
    hit.


    [**The world''s longest React hooks migration (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fcraft.faire.com%2Fthe-worlds-longest-react-hooks-migration-8f357cdcdbe9%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/qp5RJXs_bTSeasAuSj1-vrj0DxABYakVupEg6p8oiA4=415)


    Faire completed a massive migration from React class components and MobX to functional
    components and hooks in 2025, despite hooks being released in 2019. The company
    delayed the migration after switching to MobX in 2018, but by 2022, its codebase
    had grown 5x larger while the team only doubled, creating maintainability issues
    with bloated "kitchen-sink" classes and performance problems from large bundle
    sizes and poor caching.


    [**I''m more proud of these 128 kilobytes than anything I''ve built since (8 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fmedium.com%2F@mikehall314%2Fim-more-proud-of-these-128-kilobytes-than-anything-i-ve-built-since-53706cfbdc18%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/Di-_7ZLJopi3ASzsKEwnP0bhOxJB7RAAL0Ghal9edQA=415)


    This dev had to build a web application for users in Africa with poor internet
    infrastructure, mostly using feature phones with 240px screens and EDGE connections.
    They established strict constraints, including a 128KB total page budget, compatibility
    with Opera Mini browser, and responsive design from feature phones to 4K displays.
    Despite the extreme limitations, these tight constraints led to better solutions:
    they used system fonts instead of web fonts, built a minimal custom library called
    "Whizz" instead of heavy frameworks, and created an efficient AJAX-based navigation
    system that only loaded new page content rather than full page reloads.


    # **Opinions & Advice**


    [**Why I''m Writing Pure HTML & CSS in 2025 (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fjoeldare.com%2Fwhy-im-writing-pure-html-and-css-in-2025%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/grdcsCNN3EJkKDh7BjLzQAgiYqWXSaUtQxy-QOprQ9Q=415)


    Using pure HTML and CSS in 2025 creates web pages that load instantly, deploy
    easily, and never need security updates, while modern websites have become bloated
    with an average size of 2.65MB. Pure HTML pages have advantages, including evergreen
    compatibility (HTML from 1991 still works today), better accessibility and SEO
    through semantic tags, free hosting options, and no complex build processes or
    dependency management.


    [**Reflections on Palantir (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fnabeelqu.substack.com%2Fp%2Freflections-on-palantir%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/nEGs0gU3zn90FIQkQ8Rwf5cBqFSVZb-heANcAIUt8KI=415)


    Nabeel Qureshi''s eight-year tenure at Palantir (2015-2023) was at the same time
    the company transformed from being a relatively smaller company to joining the
    S&P 500 with a nearly $100 billion market cap. Palantir has a unique culture of
    intellectual intensity inherited from the PayPal founders, with a forward-deployed
    engineer model where engineers work directly at customer sites in difficult industries.
    This approach let the company evolve from what appeared to be a consulting firm
    into a genuine software product company.


    # **Launches & Tools**


    [**Qwen3-Coder: Agentic Coding in the World (5 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fqwenlm.github.io%2Fblog%2Fqwen3-coder%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/8GjskAOcr1arKX_n9XDKGud21EBcfLcV3rfpeVN7B6I=415)


    The Qwen Team has announced Qwen3-Coder, their most advanced agentic coding model
    to date. It features a 480B-parameter Mixture-of-Experts model with 35B active
    parameters and extended context length. The model has state-of-the-art performance
    in Agentic Coding, Browser-Use, and Tool-Use, on par with Claude Sonnet 4. Qwen
    Code, a command-line tool adapted from Gemini Code, has also been released.


    [**DaisyUI (Website)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fdaisyui.com%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/PwCk5OB3OVgEKZdT1AhrVuMpxsJEdRmyv74VLSMFWTo=415)


    DaisyUI is a Tailwind CSS plugin that provides pre-built, customizable component
    class names. It reduces the amount of code needed by offering semantic class names,
    resulting in cleaner HTML and smaller file sizes.


    [**Any LLM (GitHub Repo)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fmozilla-ai%2Fany-llm%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/9XtwStLKg5U6zY61VPGn41AHUn5I3xPl7tbbU0GORLo=415)


    Any LLM is a Python library that provides a unified interface for interacting
    with various LLM providers like Mistral and OpenAI. It makes model switching easier
    and has developer-friendly features like type hints and actionable error messages.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**More than you wanted to know about how Game Boy cartridges work (89 minute
    read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fabc.decontextualize.com%2Fmore-than-you-wanted-to-know%2F%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/2MmvCMjJh1AUQaN9I8cBZ4WSj4gz5O5Urw2p32wGZNQ=415)


    This article goes through the inner workings of Game Boy cartridges, covering
    their architecture, memory management, and how they interact with the Game Boy
    system. It explains fundamental components like ROM, RAM, and Memory Bank Controllers
    (MBCs). It also explains how the Game Boy addresses memory and how MBCs enable
    larger ROM sizes and additional functionalities.


    [**Fun with Gzip Bombs and Email Clients (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.grepular.com%2FFun_with_Gzip_Bombs_and_Email_Clients%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/TeRKVEwbQKhhAcHJGyAC8lGTt0fMTIuKSgQkde1Cm2g=415)


    Email clients are vulnerable to Gzip bombs, which are small compressed files that
    expand to a massive size when decompressed. This dev created a 10MB Gzip file
    that expands to 10GB and tested how various email clients handle it when embedded
    as an image in an email. Some clients like Firefox, Thunderbird, and Gmail''s
    proxies bailed out early, while others like Fastmail webmail''s proxies downloaded
    a partial amount before giving up. iOS Mail crashed.

    [**TODOs aren''t for doing (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fsophiebits.com%2F2025%2F07%2F21%2Ftodos-arent-for-doing%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/wcQPsPcjMdL1RC3SUEYcdTmGtUISHe-ZaDwC4GSMoZI=415)


    TODO comments in code are valuable not necessarily as tasks to be completed, but
    as a way to capture context, edge cases, and potential improvements for future
    developers.


    [**I''ve launched 37 products in 5 years and not doing that again (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.indiehackers.com%2Fpost%2Five-launched-37-products-in-5-years-and-not-doing-that-again-0b66e6e8b3%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/_A53hQjGOpdNaYUBJTp0DcArzIw-dpZZLCq1YMxOpJM=415)


    Focusing on improving a single project with slow, steady growth is more effective
    than constantly launching new ones in the hopes of achieving virality.


    [**I Watched Gemini CLI Hallucinate and Delete My Files (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fanuraag2601.github.io%2Fgemini_cli_disaster.html%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/DKR8pJ_Dzud-am0WiBwJSc7tpPIn7DHpm3eXGHmPzLg=415)


    A dev experimenting with the Gemini CLI experienced catastrophic data loss when
    the AI hallucinated successful file operations, misinterpreted error messages
    from failed commands, and deleted their files by repeatedly overwriting them while
    attempting to move them to a non-existent directory.


    [**The Perils of an .xyz Domain (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.spotvirtual.com%2Fblog%2Fthe-perils-of-an-xyz-domain%3Futm_source=tldrwebdev/1/01000198370e77dc-557cd230-7572-4a11-b8a4-5b5dd455c6b2-000000/ILYdFTL6ZELZR8E5j_3Ec-hr-BexWXO4RbksdIPN9Ao=415)


    Spot switched from the spot.xyz domain to spotvirtual.com to improve email and
    SMS deliverability, user perception, firewall accessibility, and social media
    sharing after experiencing issues with the .xyz domain being associated with spam
    and malicious content.'

    # TLDR Marketing 2025-07-25


    # **News & Trends**


    [**PR Trends: The Shifts You Can''t Ignore in 2025 (9 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.buzzstream.com%2Fblog%2Fpr-trends%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/01000198414df1b8-4124cbc1-b208-4f6e-aec1-b428be597199-000000/gk2Z36pHby17RwgBj4OWzgK1bQCz28MF8iiBtoIDPlY=415)


    LinkedIn has overtaken X as the top social platform for journalists in 2025, making
    it the most effective place for PR professionals to build relationships. Despite
    some rise in DM-based outreach, 96% of journalists still prefer to receive pitches
    via email. Journalists now value exclusives more than original research and prioritize
    access to credible sources over story ideas or data. Irrelevant pitches are increasing,
    with 47% of journalists saying they seldom receive relevant outreach, and response
    rates continue to decline as pitch volumes rise. With ongoing layoffs and more
    journalists moving to independent platforms like Substack, PR professionals must
    focus on relevance, personalization, and consistency to cut through the noise.


    [**The Art & Science of Video Storytelling (8 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fbusiness.linkedin.com%2Fcontent%2Fdam%2Fbusiness%2Fmarketing-solutions%2Fglobal%2Fen_US%2Fsite%2Fpdf%2Fwp%2F2025%2Fthe-art-and-science-of-video.pdf%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/01000198414df1b8-4124cbc1-b208-4f6e-aec1-b428be597199-000000/Wz6LA3xuYhzzjYAIglNdk9wtggN0erLZOlYMQMkM3SA=415)


    Video is now the primary format for B2B marketing. LinkedIn video viewership rose
    36% in 2024, and video posts are shared 203% more than other content types. 5
    key creative principles drive success: Cultural Coding, Human Touch, Expert Takes,
    Attention Hacking, and Inspiring Imagination. Videos with expert speakers increase
    dwell time by 31%, human-centered content boosts engagement by 18%, and authentic,
    emotive videos see up to 84% higher engagement.


    [**Pew Research: Google users are less likely to click on links when an AI summary
    appears in the results (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.pewresearch.org%2Fshort-reads%2F2025%2F07%2F22%2Fgoogle-users-are-less-likely-to-click-on-links-when-an-ai-summary-appears-in-the-results%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/01000198414df1b8-4124cbc1-b208-4f6e-aec1-b428be597199-000000/tOwUsbuUIJGPrJ4u_9yuFQzOo25h86Vkyo6B0O5GQjU=415)


    Users are less likely to click on links when Google shows an AI-generated summary,
    with only 8% clicking on a search result compared to 15% when no summary appears.
    Just 1% of visits to AI summary pages result in users clicking links within the
    summary itself. About 26% of users end their browsing after seeing a summary,
    compared to 16% for pages without one. Longer and question-based searches are
    more likely to trigger an AI summary, with 60% of question-word searches and 53%
    of 10-word-or-longer searches producing one.


    # **Strategies & Tactics**


    [**The Case for Zero-Click Content in a Zero-Trust Ecosystem (4 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fsparktoro.com%2Fblog%2Fthe-case-for-zero-click-content-in-a-zero-trust-ecosystem%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/01000198414df1b8-4124cbc1-b208-4f6e-aec1-b428be597199-000000/aQIMel5gnDB3tCW-ZnPojIKUn9_WFJI41QTvkDRwaiQ=415)


    Platforms now suppress outbound links, hide referral data, and hoard traffic.
    This makes traditional click-based marketing unreliable. Instead of chasing clicks,
    zero-click content delivers standalone value directly in-platform. Links aren''t
    off-limits but should be used sparingly, supported by consistent value-driven
    content. Success can be measured through branded search lift, audience growth,
    and conversions like booked demos.


    [**The Power of Identity: Building Lifelong Customers (10 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.socialmediaexaminer.com%2Fthe-power-of-identify-building-lifelong-customers%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/01000198414df1b8-4124cbc1-b208-4f6e-aec1-b428be597199-000000/ud8Fq8640gK7yi1XsJe3UiTeiex3g9ZIkZdVZKTBAe4=415)


    The strongest loyalty comes from brands that reflect how customers define themselves
    and what they care about most. Identity marketing involves researching how customers
    talk about their struggles and aspirations, validating those themes through real-world
    feedback, and naming identity groups with deeper meaning rather than surface-level
    slogans. When customers feel that a brand helps express who they are and what
    they believe in, they become voluntary ambassadors who spread the message out
    of pride and alignment, not obligation.


    [**Passionate employee > Faceless logo (1 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Fposts%2Fthatjillian_for-the-love-of-all-that-is-holy-brands-activity-7354189967004188672-us2S%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/01000198414df1b8-4124cbc1-b208-4f6e-aec1-b428be597199-000000/P3tpWHKf5nZJAFNDqUl9IpPCg-D6ffvF4L-1c6IXjXc=415)


    Instead of prioritizing your company LinkedIn page, identify a charismatic employee
    to serve as your public voice. People trust individuals far more than brand logos,
    and employee-led content builds a stronger audience connection. Ideal candidates
    often have public speaking experience, creative backgrounds, or represent underrepresented
    groups. Support them with a ghostwriter, feature them on your company page, put
    them on stages, and compensate them accordingly.


    # **Resources & Tools**


    [**ChatGPT uses Google SERP Snippets for its Answers (6 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.aleydasolis.com%2Fen%2Fai-search%2Fchatgpt-uses-google-serp-snippets-for-answers%2F%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/01000198414df1b8-4124cbc1-b208-4f6e-aec1-b428be597199-000000/pubNrmUeCQrEwzbyGLEnWxbLDNRgl0JL2f05l6xCANI=415)


    A test confirmed that ChatGPT relies on Google Search result snippets for its
    answers. A newly published webpage, not submitted to search engines, couldn''t
    be located by ChatGPT even with web search enabled. Gemini, in contrast, fetched
    the live content directly. Once the page was indexed in Google but not yet visible
    in search results, ChatGPT still failed to access it. Only after the page appeared
    in Google SERPs did ChatGPT provide a partial response, clearly drawn from the
    Google snippet rather than the actual page. This shows ChatGPT''s dependence on
    Google''s indexed summaries, not direct page access.


    [**When using AI bots turns customers away (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fapp.sciencesays.com%2Fp%2Fwhen-using-ai-bots-turns-customers-away%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/01000198414df1b8-4124cbc1-b208-4f6e-aec1-b428be597199-000000/JdNy3Ws0pwtFssaxVrsUmghpWI8zZU7OONOriuQ4Gms=415)


    Customers are 23.7% less likely to continue using a service when it is provided
    by AI instead of a human if warmth is important. The drop in preference is stronger
    when the service is associated with fun or pleasure, with a 29.8% decrease in
    usage intention, compared to 17.5% when the focus is on efficiency. AI is perceived
    as 19.5% less warm than human staff, but using informal language helps reduce
    this effect. Companies like Henn na Hotel and McDonald''s abandoned full AI setups
    due to poor customer response, while hybrid models like Starbucks'' app chatbot
    have been more successful.


    # **Miscellaneous**


    [**Slack''s acquisition spree: 6 purchases in 6 years to compete with Microsoft
    and Google (3 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fstrategybreakdowns.com%2Fp%2Fslackquisitions%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/01000198414df1b8-4124cbc1-b208-4f6e-aec1-b428be597199-000000/nckpF3w3AJ5siNpVIQQd_Yfn-BvSGdBIhAgA_JD28GM=415)


    Slack used a buy-over-build strategy to quickly match the features of Microsoft
    and Google by acquiring six companies between 2014 and 2020. These acquisitions
    helped it add tools like screen sharing, document collaboration, and email integration,
    allowing it to scale to 12 million daily active users by the end of 2020. Its
    2018 deal with Atlassian eliminated competitors HipChat and Stride and led to
    over 11 joint integrations. By acquiring technologies that reduced context-switching,
    Slack positioned itself as a unified work hub and ultimately attracted Salesforce,
    which acquired it in 2020.


    [**What explains Google''s record quarterly search revenue while clicks decline
    & sitetraffic drops? (2 minute read)**](https://tracking.tldrnewsletter.com/CL0/https:%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Fposts%2Fjimlecinski_clicks-sitetraffic-aioverviews-activity-7354152095022764033-6UCv%3Futm_source=tldrmarketing/1/01000198414df1b8-4124cbc1-b208-4f6e-aec1-b428be597199-000000/yGymrehj-YSsVh2LrShePXWeqf8iCktdq2ekRmLkdR0=415)


    The introduction of AI Overviews has changed the search funnel by addressing early
    research queries without requiring user clicks. As a result, fewer users proceed
    to external sites, but those who do are more likely to convert and are being monetized
    at higher rates, with CPCs rising nearly 13%. This model has enabled Google to
    grow search revenue significantly despite reduced traffic to third-party websites.

        # Answer instruction

> You are an expert summarizer agent. You will be given an input context of newsletters to be summarized, Summarize only the key finding and only present deep dive if the user request so.

IMPORTANT: Must include link to the original newsletter and article following below guideline

## How to format newsletters

- If the user questions is about giving overview of newsletters from a specific date or a date range ALWAYS USE THIS FORMAT like the example below: DO NOT USE THIS ANSWER FORMAT IF THE USER QUESTION REQUIRE DEEPER ANALYSIS
  - Example: question: Ben Lorica newsletters over the past week

```md
Here are the Ben Lorica newsletters from the past week:

**1. Quick Wins for your AI eval strategy**
_Date:_ July 15, 2025
_Key Finding:_ This newsletter offers a comprehensive guide to AI evaluation strategies, emphasizing the importance of systematically assessing AI-generated outputs for quality, reliability, and business impact. It outlines a roadmap covering foundational principles, operational excellence, and frontier techniques to effectively deploy AI. Key takeaways include establishing evaluation as a first-class engineering discipline, layering multiple evaluation methods, prioritizing reliability over peak performance, implementing dual-track evaluation, building production-to-development feedback loops, integrating human oversight, designing cost-aware practices, evaluating agent workflows holistically, continuously improving evaluation systems, connecting metrics to business outcomes, and documenting practices for governance.
_Read more of the article: [Quick Wins for your AI eval strategy](https://substack.com/app-link/post?publication_id=20983&post_id=167485385&utm_source=post-email-title&utm_campaign=email-post-title&isFreemail=true&r=5s83oz&token=eyJ1c2VyX2lkIjozNDk3MzgxNjMsInBvc3RfaWQiOjE2NzQ4NTM4NSwiaWF0IjoxNzUyNTg4NTcwLCJleHAiOjE3NTUxODA1NzAsImlzcyI6InB1Yi0yMDk4MyIsInN1YiI6InBvc3QtcmVhY3Rpb24ifQ.ZFbDNwQooEmRIoTdObq9ukLgBQX_0qsIEHCFtchn_zQ)_
_Read more of the newsletter: [Ben Lorica - 2025/07/15](https://polskitran.github.io/Sumitup-quartz-dev/2025-07-15/ben-lorica-2025-07-15)_

**2. Superposition Meets Production—A Guide for AI Engineers**
_Date:_ July 17, 2025
_Key Finding:_ This newsletter delves into the current landscape and future prospects of quantum computing for AI applications, featuring insights from DeepMind veteran Jennifer Prendki. It highlights that while universal quantum computers are still some years away, specific quantum applications for machine learning are emerging today, particularly in recommendation systems, financial applications (e.g., fraud detection), and pharmaceuticals. A significant challenge is the lack of a mature "QMLOps" software layer, as the quantum computing stack is fragmented and primitive compared to classical ML infrastructure. The "no-cloning theorem" fundamentally alters data operations in quantum environments, requiring a shift to on-demand regeneration of quantum states rather than traditional backups or reproducibility. The newsletter also discusses how quantum computing enables new paradigms like Topological Data Analysis and emphasizes the need for "bridge talent" in engineering rather than deep quantum physics expertise for practitioners.
_Read more of the article: [Superposition Meets Production—A Guide for AI Engineers](https://substack.substack.com/app-link/post?publication_id=20983&post_id=167287075&utm_source=post-email-title&utm_campaign=email-post-title&isFreemail=true&r=5s83oz&token=eyJ1c2VyX2lkIjozNDk3MzgxNjMsInBvc3RfaWQiOjE2NzI4NzA3NSwiaWF0IjoxNzUyNzYxNjAwLCJleHAiOjE3NTUzNTM2MDAsImlzcyI6InB1Yi0yMDk4MyIsInN1YiI6InBvc3QtcmVhY3Rpb24ifQ.Ww9oOjjJfJeXHNyFZ8TEN2d7rOXvzD4l0xYbdDwJHCw)_
_Read more of the newsletter: [Ben Lorica - 2025/07/17](https://polskitran.github.io/Sumitup-quartz-dev/2025-07-17/ben-lorica-2025-07-17)_
```

```
## Newsletter link format - Every answer should be accompany with the link to the original newsletters like below:

- `Read more of the newsletters` link will always be in the form of `[{newsletter-name}-{YYYY-MM-DD}](https://polskitran.github.io/Sumitup-quartz-dev/{YYYY-MM-DD}/{newsletter-name}-{YYYY-MM-DD})`. Example: A link for newsletter from Ben Lorica on 2025-07-10 will be `[Ben Lorica - 2025/7/10](https://polskitran.github.io/Sumitup-quartz-dev/2025-07-10/ben-lorica-2025-07-10)`
- `Read more of the article` link should be included with each headline article.

Available {newsletter-name}: tldr, tldr-ai, tldr-data, tldr-web-dev, tldr-fintech, tldr-infosec, tldr-marketing, tldr-product, tldr-founders, tldr-devops, tldr-design, ben-lorica, last-week-in-ai, tech-brew, bytebytego, chinai-newsletter
```
